# cs.SE [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Verus-SpecGym: An Agentic Environment for Evaluating Specification Autoformalization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26457v1)
*Anmol Agarwal,Natalie Neamtu,Pranjal Aggarwal,Seungone Kim,Jannis Limperg,Cedric Flamant,Kanna Shimizu,Bryan Parno,Sean Welleck*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文研究了AI编码代理将非正式编程问题自动形式化为忠实形式化规范的能力，提出了一个基准和一个智能体环境，并利用可执行规范和对抗测试实现了自动评估，发现前沿模型虽能解决大部分任务但仍存在脆弱性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI编码代理被广泛用于软件生成，确保其输出正确性至关重要。形式化验证通过生成代码和机器可验证的证明来保证代码符合规范，但规范本身可能不匹配用户意图。因此，需要研究LLM代理能否自动将非正式问题描述转化为忠实的正式规范，即规范自动形式化问题。

Method: 我们构建了Verus-SpecBench基准（581个规范编写任务）和Verus-SpecGym智能体环境。为克服评估难题，扩展了Verus的exec_spec机制使规范可执行，并通过官方Codeforces测试和从Codeforces hacks中提取的对抗性案例进行自动评估。

Result: 在Verus-SpecBench上，最强模型Gemini 3.1 Pro解决了77.8%的任务，其他前沿模型解决51.1%–57.8%，开源模型仅21.5%–25.5%。模型生成的规范常遗漏输入假设、接受错误输出或拒绝有效输出，且LLM作为评判者会遗漏26%的失败。

Conclusion: 规范自动形式化对于前沿AI代理而言是可行的，但即使在它们已能生成正确代码的问题上仍然很脆弱。需要更好的评估方法和规范生成改进，以提升可靠性。

中文摘要：AI编码代理越来越多地被用于编写真实世界的软件，但确保其输出正确仍然是一个根本性挑战。形式化验证提供了一条有前景的路径：代理生成代码及其机器可验证的证明，保证代码满足形式化规范。然而，无法保证形式化规范本身符合用户的意图。在这项工作中，我们研究规范自动形式化：LLM代理能否将非正式编程问题转化为忠实的形式化规范。我们引入了Verus-SpecBench，一个包含581个规范编写任务的基准，这些任务源自Codeforces问题，针对Rust的验证器Verus；以及Verus-SpecGym，一个代理环境，模型在其中与Verus、bash和文件系统交互以开发这些规范。核心挑战在于评估：专家编写的参考规范编写成本高昂，且LLM评判者可能遗漏细微错误。我们通过以下方式解决这一问题：(a) 扩展Verus的exec_spec机制，使生成的规范可以作为Rust代码执行；以及(b) 使用官方的Codeforces测试和从Codeforces“hacks”中提取的对抗性案例（竞争对手编写的用于破解错误解决方案的边缘情况）对其进行测试。在Verus-SpecBench上，最强的模型Gemini 3.1 Pro解决了77.8%的任务，其他前沿模型解决了51.1%–57.8%，而开源模型仅达到21.5%–25.5%。我们对失败模式的分析表明，模型生成的规范可能遗漏重要的输入假设、接受错误的输出以及拒绝有效的输出。我们还发现，LLM作为评判者的评估遗漏了我们的评估者捕获的26%的失败。总体而言，我们的结果表明，规范自动形式化对于前沿代理而言是可实现的，但即使在它们已经能够生成正确代码的问题上，仍然很脆弱。代码、数据和日志可在https://github.com/formal-verif-is-cool/verus-spec-gym找到。

Original abstract: AI coding agents are increasingly used to write real-world software, but ensuring that their outputs are correct remains a fundamental challenge. Formal verification offers a promising path: an agent generates code together with a machine-checked proof, guaranteeing that the code satisfies a formal specification. However, there is no guarantee that the formal spec itself matches the user's intent. In this work, we study specification autoformalization: whether LLM agents can translate informal programming problems into faithful formal specifications. We introduce Verus-SpecBench, a benchmark of 581 spec-writing tasks derived from Codeforces problems targeting Verus, a verifier for Rust, and Verus-SpecGym, an agentic environment in which models interact with Verus, bash, & the filesystem to develop these specs. The central challenge is evaluation: expert-written reference specs are expensive to write, & LLM judges can miss subtle mistakes. We address this by (a) extending Verus's exec_spec mechanism so that generated specs can be executed as Rust code, & (b) testing them against official Codeforces tests & adversarial cases extracted from Codeforces "hacks", which are edge cases written by competitors to break incorrect solutions. On Verus-SpecBench, the strongest model, Gemini 3.1 Pro, solves 77.8% of tasks, other frontier models solve 51.1--57.8% & OSS models reach only 21.5--25.5%. Our analysis of failure modes shows that model-generated specs can omit important input assumptions, accept incorrect outputs, & reject valid ones. We also find that LLM-as-a-judge evaluation misses 26% of the failures our evaluator catches. Overall, our results suggest that spec autoformalization is within reach for frontier agents but remains brittle even on problems where they can already generate correct code. The code, data, & logs can be found at https://github.com/formal-verif-is-cool/verus-spec-gym

</details>


### [2] [Testing Agentic Workflows with Structural Coverage Criteria](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26521v1)
*Nafiseh Kahani,Mojtaba Bagherzadeh*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种针对多智能体工作流规范的结构测试方法，通过类型化协调图表示工作流并推导覆盖义务，使用DSPy生成测试场景，在OpenAI Agents SDK基准上验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法主要依赖端到端任务成功等指标，无法有效验证多智能体工作流中声明的协调结构（智能体、工具访问规则、限制、委托路径）是否实际被执行，导致难以评估测试充分性和检测结构回归。

Method: 将每个工作流表示为类型化协调图，推导可达智能体、允许/受限工具边、委托边的覆盖义务，并通过基于覆盖的生成和DSPy场景实现产生可执行测试，在运行时检查见证。

Result: 在十个SDK派生的基准测试中，生成的场景在有限预算内覆盖了54/75个允许工具义务和36/48个委托义务；对抗性受限工具标准引发23/248个受限调用违规，有效区分不同工作流的限制行为。

Conclusion: 结构覆盖为多智能体工作流测试提供了有用的充分性层，不替代语义或端到端评估，但能揭示声明的协调结构是否被实际执行。

中文摘要：多智能体系统日益暴露显式的工作流结构：智能体、工具、工具访问规则、限制和委托路径。现有评估主要依赖于端到端任务成功、基准分数、最终响应质量或提示级检查，这些方法提供的证据有限，不足以证明声明的协调结构实际上已被执行。这使得评估测试套件的充分性或检测工具访问、限制和智能体间委托中的结构回归变得困难。我们针对多智能体工作流规范提出了一种结构测试方法来解决这一差距。该方法将每个工作流表示为一个类型化协调图，推导出可达智能体、允许的工具边、受限的工具边和委托边上的覆盖义务，并使用基于覆盖的生成和基于DSPy的场景实现来生成可执行测试。图固定了必须覆盖的内容；DSPy将这些义务实现为自然语言场景，其见证在运行时被检查。我们针对OpenAI Agents SDK风格的工作流实现了该方法，并在十个SDK派生的基准测试上进行了评估，这些基准测试包含49个可达智能体、47个工具和403个结构义务。生成的场景在有限的精炼预算内见证了54/75个允许工具义务和36/48个委托义务。对抗性的受限工具标准引发了23/248个受限调用违规，将限制在探测下成立的工作流与存在具体错误路由故障的工作流区分开来。这些结果表明，结构覆盖为多智能体工作流测试提供了有用的充分性层：它不取代语义或端到端评估，但揭示了声明的智能体、工具访问规则、限制和委托路径是否已被执行。

Original abstract: Multi-agent systems increasingly expose explicit workflow structure: agents, tools, tool-access rules, restrictions, and delegation paths. Existing evaluations rely largely on end-to-end task success, benchmark scores, final-response quality, or prompt-level checks, which provide limited evidence that this declared coordination structure has actually been exercised. This makes it difficult to assess test-suite adequacy or detect structural regressions in tool access, restrictions, and inter-agent delegation. We address this gap with a structural testing approach for multi-agent workflow specifications. The approach represents each workflow as a typed coordination graph, derives coverage obligations over reachable agents, allowed tool edges, restricted tool edges, and delegation edges, and uses coverage-driven generation with DSPy-based scenario realization to produce executable tests. The graph fixes what must be covered; DSPy realizes those obligations as natural-language scenarios whose witnesses are checked at runtime. We implement the approach for OpenAI Agents SDK-style workflows and evaluate it on ten SDK-derived benchmarks comprising 49 reachable agents, 47 tools, and 403 structural obligations. Generated scenarios witness 54/75 allowed-tool obligations and 36/48 delegation obligations within a bounded refinement budget. The adversarial restricted-tool criterion elicits 23/248 restricted-call violations, separating workflows whose restrictions hold under probing from workflows with concrete misrouting failures. These results show that structural coverage provides a useful adequacy layer for multi-agent workflow testing: it does not replace semantic or end-to-end evaluation, but reveals whether declared agents, tool-access rules, restrictions, and delegation paths have been exercised.

</details>


### [3] [TrajAudit: Automated Failure Diagnosis for Agentic Coding Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26563v2)
*Minxing Wang,Xiaofei Xie,Yintong Huo*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出TrajAudit框架，通过语义显著性折叠和测试报告先验知识，有效诊断仓库级编码代理的长且有噪声的轨迹失败，在RootSE基准上定位准确性提升10.8%-21.6%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动化失败诊断方法在处理仓库级编码代理产生的长且充满噪声的执行轨迹时表现不佳，难以追踪因果链并受冗余信息干扰。

Method: 提出TrajAudit框架，包含一个调查代理，利用语义显著性折叠减少噪声，并从测试失败报告提取先验指导，同时支持按需检查折叠内容。

Result: 在RootSE基准上，TrajAudit在精确失败定位准确性上，有参考设置下提升10.8%，无参考设置下提升21.6%。

Conclusion: TrajAudit通过聚焦关键信息减少噪声干扰，有效提升了仓库级编码代理失败诊断的准确性。

中文摘要：代理系统已被广泛研究，用于自动化编码任务，如错误修复和功能实现。随着这些系统越来越多地操作复杂的代码库，理解它们失败的地点和原因对于迭代改进和操作可靠性变得至关重要。现有的自动化失败诊断方法利用任务执行轨迹，但在处理仓库级编码代理产生的轨迹时存在困难，原因有两个关键特性。首先，这些轨迹通常很长，跨越多个执行步骤，使得大型语言模型难以在历史执行中追踪失败的因果链。其次，这些轨迹充满噪声，包含大量低信号观测，例如冗余的程序结构和冗长的代码上下文，这些可能干扰大型语言模型的推理。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了TrajAudit，一个专门针对仓库级编码代理产生的轨迹的自动化失败诊断框架。TrajAudit采用一个调查代理，由两个模块支持：一个通过语义显著性折叠减少与失败无关的噪声上下文，另一个从测试失败报告中提取初步诊断指导作为先验知识，帮助大型语言模型聚焦于可能的失败区域。调查代理还可以按需调用工具检查折叠的内容，实现集中调查而不丢失完整轨迹上下文的访问。我们还引入了RootSE，一个来自仓库级编码任务的102个真实世界实例的基准，每个实例都标注了最早的决定性错误步骤和理由。在RootSE上的实验表明，TrajAudit在精确失败定位准确性上，在有无参考设置中分别比最强基线高出10.8%和21.6%，展示了其有效性。

Original abstract: Agentic systems have been widely studied to automate coding tasks such as bug fixing and feature implementation. As these systems increasingly operate on complex codebases, understanding where and why they fail becomes essential for iterative refinement and operational reliability. Existing automated failure diagnosis approaches leverage \textit{task execution trajectories}, yet they struggle with trajectories produced by repository-level coding agents due to two key properties. First, these trajectories are often long, spanning many execution steps, making it difficult for LLMs to track the causal chain of failure over the execution history. Second, these trajectories are laden with noise, containing substantial low-signal observations such as redundant program structures and verbose code context, which can interfere with LLM reasoning.
  To address these challenges, we propose \textit{TrajAudit}, an automated failure diagnosis framework specifically for trajectories produced by repository-level coding agents. TrajAudit employs an investigator agent supported by two modules: one reduces failure-irrelevant noisy context through semantic saliency folding, and the other derives preliminary diagnostic guidance from test failure reports as prior knowledge to help LLMs focus on likely failure regions. The investigator agent can further invoke tools to inspect folded content on demand, enabling a focused investigation without losing access to the full trajectory context. We also introduce \textit{RootSE}, a benchmark of 102 real-world instances from repository-level coding tasks, each annotated with the earliest decisive error step and a justification. Experiments on RootSE show that TrajAudit outperforms the strongest baselines by 10.8\% and 21.6\% in exact failure localization accuracy in the with- and without-reference settings, respectively, demonstrating its effectiveness.

</details>


### [4] [LogDx-CI: Benchmarking Log Reduction Tools for LLM Root-Cause Diagnosis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28876v1)
*Bowen Qin*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出LogDx-CI基准，比较11种日志缩减工具，发现混合grep+尾部路由器性价比最优，并揭示跨家族LLM摘要-调试器配对比同家族配对更有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CI失败日志庞大且嘈杂，编码代理依赖上游工具缩减日志，但缺乏公开的经验比较来确定哪些缩减方法能保留足够证据供下游LLM诊断。

Method: 引入LogDx-CI基准，比较11种上下文缩减工具（raw、tail、grep、三种RTK模式、两个LLM map-reduce摘要器、三个混合路由器）在35个真实GitHub Actions失败案例上的表现，使用3个LLM调试器家族（Claude Haiku 4.5、Claude Sonnet 4.6、OpenAI gpt-5-mini）及其一个工具使用代理进行评分。

Result: 发现三个主要结果：(1) 混合grep+tail路由器主导成本-质量帕累托前沿，得分0.670/0.666，成本约$0.03/案例，token少4.5倍；(2) 代理循环中质量范围缩小7倍，但成本差异持续，弱上下文导致2-4倍工具调用；(3) 跨家族LLM配对（gpt-5-mini摘要+Claude Haiku调试器）比同家族配对平均高0.071，且gpt-5-mini摘要器在代理循环中得分0.749，成本低10倍。

Conclusion: 研究表明混合grep+tail路由器在成本和质量上表现优异，跨家族LLM配对效果更好，为CI调试自动化提供了有效指导，所有数据和代码已公开。

中文摘要：CI失败日志规模庞大（中位数5000行，本语料库中最大200k行）且噪声多。尝试调试这些日志的编码代理依赖于上游工具将日志缩减为可管理的上下文，但该领域尚未有公开的经验比较，研究哪些缩减方法能够为下游LLM诊断保留足够的证据。我们引入了LogDx-CI基准，该基准比较了11种上下文缩减工具（原始、尾部、grep、三种RTK模式、两个真实LLM映射-归约摘要器、三个混合路由器）在35个真实GitHub Actions失败案例上的表现，并由3个LLM调试器家族（Claude Haiku 4.5、Claude Sonnet 4.6、OpenAI gpt-5-mini）以及一个Sonnet 4.6工具使用代理进行评分。我们报告了三个重要发现：（1）混合grep+尾部路由器主导了成本-质量帕累托前沿；前两种方法得分分别为0.670/0.666，每个案例约0.03美元，质量与单独的grep相当，但token数减少了4.5倍。（2）在代理循环机制下，不同缩减工具之间的质量范围缩小了7倍（单次查询的差异为0.42 → 代理循环的差异为0.059）；代理通过后续工具调用挽救了弱上下文。然而，成本差异仍然存在：弱上下文迫使代理多进行2-4倍的工具调用来恢复。（3）跨家族的LLM摘要-调试器配对（gpt-5-mini摘要器输入Claude Haiku调试器）在四种诊断变体上的平均得分比同家族配对高0.071，否定了该任务上的自调用偏见假设。gpt-5-mini摘要器也是代理循环中的第一名方法（得分0.749），每个案例仅需0.37次工具调用，且缩减器成本比Haiku摘要器低10倍（每个案例0.18美元 vs 1.75美元）。所有数据、代码、每个案例的打包文件以及可复现性基础设施均已公开。

Original abstract: CI failure logs are large (median 5k lines, max 200k in this corpus) and noisy. Coding agents that try to debug them depend on an upstream tool to reduce the log to a manageable context, but the field has had no public empirical comparison of which reductions preserve enough evidence for downstream LLM diagnosis. We introduce LogDx-CI, a benchmark that compares 11 context-reduction tools (raw, tail, grep, three RTK modes, two real LLM map-reduce summarizers, three hybrid routers) on 35 real GitHub Actions failure cases, scored by 3 LLM debugger families (Claude Haiku 4.5, Claude Sonnet 4.6, OpenAI gpt-5-mini) plus a Sonnet 4.6 tool-using agent. We report three load-bearing findings. (1)~Hybrid grep+tail routers dominate the cost-quality Pareto frontier; the top two methods score 0.670 / 0.666 at $\sim$ \$0.03 per case, same-ballpark quality as standalone grep at $4.5\times$ fewer tokens. (2)~In the agent-loop regime, the quality range across reduction tools collapses $7\times$ (single-shot spread 0.42 $\to$ agent-loop spread 0.059); the agent rescues weak contexts via follow-up tool calls. However, cost differences persist: weak contexts force the agent to issue 2--4$\times$ more tool calls to recover. (3)~A cross-family LLM-summary pair (gpt-5-mini summarizer feeding a Claude Haiku debugger) beats the same-family pair by $+0.071$ averaged across four diagnoser variants, falsifying the self-call-bias hypothesis on this task. The gpt-5-mini summarizer is also the agent-loop \#1 method (score 0.749) at $0.37$ tool-calls per case and $10\times$ lower reducer cost than the Haiku summarizer (\$0.18 vs \$1.75 per case). All data, code, per-case bundles, and reproducibility infrastructure are public.

</details>


### [5] [Energy-Aware Decision Making in Software Stack Upgrades](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26609v1)
*Mirko Stocker,Michael Wahler*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过系统方法测量了Spring Boot和JVM版本对应用程序能耗的影响，发现新版本和虚拟线程能显著节能，为软件升级决策提供了依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软件升级对能耗的影响未被充分理解，而组织对可持续发展的关注日益增长，因此需要系统的方法评估能耗变化以支持决策。

Method: 提出系统性方法，通过自动化基准测试评估不同版本Spring Boot和JVM的组合对应用能耗的影响，并以Spring Petclinic REST应用为例进行实验。

Result: 能耗在不同版本间差异显著，新JVM版本和虚拟线程（Java 21/23）带来节能效果，且无需修改应用代码，但某些版本组合出现能耗退化。

Conclusion: 软件升级能显著影响能耗，测量能耗可为软件维护和演进决策提供重要依据，建议将能耗纳入升级评估标准。

中文摘要：软件栈升级是软件维护和演进的常规部分，通常出于性能、稳定性或功能的改进。然而，它们对能耗的影响——这一对追求可持续发展的组织日益重要的关注点——仍然知之甚少。本文提出了一种系统方法，用于测量核心软件栈组件（如Spring Boot和Java虚拟机）的不同版本如何影响应用程序的能耗。我们的方法通过自动化基准测试评估框架版本、运行时版本和执行平台的组合。基于Spring Petclinic REST应用程序的案例研究，我们展示Spring Boot和JVM版本之间的能耗差异显著，在某些情况下出现了意外的性能退化。值得注意的是，新的JVM版本和虚拟线程（在Java 21和23中引入）在没有修改应用程序的情况下实现了显著的节能效果。这些结果表明，软件升级能够显著影响能耗，并且测量能耗为软件维护和演进中的决策提供了有价值的证据。

Original abstract: Software stack upgrades are a routine part of software maintenance and evolution, typically motivated by improved performance, stability, or functionality. Yet their impact on energy consumption - a growing concern for organizations pursuing sustainability - remains poorly understood. This paper presents a systematic method for measuring how different versions of core software stack components, such as Spring Boot and the Java Virtual Machine (JVM), influence the energy consumption of applications. Our approach evaluates combinations of framework versions, runtime versions, and execution platforms through automated benchmarking. Using a case study based on the Spring Petclinic REST application, we show that energy consumption varies substantially across Spring Boot and JVM versions, in some cases producing unexpected regressions. Notably, newer JVM releases and virtual threads (introduced in Java 21 and 23) yielded significant energy savings without requiring application changes. These results demonstrate that software upgrades can meaningfully affect energy usage and that measuring energy consumption provides valuable evidence for decision making in software maintenance and evolution.

</details>

This study systematically explores the SE podcast landscape, analyzing its content and surveying researchers to assess how podcasts can serve as a meaningful resource for advancing empirical software engineering research.

### [7] [HTMLCure: Turning Browser Experience into State Guided Repair for Interactive HTML](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26807v1)
*Jiajun Wu,Jian Yang,Tuney Zheng,Wei Zhang,Haowen Wang,Yihang Lou,Xianglong Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: HTMLCure是一个浏览器体验框架，通过交互式评估和闭环修复生成高质量HTML页面，显著提升SFT数据质量和模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有HTML生成评估仅检查初始渲染，忽略交互状态下的失败；截图评估有遗漏，过滤丢弃可修复页面，导致大量低质量页面未被有效利用。

Method: HTMLCure在浏览器中与HTML页面交互后，跨视口和状态执行，记录确定性证据并提取关键帧；利用状态信号驱动闭环修复引擎，诊断页面、选择修复类别、运行候选并导出质量清除页面，用于构建精炼SFT集。

Result: 在97K提示语料库上生成63703个质量清除页面，构建40K SFT集；HTMLCure-27B-Refined在HTMLBench-400上达到50.6分（45.2%确定性测试通过），在MiniAppBench上平均81.2分，比基线提升15.3分。

Conclusion: HTMLCure通过闭环交互评估与修复，有效提升了HTML生成质量和下游模型性能，性能接近强参考系统（如Kimi-K2.6和GPT-5.4）。

中文摘要：大语言模型现在能够生成完整的HTML页面，但其中许多页面仅仅是表面正确：它们能渲染一次，但在滚动、悬停、点击、调整大小或游戏互动时失败。基于截图的评估可能错过这些失败，而过滤会丢弃许多仍然可修复的页面。我们引入了HTMLCure，一个浏览器体验框架，该系统在与HTML交互后对其进行评估。评估器跨视口和交互状态执行页面，记录确定性的浏览器证据，并向VLM提供来自执行轨迹的关键帧，而非孤立的截图。相同的状态信号驱动一个闭环修复引擎：HTMLCure诊断当前页面，选择特定于状态的修复类别，重新运行每个候选方案，并导出质量已清除的页面用于SFT。在一个97K提示语料库上，这将直接可用的种子扩展为63703个质量已清除的候选池，从中我们构建了最终的40K页面的精炼SFT集。在相同的骨干和训练方法下，HTMLCure-27B-Refined在HTMLBench-400上达到50.6分，确定性测试用例通过率为45.2%，使其与强参照行如Kimi-K2.6和GPT-5.4处于相同的性能范围。在已发布的MiniAppBench验证集上，它达到81.2的平均分，比原始的27B SFT提高了15.3分，接近强参考系统的水平。

Original abstract: LLMs can now produce full HTML pages, but many of those pages are only superficially correct: they render once, then fail under scroll, hover, click, resize, or gameplay. Evaluation from screenshots can miss these failures, and filtering discards many pages that are still repairable. We introduce HTMLCure, a browser experience framework that evaluates HTML after the system has interacted with it. The evaluator executes the page across viewports and interaction states, records deterministic browser evidence, and gives the VLM curated keyframes from the executed trajectory rather than isolated screenshots. The same state signal drives a closed loop repair engine: HTMLCure diagnoses the current page, chooses a state specific repair family, runs each candidate again, and exports quality cleared pages for SFT. On a 97K prompt corpus, this expands the directly usable seed into a candidate pool of 63703 quality cleared pages, from which we construct the final refined SFT set of 40K pages. Under the same backbone and training recipe, HTMLCure-27B-Refined reaches 50.6 on HTMLBench-400 with 45.2% deterministic test case pass, placing it in the same performance band as strong reference rows such as Kimi-K2.6 and GPT-5.4. On the released MiniAppBench validation split, it reaches 81.2 average, improving raw 27B SFT by 15.3 points and approaching the level of strong reference systems.

### [8] [On the GitHub Actions Language: Usage, Evolution, and Workflow Reliability](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26825v1)
*Aref Talebzadeh Bardsiri,Alexandre Decan,Tom Mens*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过分析大量GitHub Actions工作流，发现仅少数语言结构被频繁使用，复杂工作流与高失败率和维护负担相关，并识别出风险特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发者常因GitHub Actions工作流配置维护困难而苦恼，且执行失败频繁，需探究语言结构的影响。

Method: 定量分析了来自49K仓库的260K个工作流，识别197种语言结构并映射到14个特性，统计使用频率和演变。

Result: 少数结构和特性频繁使用；更大更复杂的工作流有更高失败率和维护工作量；特定特性与可靠性和可维护性风险相关。

Conclusion: 研究结果有助于开发者和研究人员理解GitHub Actions语言，改进工作流自动化实践。

中文摘要：开发人员在使用 GitHub 托管的仓库中维护 GitHub Actions 工作流配置时经常遇到困难，近期研究显示执行失败频繁发生。本文通过实证研究探讨 GitHub Actions 语言结构的采用和演变如何影响工作流的可靠性和可维护性。为此，我们对来自 49K 个 GitHub 仓库的 260K 个工作流进行了定量分析，以了解它们在实际中的使用方式以及从 2019 年 7 月到 2025 年 8 月的使用演变。我们识别了 GitHub Actions 语言中可用的 197 种语言结构，并将其映射到反映工作流能力的 14 个特性。我们观察到只有一小部分结构和特性被频繁使用，且更大更复杂的工作流与更高的失败率和更多的维护工作相关。我们识别出特定的特性更可能与可靠性和可维护性风险相关。这些见解可以帮助从业者和研究人员更好地理解和使用 GitHub Actions 语言，从而有助于改进和维持工作流自动化实践。

Original abstract: Developers often struggle with maintaining GitHub Actions workflow configurations in GitHub-hosted repositories, with recent studies showing frequent execution failures. This paper empirically explores how the adoption and evolution of GitHub Actions language constructs impacts workflow reliability and maintainability. To do so, we quantitatively analyse 260K workflows from 49K GitHub repositories to understand how they are used in practice and how their usage has evolved from July 2019 to August 2025. We identify 197 language constructs available in the GitHub Actions language and map them to 14 features reflecting workflow capabilities. We observe that only a small set of constructs and features are used very frequently, and that larger and more complex workflows are associated with higher failure rates and more maintenance effort. We identify specific features that are more likely to be linked with reliability and maintainability risks. These insights can help practitioners and researchers improve their understanding and usage of the GitHub Actions language, which can help in improving and sustaining workflow automation practices.

### [9] [LLM-based Mockless Unit Test Generation for Java](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26851v1)
*Qinghua Xu,Guancheng Wang,Lionel Briand,Zhaoqiang Guo,Kui Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出MocklessTester，通过上下文丰富生成和约束增强修复解决LLM在无模拟单元测试中的幻觉问题，在Defects4J和Deps4J上显著提升覆盖率与变异得分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM生成Java单元测试依赖模拟框架，无模拟测试面临幻觉、语言约束和依赖感知不足等挑战，影响测试有效性。

Method: MocklessTester：上下文丰富生成（挖掘真实使用模式）和约束增强修复（符号、协议、迭代级约束下的两阶段修复，结合类索引、马尔可夫型状态模型和经验记忆）。

Result: 在Defects4J和Deps4J上，行覆盖率提升19.99%和22.69%，分支覆盖率提升24.90%和15.78%，变异得分提升13.67%和0.17%，额外覆盖依赖代码378和55行，成本平均每方法108.97秒/26.59k令牌和69.85秒/25.46k令牌。

Conclusion: MocklessTester有效提升无模拟测试质量，主要组件均贡献积极，成本实用可行。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在自动测试生成方面显示出强大的潜力，但大多数生成Java单元测试的方法仍然依赖模拟框架来处理依赖关系。无模拟测试生成可以执行更多真实的底层代码，但它面临由于幻觉导致的无效测试代码生成、严格的语言约束以及不充分的依赖感知等挑战。我们确定了这些幻觉背后的两个原因：不知道——LLM缺乏足够的上下文，以及不遵循——即使提供了约束，LLM也未能遵守。我们提出了MocklessTester，这是一种无模拟单元测试生成方法，围绕两个策略构建：上下文丰富生成和约束增强修复。为了缓解不知道的问题，上下文丰富生成从现有代码中挖掘真实使用模式来生成测试。为了缓解不遵循的问题，约束增强修复在符号、协议和迭代级别约束下执行两阶段修复，使用类索引、马尔可夫类型状态模型和经验记忆。我们在Defects4J和Deps4J上对MocklessTester与最先进的基线进行了评估。结果表明，MocklessTester在两个基准测试上分别将行覆盖率提高了19.99%和22.69%，分支覆盖率提高了24.90%和15.78%，并将变异得分提高了13.67%和0.17%。除了被测类之外，MocklessTester还执行了更多的真实依赖代码，分别在依赖类中覆盖了378行和55行额外的代码。测试质量的提高伴随着比基线更高的总令牌和时间成本。然而，每个方法的成本仍然是实用的，在Defects4J上平均为108.97秒和26.59k令牌，在Deps4J上平均为69.85秒和25.46k令牌。消融结果证实，所有主要组件都对最终性能做出了积极贡献。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown strong potential for automated test generation, yet most approaches to generating Java unit tests still rely on mocking frameworks to handle dependencies. Mockless test generation could exercise more real low-level code, but it faces challenges such as invalid test code generation due to hallucination, strict language constraints, and inadequate dependency awareness. We identify two causes behind these hallucinations: not knowing, where the LLM lacks sufficient context, and not following, where the LLM fails to comply with constraints even when they are provided.
  We present MocklessTester, a mockless unit test generation approach built around two strategies: context-enriched generation and constraint-enforced fixing. To mitigate not knowing, context-enriched generation mines real usage patterns from existing code to generate tests. To mitigate not following, constraint-enforced fixing performs two-stage repair under symbol-, protocol-, and iteration-level constraints, using a ClassIndex, a Markov typestate model, and experience memory.
  We evaluate MocklessTester against the state-of-the-art baseline on Defects4J and Deps4J. Results show that MocklessTester improves line coverage by 19.99% and 22.69% and branch coverage by 24.90% and 15.78% on the two benchmarks, respectively, and improves mutation score by 13.67% and 0.17%. Beyond the class under test, MocklessTester also exercises more real dependency code, covering 378 and 55 additional lines in dependency classes, respectively. The improvement in test quality comes with higher total token and time costs than the baseline. Nevertheless, the cost per method remains practical, averaging 108.97 seconds and 26.59k tokens on Defects4J, and 69.85 seconds and 25.46k tokens on Deps4J. Ablation results confirm that all major components contribute positively to the final performance.

</details>


### [10] [Strategies for Guiding LLMs to Use Software Design Patterns: A Case of Singleton](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26898v1)
*Viktor Kjellberg,Farnaz Fotrousi,Miroslaw Staron*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过实验比较了四种提示策略，发现迭代二元反馈最能引导LLM生成符合单例设计模式的代码，同时保持或提升功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成的代码常忽略设计模式，影响长期软件质量，因此需要研究如何引导LLM遵循设计原则。

Method: 设计计算实验，测试13个LLM在164个Java任务中采用四种提示策略（指令、二元反馈、广泛反馈、广泛反馈+少样本）生成单例模式代码。

Result: 最优策略依赖模型类型；整体上迭代二元反馈效果最佳；Llama 3.3和Qwen 3在指令或二元反馈下表现突出。

Conclusion: 简单策略即可有效引导LLM应用设计模式，但需根据模型选择策略。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）能够从自然语言提示生成功能性源代码，但往往无法一致地遵循更高级的架构结构或设计模式。由于LLM越来越多地用于软件工程，它们将既定设计原则应用于生成代码的能力对于软件产品的长期成功至关重要。因此，本文的目标是确定引导LLM将设计模式纳入生成代码的策略。我们设计了一个计算实验，评估13个LLM使用四种提示策略（指令、二元自动反馈、广泛自动反馈以及广泛反馈加少样本提示）在HumanEval-X的164个Java编码挑战中生成遵循单例设计模式的代码的能力。我们的结果表明，引导LLM包含设计模式的最优策略在很大程度上取决于模型类型。但总体而言，迭代二元反馈在保持或改善代码功能的同时，提供了与单例模式的最佳对齐。通过指令引导时，Llama 3.3在100%的情况下生成了单例类，并改善了代码功能，使通过的测试数量增加了34.1个百分点。通过指令和二元反馈引导时，它取得了类似的结果。Qwen 3（8B）使用二元反馈使与单例模式的对齐增加到99.2%，功能性提高到58.6%。我们的结果表明，即使是简单的策略也可以用来引导LLM使用设计模式。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) can generate functional source code from natural-language prompts, but often fail to consistently follow higher-level architectural structures or design patterns. Since LLMs are increasingly used in software engineering, their ability to apply established design principles to generated code is crucial to the long-term success of software products. Therefore, the goal of this paper is to identify strategies for guiding LLMs to incorporate design patterns into the generated source code. We designed a computational experiment to evaluate the ability of 13 LLMs to generate code that follows the Singleton design pattern, using four prompting strategies: instructions, binary automated feedback, extensive automated feedback, and extensive feedback with few-shot prompts, in 164 Java coding challenges from HumanEval-X. Our results shows that the optimal strategy to guide LLMs to include design patterns depends heavily on the type of model. Still, overall, iterative binary feedback provides the best alignment with Singleton while preserving or improving the code's functionality. With guiding with instructions, Llama 3.3 generated Singleton classes in 100% of cases and improved code functionality, increasing the number of tests passed by 34.1 percentage points. It achieved a similar result with guidance through instructions and binary feedback. Qwen 3 (8B) increased the alignment with Singleton to 99.2% and the functionality to 58.6% using binary feedback. Our result suggests that even simple strategies can be used to guide LLMs to use design patterns.

</details>


### [11] [ConVer: Using Contracts and Loop Invariant Synthesis for Scalable Formal Software Verification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27051v1)
*Muhammad A. A. Pirzada,Weiqi Wang,Yiannis Charalambous,Konstantin Korovin,Lucas C. Cordeiro*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: ConVer是一种自顶向下组合式C程序验证工具，利用LLM合成函数契约和CEGAR-CEGIS循环，在多个基准测试上优于SOTA，并提出了ESBMC-LF转换LF模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有BMC工具因状态空间爆炸难以验证大型C程序，需要更高效的分解验证方法。

Method: 自顶向下分解验证：LLM合成函数契约，结合CEGAR-CEGIS循环和SMART ICE学习细化契约，以及ESBMC-LF转换LF模型。

Result: 在多个基准测试上实现33-96%成功率，多数仅需一次CEGAR-CEGIS迭代，优于SOTA工具。

Conclusion: ConVer结合LLM和组合验证能有效缓解状态空间爆炸，ESBMC-LF扩展了其应用范围。

中文摘要：大型C程序的形式化验证受到状态空间爆炸的阻碍：有界模型检验（BMC）工具必须通过展开所有嵌套构造来编码达到预定边界的整个状态空间。我们提出了ConVer，一种自顶向下的组合式验证工具。给定一个带有顶层断言的C程序，ConVer自顶向下分解验证：它使用大语言模型（LLM）从系统属性合成函数契约，然后在CEGAR-CEGIS循环中交替进行系统级和函数级检查，每当检查失败时通过SMART ICE学习细化契约。我们在四个难度递增的基准测试套件上评估ConVer，并与其他最先进（SOTA）工具进行比较。在包含45个简单C程序的Frama-C基准测试上，ConVer在三个LLM后端上实现了82-96%的验证成功率，其中93-95%的收敛程序仅需一次CEGAR-CEGIS迭代。在X.509解析器基准测试（6个程序）和LF2C-Simple套件（17个程序）上，ConVer分别实现了33-50%和82-88%的成功率。在包含11个递归和循环密集型程序的VerifyThis套件上，前置抽象策略实现了55-64%的成功率。此外，我们提出了ESBMC-LF，一个将LF模型转换为C同时保留LF文件属性的预处理器工具，使ConVer能够验证它们。我们使用ESBMC-LF将LF验证器基准测试转换为C；我们将其记为LF-Hard。我们表明ConVer整体成功验证了67%的LF-Hard基准测试。

Original abstract: Formal verification of large C programs is impeded by state-space explosion: Bounded Model Checking (BMC) tools must encode the entire state space up to the predetermined bound by unrolling all nested constructs. We present ConVer, a top-down compositional verification tool. Given a C program with a top-level assertion, ConVer decomposes verification top-down: it uses a large language model (LLM) to synthesise function contracts from the system property, then alternates system-level and function-level checks in a CEGAR-CEGIS loop, refining contracts whenever a check fails via SMART ICE learning. We evaluate ConVer on four benchmark suites of increasing difficulty and against other state-of-the-art (SOTA) tools. On the Frama-C benchmark of 45 simple C programs, ConVer achieves 82-96% verification success across three LLM backends, with 93-95% of converged programs requiring only a single CEGAR-CEGIS iteration. On the X.509 parser benchmark (6~programs) and LF2C-Simple suite (17 programs), ConVer achieves 33-50% and 82-88% success respectively. On the VerifyThis suite of 11 recursive and loop-intensive programs, the Pre-Abstraction strategy achieves 55-64% success. In addition, we present ESBMC-LF a preprocessor tool that converts LF models to C while preserving the properties of the LF files, enabling ConVer to verify them. We transpile the LF Verifier Benchmarks using ESBMC-LF to C; we denote those LF-Hard. We show that ConVer successfully verifies 67% of LF-Hard benchmarks overall.

</details>


### [12] [EviACT: An Evidence-to-Action Framework for Agentic Program Repair](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27238v1)
*Qianru Meng,Xiao Zhang,Zhaochun Ren,Joost Visser*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: EviACT是一个基于执行证据驱动的智能体APR框架，通过协调三个防护栏（检索脚手架、编译门、测试驱动门）在修复各阶段引导定位、生成和验证，在多个基准上显著提升修复率并降低API成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体APR系统无法有效利用执行证据来指导定位、补丁生成和验证，导致效率低下。

Method: 提出EviACT框架，包含三个证据驱动防护栏：检索脚手架用于定位修复上下文，编译门过滤无效编辑，测试驱动门在完全回归前检查目标测试恢复。

Result: 在四个基准上，EviACT相比最强基线提升修复率1.6-6.0个百分点，每漏洞API成本降低70.1-88.6%。

Conclusion: 协调的证据到行动链使智能体APR更有效和高效，消融和诊断实验证实了各组件贡献。

中文摘要：基于LLM的智能体已经将自动程序修复（APR）从固定上下文的补丁生成转变为交互式仓库级修复。然而，现有的智能体APR系统仍然难以利用执行证据来指导定位、补丁生成和验证。我们提出了EviACT（Evidence-to-Action），一个智能体APR框架，它协调了三个跨修复阶段的证据驱动防护栏。检索脚手架为修复上下文提供基础，编译门过滤无效编辑，测试驱动门在完全回归之前检查目标测试恢复。在四个基准测试中，EviACT相对于报告的最强可比基线将解决率提高了1.6-6.0个百分点，并且在基线成本可用的情况下，每漏洞API成本降低了70.1-88.6%。消融和诊断表明，这些收益与协调的证据到行动链相关，使得智能体APR更加有效和高效。

Original abstract: LLM-based agents have moved automated program repair (APR) from fixed-context patch generation to interactive repository-level repair. However, existing agentic APR systems still struggle to use execution evidence to guide localization, patch generation, and validation. We propose EviACT (Evidence-to-Action), an agentic APR framework that coordinates three evidence-driven guardrails across repair stages. The retrieval scaffold grounds repair context, the compile gate filters invalid edits, and the test-driven gate checks target-test recovery before full regression. Across four benchmarks, EviACT improves resolve rate over the strongest reported comparable baselines by 1.6-6.0 percentage points and shows 70.1-88.6% lower reported per-bug API cost where baseline costs are available. Ablations and diagnostics suggest that these gains are associated with the coordinated evidence-to-action chain, making agentic APR more effective and efficient.

</details>


### [13] [Benchmarks are Not Enough: RAMP for Runtime Assessing of Agentic Models in Production Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27492v1)
*Yipeng Ouyang,Xin Huang,Bingjie Liu,Zhongchun Zheng,Yuhao Gu,Xianwei Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: RAMP是一个生产导向的评估基础设施，用于评估长周期软件工程代理，揭示了在连续任务中模型性能显著下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试无法捕捉真实生产环境的动态复杂性和长周期任务，导致模型实际能力被高估。

Method: 基于YatCC平台，提供统一运行时评估架构，引入编译器构建工作负载和分阶段恢复机制，采用面向效用的多维指标。

Result: 15个主流模型在串行工作流中任务完成率从100%降至20%，无模型完成整个流水线，计算成本差异达三个数量级，故障传播显著。

Conclusion: RAMP将评估推向持续、运行时可观察和生产导向，揭示了传统基准测试不可见的能力退化。

中文摘要：LLM代理正迅速从编码助手演变为自主软件工程系统。然而，现有的评估方法仍然主要集中于静态、孤立和短视的基准测试，未能捕捉真实生产工作流的动态复杂性。因此，基准测试性能可能无法很好地反映在涉及长执行链、工具交互、依赖管理和迭代反馈循环的真实运行时环境中的实际能力。为此，我们提出了RAMP，一个用于评估长周期软件工程代理的生产导向基础设施。RAMP建立在YatCC集成平台之上，通过标准化编排和执行接口提供统一的运行时评估架构。RAMP引入了具有串行依赖和复杂工具链交互的真实编译器构建工作负载，以及一个用于分析部分工作流失败下执行行为的分阶段恢复机制。该框架进一步结合了面向效用的多维指标，共同评估结果质量和过程效率。我们跨15个主流模型进行了运行时评估，观察到在传统孤立基准测试中基本不可见的显著能力退化。任务完成率在串行工作流中逐渐崩溃，从初始阶段的100%下降到最终阶段的仅20%，且没有一个评估模型成功完成整个流水线。运行时分析揭示了系统性的故障传播和显著的资源低效，不同模型的计算成本差异高达三个数量级。这些发现表明，RAMP将代理模型评估推向持续、运行时可观察和生产导向的评估。

Original abstract: LLM agents are rapidly evolving from coding assistants into autonomous software engineering systems. However, existing evaluation methodologies remain largely centered on static, isolated, and short-horizon benchmarks that fail to capture the dynamic complexity of real-world production workflows. As a result, benchmark performance may poorly reflect practical capability under realistic runtime environments involving long execution chains, tool interactions, dependency management, and iterative feedback loops. We thus present RAMP, a production-grounded infrastructure for assessing long-horizon software engineering agents. Built upon the YatCC integrated platform, RAMP provides a unified runtime assessment architecture through standardized orchestration and execution interfaces. RAMP introduces realistic compiler-construction workloads with serial dependencies and complex toolchain interactions, together with a staged recovery mechanism for analyzing execution behavior under partial workflow failure. The framework further incorporates utility-oriented multi-dimensional metrics that jointly evaluate outcome quality and process efficiency. We conduct runtime assessments across 15 mainstream models and observe substantial capability degradation that remains largely invisible to conventional isolated benchmarks. Task completion rates progressively collapse across serial workflows, dropping from 100% in the initial stage to only 20% in the final stage, while none of the evaluated models successfully completes the entire pipeline. Runtime analysis reveals systematic failure propagation and significant resource inefficiencies, with computational costs differing by up to three orders of magnitude among comparable models. These findings suggest RAMP advances agentic model evaluation toward continuous, runtime-observable, and production-grounded assessment.

</details>


### [14] [Governed Evolution of Agent Runtimes through Executable Operational Cognition](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27328v1)
*Mariano Garralda-Barrio*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一个通过可执行操作认知实现多智能体系统受控运行时演化的框架，引入HarnessMutation机制，确保演化过程明确、可审计且受约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体系统对生成的代码产物缺乏治理、生命周期管理和操作演化的明确规范，导致运行时演化不受控。

Method: 将智能体生成产物视为持久运行时能力，提出HarnessMutation作为生命周期感知的运行时适应机制，在验证、可追溯、评估和回滚约束下运行，并将演化建模为有界可观察过程。

Result: 展示了该框架可在现代智能体运行时和治理型编排系统中实现，为自适应基础设施提供概念基础。

Conclusion: 该框架使得多智能体系统的运行时演化保持明确、可审计且受约束，为构建可长期演化的自适应系统提供了理论基础。

中文摘要：近期在智能体系统中的进展越来越多地将代码视为可执行的操作基底，而非一次性的输出产物。先前的工作如《Code as Agent Harness》将经过验证的智能体生成产物视为运行时实体，可在长时间运行的认知循环中被创建、执行、修改、持久化和重用。然而，这些产物的治理、生命周期管理和操作演化仍然未被充分定义。本文提出了一个通过可执行操作认知实现多智能体系统中受控运行时演化的框架。我们将智能体生成的产物形式化为持久的运行时能力，这些能力逐步成为操作基底的一部分，而非瞬时的中间输出。基于这一视角，我们引入了《HarnessMutation》作为一种受控机制，用于生命周期感知的运行时适应，并在明确的验证、可追溯性、评估和回滚约束下运行。该框架并未将运行时适应视为不受限制的自我修改，而是将演化建模为在持久操作记忆上的有界且可观察的过程。它还展示了如何将这些思想在现代智能体运行时和面向治理的编排系统中付诸实践，为自适应基础设施提供了概念基础，使其演化保持明确、可审计且受约束。

Original abstract: Recent advances in agentic systems increasingly treat code as an executable operational substrate rather than as a disposable output artifact. Prior work such as \emph{Code as Agent Harness} frames validated agent-generated artifacts as runtime entities that can be created, executed, revised, persisted, and reused within long-running cognitive loops. However, the governance, lifecycle management, and operational evolution of such artifacts remain under-specified.
  This paper proposes a framework for governed runtime evolution in multi-agent systems through executable operational cognition. We formalize agent-generated artifacts as persistent runtime capabilities that progressively become part of the operational substrate rather than transient intermediate outputs. Building on this perspective, we introduce \emph{HarnessMutation} as a governed mechanism for lifecycle-aware runtime adaptation operating under explicit validation, traceability, evaluation, and rollback constraints.
  Rather than treating runtime adaptation as unrestricted self-modification, the proposed framework models evolution as a bounded and observable process over persistent operational memory. It further shows how these ideas can be operationalized over modern agent runtimes and governance-oriented orchestration systems, providing a conceptual foundation for adaptive infrastructures whose evolution remains explicit, auditable, and constrained.

</details>


### [15] [EdgeFlow: Edge-Map Augmented VLM-Based Flowchart Processing for Industrial Requirements Engineering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27332v1)
*Zhifei Dou,Shabnam Hassani,Ou Wei*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出EdgeFlow，通过向VLM输入添加Canny边缘图作为结构先验，无需训练即可改进流程图到Mermaid转换，在工业数据集上显著提升拓扑保留性能，但在合成基准上无明显改善。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLM在流程图转换中常忽略拓扑关键视觉细节，导致转换失败。

Method: 增强VLM输入，加入确定性提取的Canny边缘图作为结构先验，无需标注数据或微调。

Result: 在IndusReqFlow上，节点级F1提升17.39pp，边级F1提升16.94pp，路径级F1提升11.06pp；在合成基准上无显著提升。

Conclusion: EdgeFlow提供了实用的训练免费方法，但需更多工业数据基准以全面评估VLM-based RE工具。

中文摘要：流程图广泛应用于工业需求中，但通常以静态图像形式嵌入。视觉语言模型（VLM）在将这些流程图转换为用于RE活动的机器可读模型方面显示出潜力，然而，当直接应用于流程图转换时，它们常常在拓扑关键视觉细节上失败。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了EdgeFlow，它通过增强VLM的原始输入，添加一个确定性提取的Canny边缘图——作为结构先验——来改进流程图到Mermaid的转换，而无需标注训练数据或领域特定模型微调。我们在IndusReqFlow（一个来自真实世界需求的数据集）上评估EdgeFlow。与现成的VLM相比，EdgeFlow将节点级F1提高了17.39个百分点，边级F1提高了16.94个百分点。在路径级别，EdgeFlow将路径F1提高了11.06个百分点，从而更好地支持基于模型的测试。这些结果表明，EdgeFlow提供了一种实用的、无需训练的方法，用于改进工业RE中保持拓扑结构的流程图到Mermaid转换。在公共合成基准上的跨数据集评估结果显示没有显著改善；这突出表明需要包含工业数据的多样化基准，以全面评估未来的基于VLM的RE工具。

Original abstract: Flowcharts are widely used in industrial requirements, but usually remain embedded as static images. Vision Language Models (VLMs) show promise in the conversion of these flowcharts into machine-readable models for RE activities, yet, when directly applied to flowchart conversion, they often fail on topology-critical visual details. To address this, we propose EdgeFlow that augments a VLM's original input with a deterministically extracted Canny edge map-acting as a structural prior-to improve flowchart-to-Mermaid conversion, without requiring annotated training data or domain-specific model fine-tuning.
  We evaluate EdgeFlow on IndusReqFlow, a dataset sourced from real-world requirements. Compared with off-the-shelf VLMs, EdgeFlow improves node-level F1 by 17.39 percentage points and edge-level F1 by 16.94 percentage points. At the path level, EdgeFlow improves path F1 by 11.06 percentage points, enabling better support for model-based testing. These results demonstrate that EdgeFlow provides a practical, training-free means to improve topology-preserving flowchart-to-Mermaid conversion for industrial RE. Cross-dataset evaluation results on a public synthetic benchmark show no significant improvement; this highlights the need for diverse benchmarks incorporating industrial data for the comprehensive evaluation of future VLM-based RE tools.

</details>


### [16] [LLM Based Web Accessibility Repair: An Empirical Study of Detection, Remediation, and Cost](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27716v1)
*Oluwatoyosi Oyelayo,Ghada Abushaqra,Parham Asadi,Durjoy Dey,Diego Elias Costa*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 评估LLM（Kimi K2.5）在网页可访问性检测和修复上的表现，发现其部分有效但不可靠，建议结合规则验证的混合方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克服规则工具覆盖面有限和手动修复成本高且易出错的问题，探索LLM在可访问性自动化上的潜力。

Method: 使用Kimi K2.5 LLM智能体进行自动化可访问性检测和修复，并与基于规则的工具进行性能对比。

Result: 检测F1约0.65，语义理解F1为0.83；修复后违规数从3.98降至1.7，但完全解决率低于26%，约30%补丁引入结构变化；迭代细化增加成本但未改善结果。

Conclusion: LLM对部分可访问性修复有效，但无法实现完全可靠的修复，需要混合（LLM+规则验证+约束感知修正）方法以实现可扩展的解决方案。

中文摘要：确保大规模网页可访问性仍然具有挑战性，因为基于规则的工具覆盖面有限，而手动修复成本高且易出错。本文评估了基于大语言模型的智能体，特别是Kimi K2.5，用于自动化可访问性检测和修复，并与基于规则的方法进行比较。在检测方面，LLM取得了与基于规则工具相当的性能，F1约为0.65，语义理解能力强（F1为0.83），但在语法和布局相关违规方面的可靠性较低。在修复方面，LLM生成的修复在超过99.7%的情况下语法有效，并在80.2%的实例中提高了可访问性合规性，将每个文件的违规数从3.98减少到1.7。然而，完全解决的情况不到26%，约30%的补丁引入了结构变化。我们还发现，基于智能体的迭代细化会使计算成本增加52%，API使用量增加1.64倍，但并未改善修复结果。这些发现表明，虽然LLM在部分可访问性修复方面有效，但不足以实现完全可靠的修复。可扩展的可访问性解决方案需要结合LLM能力与基于规则的验证及约束感知修正机制的混合方法。

Original abstract: Ensuring web accessibility at scale remains challenging because rule-based tools provide limited coverage while manual remediation is costly and error-prone. This paper evaluates large language model based agents, specifically Kimi K2.5, for automated accessibility detection and repair compared with rule-based approaches. For detection, the LLM achieves performance comparable to rule-based tools, with F1 around 0.65, strong semantic understanding with F1 of 0.83, but lower reliability for syntactic and layout-related violations. For remediation, LLM-generated fixes are syntactically valid in over 99.7 percent of cases and improve accessibility compliance in 80.2 percent of instances, reducing violations from 3.98 to 1.7 per file. However, fewer than 26 percent of cases are fully resolved, and about 30 percent of patches introduce structural changes. We also find that iterative agent-based refinement increases computational cost by 52 percent and API usage by 1.64 times without improving remediation outcomes. These findings indicate that while LLMs are effective for partial accessibility repair, they are insufficient for complete and reliable remediation. Scalable accessibility solutions require hybrid approaches that combine LLM capabilities with rule-based validation and constraint-aware correction mechanisms.

</details>

### [17] [From Static Context to Calibrated Interactive RL: Mitigating Distribution Shift in Multi-turn Dialogue with Aligned Simulator](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26403v1)
*Xiaohua Wang,Jiakang Yuan,Zisu Huang,Muzhao Tian,Changze Lv,Kaitao Song,Tao Chen,Xiaoqing Zheng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出校准交互RL框架解决对话agent的分布偏移，可迁移到agent自我改进。

TL;DR: 提出Calibrated Interactive RL框架，通过交互式RL与模拟器对齐来解决对话中的上下文分布偏移问题，实验证明其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对话策略优化方法（静态上下文RL和交互式RL）受限于上下文分布偏移，该偏移在对话轮次中二次方累积，严重降低对话质量。

Method: 提出Calibrated Interactive RL，耦合交互式RL与模拟器对齐，通过对齐模拟器与人类交互模式减少模拟到真实差距，缓解累积分布偏移。

Result: 在多个对话任务中，交互式RL显著优于静态上下文基线；校准模拟器进一步弥合模拟到真实差距，取得最先进性能。

Conclusion: 上下文分布偏移是对话策略优化的关键瓶颈，所提框架通过模拟器对齐有效缓解该问题，验证了理论分析。

中文摘要：研究界的一个长期目标是开发高度交互的基于LLM的对话代理。最近的研究侧重于基于固定离线日志（静态上下文RL）或使用基于提示的模拟器（交互式RL）来优化策略。在这项工作中，我们从理论上表明，这两种范式都受到上下文分布偏移的根本限制——即训练期间观察到的对话历史与真实对话中遇到的对话历史之间的不匹配。这种偏移在轮次之间呈二次方累积，并严重降低对话质量。具体来说，我们将这种偏移归因于两个不同的来源：（i）策略引起的偏移，源于在静态历史上训练而非自我生成的轨迹；（ii）模拟器引起的偏移，源于模拟人类行为与真实人类行为之间的差异。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了校准交互式RL，一个将交互式RL与模拟器对齐相结合的统一框架。通过将模拟器与人类交互模式对齐，我们的方法减少了模拟到真实的差距并减轻了累积分布偏移。在多个对话任务上的实验证实了我们的理论分析：（i）交互式RL通过减轻策略分布偏移，显著优于静态上下文基线；（ii）使用我们的对齐方法校准模拟器进一步弥合了模拟到真实的差距，产生了最先进的下游性能。

Original abstract: A long-standing goal of the research community is to develop highly interactive LLM-based dialogue agents. Recent research focuses on optimizing policies based on fixed offline logs (Static Context RL) or using a prompt-based simulator (Interactive RL). In this work, we theoretically show that both paradigms are fundamentally limited by context distribution shift--a mismatch between dialogue histories observed during training and those encountered in real conversations. This shift compounds quadratically over turns and severely degrades dialogue quality. Specifically, we attribute this shift to two distinct sources: (i) policy-induced shift, arising from training on static histories rather than self-generated trajectories; and (ii) simulator-induced shift, stemming from discrepancies between simulated and real human behaviors. To address these challenges, we propose Calibrated Interactive RL, a unified framework that couples interactive RL with simulator alignment. By aligning the simulator with human interaction patterns, our approach reduces the sim-to-real gap and mitigates compounding distribution shifts. Experiments across multiple dialogue tasks confirm our theoretical analysis: (i) Interactive RL significantly outperforms the Static Context baseline by mitigating policy distribution shift; and (ii) calibrating simulators with our alignment method further bridges the sim-to-real gap, yielding state-of-the-art downstream performance.

</details>


### [18] [Reasoning, Code, or Both? How Large Language Models Handle Variations in Math Questions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26414v1)
*Matthew Kutakh*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 比较推理与代码执行agent在数学问题中的鲁棒性，涉及coding agent评估。

TL;DR: 代码执行方法（单次或迭代）并未改善LLM在年级水平数学问题变体上的推理鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码执行方法被提出用于提高LLM的推理鲁棒性，但其效果尚未被系统测试。

Method: 在GSM-Symbolic数据集的1000个问题上评估三种方法：CoT（纯推理）、PAL（单次代码执行）、SBSC（迭代代码执行），使用Claude Haiku 4.5，对比原始和修改问题。

Result: CoT最鲁棒（准确率降1.3%，1.8%失效），PAL最差（降1.7%，3.1%失效），SBSC居中；差异不显著（p=.096），但趋势一致。

Conclusion: 代码执行（单次或迭代）未能改善年级水平问题变体上的推理鲁棒性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）在数学推理基准测试上取得了令人印象深刻的准确性，但当问题经过简单修改（如改变名称或数字）时，其性能会下降。代码执行方法——让模型生成并运行Python代码而非用自然语言推理——已被提出作为解决方案，但其对推理鲁棒性（即在问题变体中保持准确性的能力）的影响尚未经过系统性测试。本研究在GSM-Symbolic数据集的1000个问题上评估了三种方法：使用思维链（CoT）提示的纯推理、使用程序辅助语言模型（PAL）的单次代码执行、以及使用逐步编码（SBSC）的迭代代码执行。所有三种方法均在配对原始问题和修改问题上使用Claude Haiku 4.5运行。CoT是最鲁棒的方法，准确率下降1.3个百分点，且有1.8%的问题在扰动下失效。PAL是最不鲁棒的，准确率下降1.7个百分点，3.1%失效，SBSC介于两者之间。尽管这些差异在统计上不显著（p = .096），但方向性趋势在所有测量中一致，表明代码执行（无论是单次还是迭代）并不能改善年级水平问题变体上的推理鲁棒性。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) achieve impressive accuracy on mathematical reasoning benchmarks, yet their performance drops when problems are modified with simple changes like different names or numbers. Code execution methods, which let models generate and run Python code instead of reasoning in natural language, have been proposed as a solution, but their effect on reasoning robustness (the ability to maintain accuracy across problem variations) has not been systematically tested. This study evaluates three approaches on 1,000 problems from the GSM-Symbolic dataset: pure reasoning using chain-of-thought (CoT) prompting, single-shot code execution using Program-Aided Language models (PAL), and iterative code execution using Step-by-Step Coding (SBSC). All three were run on paired original and modified problems using Claude Haiku 4.5. CoT was the most robust method, with an accuracy drop of 1.3 percentage points and 1.8% of problems breaking under perturbation. PAL was the least robust at 1.7 percentage points and 3.1% broke, with SBSC falling in between. Although these differences were not statistically significant ($p = .096$), the directional trend was consistent across all measures, suggesting that code execution, whether single-shot or iterative, does not improve reasoning robustness on grade-school-level problem variations.

</details>

*MiniMax,:,Aili Chen,Aonian Li,Baichuan Zhou,Bangwei Gong,Binyang Jiang,Boji Dan,Changqing Yu,Chao Wang,Cheng Ma,Cheng Zhong,Cheng Zhu,Chengjun Xiao,Chengyi Yang,Chengyu Du,Chenyang Zhang,Chi Liao,Yuxuan Shi,Yuze Wenren,Zebin Li,Zehan Li,Zejian Luo,Zeyu Jin,Zeyuan Sun,Zhanpeng Zhou,Zhaochen Su,Zhendong Li,Zhengmao Zhu,Zhengyuan Peng,Zhenhua Fan,Zhi Zhang,Zhichao Xu,Zhiheng Lv,Zhikang Xu,Zhitao He,Zhiwei He,Zhongyuan Li,Zibo Gao,Zijia Wu,Zijian Song,Zijian Zhou,Zijun Sun,Zishan Huang,Ziying Chen,Ziyue Ge*

Selection reason: MiniMax-M2系列，系统性agent管道与RL训练，直接相关coding agent

TL;DR: MiniMax-M2系列通过小型激活和混合专家模型，结合智能体驱动数据流水线和强化学习系统，在多个基准上取得前沿性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于“小型激活可以释放最大现实世界智能”原则，构建高效且适用于智能体部署的语言模型。

Method: 采用三个核心组件：智能体驱动的数据流水线（生成可验证轨迹）、Forge强化学习系统（支持长期轨迹与训练-推理解耦）以及M2.7的自我进化能力。

Result: 在智能体编码、深度搜索、办公任务和推理基准上达到前沿性能。

Conclusion: 小型激活足迹结合智能体驱动设计与强化学习，可转化为实际任务中的高水平表现。

中文摘要：我们介绍了MiniMax-M2系列，这是一个基于“小型激活可以释放最大现实世界智能”原则的混合专家语言模型家族。旗舰模型M2总参数量为2299亿，但每个token仅激活98亿参数。M2系列专为智能体部署而端到端设计，基于三个组件：(i) 智能体驱动的数据流水线，产生大规模、可验证的轨迹，涵盖智能体编码和智能体协作，每个轨迹都基于可执行工作空间和与工件对齐的奖励；(ii) Forge，一个可扩展的智能体原生强化学习系统，适应长期智能体轨迹，结合了窗口FIFO调度、前缀树合并、推理优化，以及清晰的训练-推理-智能体解耦，支持白盒和黑盒智能体；(iii) 最新的M2.7检查点向自我进化迈出了早期一步——自主调试训练运行并修改自身框架。从M2到M2.7，这种组合将小型激活足迹转化为在智能体编码、深度搜索、办公任务和推理基准上的前沿性能。

Original abstract: We introduce the MiniMax-M2 series, a family of Mixture-of-Experts language models built around the principle that mini activations can unleash maximum real-world intelligence. The flagship M2 contains 229.9B total parameters with only 9.8B activated per token. Designed end-to-end for agentic deployment, the M2 series rests on three components: (i) agent-driven data pipelines producing large-scale, verifiable trajectories across agentic coding and agentic cowork, each grounded in an executable workspace and an artifact-aligned reward; (ii) Forge, a scalable agent-native RL system that adapts to long-horizon agent trajectories, paired with windowed-FIFO scheduling, prefix-tree merging, inference optimization, and a clean training-inference-agent decoupling that supports both white-box and black-box agents; (iii) the latest M2.7 checkpoint takes an early step toward self-evolution -- autonomously debugging training runs and modifying its own scaffold. Across M2 through M2.7, this combination translates a mini-activation footprint into frontier-tier performance on agentic coding, deep search, office-task, and reasoning benchmarks.

### [20] [Which Changes Matter? Towards Trustworthy Legal AI via Relevance-Sensitive Evaluation and Solver-Grounded Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26530v1)
*Chen Linze,Cai Yufan,Hou Zhe,Dong Jin Song*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 法律AI多agent框架，使用SMT验证，可迁移至代码agent验证与鲁棒性

TL;DR: 提出LexGuard框架，通过形式推理和多智能体对抗提高法律LLM对法律相关变化的敏感性和推理可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有法律LLM对法律无关变化敏感且未能区分相关法律要素和规则，需要提升对法律相关变化的校准敏感性。

Method: LexGuard将法规形式化为可执行约束，使用对抗性智能体提取竞争性事实-法规论证，并调用SMT求解器验证法律满足性和逻辑一致性。

Result: LexGuard减少了操纵性框架的脆弱性，改进了相似法规的区分，限制了法律无关属性的影响，提高了良性重述下的一致性。

Conclusion: 法律可信赖性不仅需要准确性，还需要对法律重要变化的校准敏感性。

中文摘要：法律推理需要区分那些重要的变化和那些无关紧要的变化。法律人工智能在面临法律上无关的扰动时应保持稳定，但当扰动改变法律上的关键点时，它应该发生变化。我们将这一要求表述为一个法律相关性敏感性评估问题：大语言模型只应对法律相关的变化敏感。我们引入了一个统一的评估套件，涵盖司法公平性、鲁棒性和法规混淆场景中的“应变化”和“不应变化”评估。我们的评估显示，现有的法律大语言模型系统性地对法律上无关的变化敏感，并且常常无法区分相关的法律要素和法规规则。为了缓解这些失败，我们提出了LexGuard，一种基于形式推理的对抗性多智能体框架。LexGuard将法规形式化为可执行的约束，使用对抗性智能体提取竞争性的事实-法规论证，并调用SMT求解器来验证法律满足性和逻辑一致性。实验表明，LexGuard通过减少对操纵性框架的脆弱性、改进相似法规之间的区分、限制法律上无关属性的影响以及提高良性重述下的一致性，提高了法律推理的可靠性。我们表明，法律可信赖性不仅需要准确性，还需要对法律重要变化的校准敏感性。

Original abstract: Legal reasoning requires distinguishing changes that matter from those that do not. Legal AI should remain stable under legally irrelevant perturbations, but should change when perturbations alter legally material points. We formulate this requirement as a legal-relevance-sensitive evaluation problem: LLMs should only be sensitive to the legally relevant change. We introduce a unified evaluation suite covering should-change and should-not-change evaluation across judicial fairness, robustness, and statute-confusion scenarios. Our evaluation shows that existing legal LLMs are systematically sensitive to legally irrelevant variations and often fail to distinguish related legal elements and statutory rules. To mitigate these failures, we present LexGuard, an adversarial multi-agent framework grounded in formal reasoning. LexGuard formalizes statutes into executable constraints, uses adversarial agents to extract competing fact-statute arguments, and invokes SMT solvers to verify legal satisfaction and logical consistency. Experiments show that LexGuard improves legal reasoning reliability by reducing vulnerability to manipulative framing, improving disambiguation among similar statutes, limiting the influence of legally irrelevant attributes, and increasing consistency under benign reformulations. We show that legal trustworthiness requires not only accuracy, but calibrated sensitivity to legally material changes.

</details>


### [21] [MobileExplorer: Accelerating On-Device Inference for Mobile GUI Agents via Online Exploration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26546v1)
*Runxi Huang,Liyu Zhang,Shengzhong Liu,Xiaomin Ouyang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 移动GUI agent，在线探索加速设备端推理，可迁移至coding agent的探索机制

TL;DR: MobileExplorer通过在线探索和两层回滚机制，在端上设备上减少了23%的推理步骤和延迟，并提高了任务成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有移动GUI代理依赖云端推理，存在隐私和延迟问题，且完全端上部署未被充分探索。

Method: 利用VLM的长推理时间进行轻量级并行探索UI元素，记录探索轨迹并注入上下文提示；设计两层回滚机制恢复UI状态。

Result: 在多个设备上评估，平均推理步骤和延迟减少23%，成功率提升高达5%。

Conclusion: MobileExplorer有效加速端上推理并保持或提升了任务性能。

中文摘要：移动图形用户界面（GUI）代理使AI模型能够代表用户自主操作智能手机。然而，大多数现有系统主要侧重于优化任务准确性，并依赖云端模型进行推理，这引入了隐私问题和网络依赖的延迟。因此，完全在设备上部署移动GUI代理仍未得到充分探索。我们提出了MobileExplorer，一种通过在线探索加速基于视觉的移动GUI代理的端上推理的新框架。关键思想是利用视觉语言模型（VLM）的每步长推理时间，通过轻量级并行探索UI元素。在模型推理期间，代理主动探测语义相关的UI元素，并将这些探索轨迹记录为结构化记忆。为了确保在真实移动环境中的可靠执行，我们设计了一个两层回滚机制，当快速但天真的回溯策略失败时，能够稳健地恢复初始UI状态。收集到的探索轨迹随后被总结为简洁的上下文提示，并注入到提示中，以增强后续的推理步骤。我们在使用AndroidWorld基准测试以及新设计的更复杂任务和动态设备环境中的多个现成设备上评估了MobileExplorer。MobileExplorer将平均推理步骤数和端到端延迟减少了23%，同时将任务成功率保持或提高了最多5%。一个展示MobileExplorer在真实世界中表现的视频演示可在https://youtu.be/thK7MJmdlvM获得。

Original abstract: Mobile graphical user interface (GUI) agents enable AI models to autonomously operate smartphones on behalf of users. However, most existing systems focus primarily on optimizing task accuracy and rely on cloud-hosted models for inference, which introduces privacy concerns and network-dependent latency. As a result, fully on-device deployment of mobile GUI agents remains underexplored. We propose MobileExplorer, a new framework that accelerates on-device inference for vision-based mobile GUI agents via online exploration. The key idea is to exploit the long per-step reasoning time of vision-language models (VLMs) by performing lightweight, parallel exploration of UI elements. During model inference, the agent proactively probes semantically relevant UI elements and records these exploration traces as structured memory. To ensure reliable execution in live mobile environments, we design a two-level rollback mechanism that robustly restores the initial UI state when a fast but naive backtracking strategy fails. The collected exploration traces are then summarized into concise contextual hints and injected into the prompt to enhance the subsequent reasoning step. We evaluate MobileExplorer on multiple off-the-shelf devices using the AndroidWorld benchmark, as well as newly designed, more complex tasks and dynamic on-device environments. MobileExplorer reduces the average number of reasoning steps and end-to-end latency by 23\%, while maintaining or improving task success rates by up to 5\%. A video demonstration of MobileExplorer performance in the real world is available at https://youtu.be/thK7MJmdlvM .

</details>


### [22] [AGORA: Adapter-Grounded Observation-Action Retention for Inference-Free Prompt Compression in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26596v1)
*Haoran Zhang,Zhaohua Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM agent提示压缩，避免动作语法破坏，直接提升agent效率

TL;DR: 令牌级压缩器会破坏LLM智能体的动作语法，而提出的步骤级压缩器AGORA在大多数情况下保留了75%以上的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有令牌级抽取式压缩器在LLM智能体场景中失效，导致平均奖励极低，原因是它们错误地移除了承载动作语义的关键令牌。

Method: 提出AGORA，一种无推理的步骤级压缩器，包含结构提示解析器、始终保留关键内容的底线、以及基于反事实标签训练的125M参数相关性评分器。

Result: AGORA在9个测试单元中的8个保留了75%以上的未压缩性能，唯一例外为73%，并实现了1.0-11.5倍的自适应端到端压缩。

Conclusion: 步骤级压缩能够避免动作语法破坏，结构底线是质量的关键，而学习到的评分器提供了自适应压缩能力。

中文摘要：广泛用于通用语言模型上下文的令牌级抽取式压缩器在结构上不适合大语言模型智能体：跨越17个（环境、主干、方法）单元，涵盖两个独立的令牌级方法家族，每个单元的平均奖励都降至<=0.05，尽管实现了1.3-13.3倍的压缩。我们命名并描述这种失败模式为动作语法破坏——承载动作语义的令牌（标识符、括号、动作动词）恰好是那些自信息排名最低的，因此通用压缩器可靠地移除它们，环境拒绝剩余部分。诊断指向步骤粒度压缩。我们引入AGORA，一种无推理的步骤级压缩器，结合了结构化提示解析器、用于格式和时效关键内容的始终保留底线，以及一个基于反事实下一动作变化标签训练的125M参数相关性评分器（约2毫秒/步，无每步大语言模型开销）。在比较的无推理和基于大语言模型的方法中，AGORA是唯一在9个单元中的8个中保留>=75%未压缩性能的方法（唯一例外为73%）；四路组件消融将结构底线隔离为主要的质量杠杆，而学习到的评分器是单个固定保留比下1.0-11.5倍自适应端到端压缩的来源。

Original abstract: The token-level extractive compressors widely used for general LM context are structurally inappropriate for LLM agents: across 17 (env, backbone, method) cells spanning two independent token-level method families, every cell collapses to mean reward <= 0.05 despite 1.3-13.3x realized compression. We name and characterize this failure mode as action-grammar destruction -- the tokens carrying action semantics (identifiers, brackets, action verbs) are exactly those self-information ranks lowest, so a general-purpose compressor reliably removes them and the environment rejects the residual. The diagnosis points to step-granularity compression. We introduce AGORA, an inference-free step-level compressor combining a structural prompt parser, an always-keep floor for format- and recency-critical content, and a 125M-parameter relevance scorer trained on counterfactual next-action-change labels (~2ms/step, zero per-step LLM toll). Across the compared inference-free and LLM-based methods, AGORA is the only one retaining >= 75% uncompressed performance in 8 of 9 cells (with the lone exception at 73%); a four-way component ablation isolates the structural floor as the dominant quality lever and the learned scorer as the source of 1.0-11.5x adaptive end-to-end compression from a single fixed keep ratio.

</details>


### [23] [UnityMAS-O: A General RL Optimization Framework for LLM-Based Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26646v1)
*Yiqun Chen,Wei Yang,Erhan Zhang,Shijie Wang,Qi Liu,Zechun Niu,Bin Zhang,Haitao Li,Rui Li,Lingyong Yan,Jinyuan Feng,Biqing Qi,Xiaochi Wei,Yan Gao,Yi Wu,Yao Hu,Jiaxin Mao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 通用RL优化框架用于LLM多agent系统，直接支持多agent训练与协调

TL;DR: UnityMAS-O是一个通用的强化学习优化框架，将LLM多智能体工作流作为整体优化单元，通过解耦逻辑角色与模型参数、支持多种参数共享和奖励分配，显著提升性能，尤其在小型模型和严格任务上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM多智能体系统多依赖手动编排，缺乏统一的RL优化接口，而现有RL后训练框架仅支持单策略优化，无法满足多智能体工作流的复杂需求。

Method: 提出UnityMAS-O框架，将完整工作流作为优化单元，引入逻辑智能体角色、图轨迹、用户定义奖励和智能体-模型映射四个第一类对象，通过Ray星形拓扑运行时实现分布式PPO优化，支持灵活的共享和奖励分配。

Result: 在检索增强QA、迭代搜索和代码生成任务上，多智能体RL优化显著改进手动指定工作流，特别是在Natural Questions、HotpotQA和代码任务上，小模型和严格指标提升显著。

Conclusion: UnityMAS-O可作为可重用基底，将多种LLM多智能体工作流转化为可训练的RL系统，展现出通用性和有效性。

中文摘要：基于LLM的多智能体系统将复杂任务分解为交互角色，但大多数仍通过提示、工具和控制规则手动编排，而智能体很少通过统一的强化学习接口进行优化。现有的RL后训练框架主要针对单策略优化，缺乏用户自定义多智能体工作流、结构化交互、角色特定信用分配和可配置参数共享的抽象。我们提出了UnityMAS-O，一个用于基于LLM的多智能体系统的通用RL优化框架。UnityMAS-O将完整工作流视为优化单元，而非单一响应或策略轨迹。它通过四个第一类对象表示工作流：逻辑智能体角色、图轨迹、用户定义奖励和智能体-模型映射。这将逻辑智能体与物理模型参数解耦，支持完全共享、完全分离和部分共享，奖励在角色、轮次和轨迹级别分配。UnityMAS-O通过基于Ray的星形拓扑运行时扩展了verl。中央控制器执行工作流、调用工具、记录结构化轨迹并组装奖励；模型本地工作线程组负责展开、缓冲、优势计算和分布式PPO风格更新。用户可以定义智能体、工作流、模型映射和奖励，而无需重写优化基础设施。我们在检索增强的QA、迭代智能体搜索和反射代码生成上实例化了UnityMAS-O。在Natural Questions、HotpotQA和保留代码任务上，多智能体RL优化后改进了手动指定的工作流，特别是对于较小模型和严格代码全部通过指标有较大提升。这些结果表明，UnityMAS-O可作为可重用基底，将多样化的基于LLM的多智能体工作流转化为可训练的多智能体RL系统。

Original abstract: LLM-based multi-agent systems decompose complex tasks into interacting roles, but most remain manually orchestrated by prompts, tools, and control rules, while agents are rarely optimized through a unified reinforcement learning interface. Existing RL post-training frameworks mainly target single-policy optimization and lack abstractions for user-defined multi-agent workflows, structured interaction, role-specific credit assignment, and configurable parameter sharing.
  We present UnityMAS-O, a general RL optimization framework for LLM-based multi-agent systems. UnityMAS-O treats the complete workflow as the optimization unit, rather than a single response or policy trajectory. It represents workflows through four first-class objects: logical agent roles, graph trajectories, user-defined rewards, and agent--model mappings. This decouples logical agents from physical model parameters, supporting full sharing, full separation, and partial sharing, with rewards assigned at role, turn, and trajectory levels.
  UnityMAS-O extends verl with a Ray-based star-topology runtime. A central controller executes workflows, invokes tools, records structured trajectories, and assembles rewards; model-local worker groups handle rollout, buffering, advantage computation, and distributed PPO-style updates. Users can define agents, workflows, model mappings, and rewards without rewriting the optimization infrastructure.
  We instantiate UnityMAS-O on retrieval-augmented QA, iterative agentic search, and reflective code generation. Across Natural Questions, HotpotQA, and held-out code tasks, multi-agent RL improves manually specified workflows after optimization, with especially large gains for smaller models and strict code all-passed metrics. These results show that UnityMAS-O can serve as a reusable substrate for converting diverse LLM-based multi-agent workflows into trainable multi-agent RL systems.

### [24] [MemFail: Stress-Testing Failure Modes of LLM Memory Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26667v1)
*Ishir Garg,Neel Kolhe,Dawn Song,Xuandong Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM记忆系统故障模式诊断基准，对agent记忆设计有直接启发

TL;DR: MemFail是一个诊断性基准测试，通过形式化记忆系统为摘要、存储和检索三个操作并构建对抗性数据集，揭示了不同记忆系统架构的失败模式和权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试将记忆系统视为黑盒，仅报告聚合准确率，无法将错误归因于特定失败模式，因此需要诊断性工具来理解这些系统的失效机制。

Method: 将记忆系统形式化为摘要、存储和检索三个操作，针对每个操作假设的失败模式构建五个对抗性数据集（涵盖四个任务），并在MemFail上评估四个最先进的记忆系统。

Result: 在MemFail上评估了四个最先进的记忆系统，实证展示了不同记忆系统架构如何导致权衡，并识别了各自的失败模式。

Conclusion: MemFail能够有效诊断LLM记忆系统的失败模式，帮助理解架构设计差异带来的权衡，为改进记忆系统提供指导。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）代理越来越依赖外部记忆系统来在长程交互中保持一致，但很少有实证工作来理解这些系统呈现的特定失败模式和设计选择。现有的基准测试报告聚合的问答准确性，并将记忆系统视为黑盒，这使得无法将错误答案归因于系统的特定失败模式。我们引入了MemFail，一个诊断性基准测试，用于隔离现代LLM记忆系统的失败模式。我们首先将记忆系统形式化为三个规范操作——摘要、存储和检索——的组合，并识别每个操作可能引起的失败模式。基于这些假设的失败模式，我们构建了五个数据集，涵盖四个任务，每个数据集都经过对抗性设计，以测试记忆系统的特定操作。使用这些数据集，我们在MemFail上评估了四个最先进的记忆系统，并展示了如何使用MemFail来实证理解记忆系统架构差异所导致的权衡。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents increasingly rely on external memory systems to remain consistent across long-horizon interactions, but little empirical work has been done to understand the specific failure modes and design choices that these systems present. Existing benchmarks report aggregate question-answering accuracy and treat memory systems as black boxes, making it impossible to attribute an incorrect answer to a particular failure mode of the system. We introduce MemFail, a diagnostic benchmark that isolates the failure modes of modern LLM memory systems. We begin by formalizing memory systems as the composition of three canonical operations -- summarization, storage, and retrieval -- and identify the potential failure modes induced by each. Based on these hypothesized failure modes, we construct five datasets spanning four tasks, each adversarially designed to test a specific operation of a memory system. Using these datasets, we evaluate four state-of-the-art memory systems on MemFail and demonstrate how MemFail can be used to empirically understand the tradeoffs induced by differences in memory system architectures.

### [25] [Mind the Tool Failures: Achieving Synergistic Tool Gains for Medical Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26691v1)
*Yunhui Gan,Tan Pan,Kaiyu Guo,Limei Han,Weimiao Yu,Guangnan Ye,Chen Jiang,Yuan Cheng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 医疗agent工具协同与GRPO强化学习，实例级工具选择方法具通用性

TL;DR: 提出一种基于GRPO的强化学习框架，通过实例级工具选择纠正单个工具失败，利用分歧感知协同学习和熵引导采样提升医疗AI代理的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有医疗AI代理假设工具可靠，但实际中工具可能失败，导致不安全决策。需要实例级的工具选择来弥补单一工具性能差距。

Method: 基于GRPO的强化学习框架，包含概率风险最小化奖励和分歧感知协同学习；采用熵引导采样加重高分歧实例权重，促进实例级工具协同。

Result: 在两个任务和七个医疗基准上，该方法比多种基线方法获得更稳健和稳定的性能提升。

Conclusion: 协同感知的实例级工具选择对构建可靠的医疗AI代理系统至关重要。

中文摘要：医疗AI代理越来越多地使用外部工具进行诊断、治疗建议和证据检索，然而大多数现有方法假设任务适恰的工具在其预期范围内是可靠的。这一假设在真实临床场景中很脆弱，因为即使相关工具也可能在具有挑战性的实例上失败，并导致不安全的后续决策。为解决此问题，我们研究了不完美工具设置下的医疗工具使用，以纠正单个工具遗漏的失败实例。实例相关的失败模式造成了最佳固定单一工具与理想实例级选择器之间的差距，我们将其称为单一Oracle风险差距。核心挑战在于，传统的任务级工具选择无法实现这一差距，因为它本质上受限于最佳单一工具的性能。基于这一观察，我们考虑实例级异质性，并将工具使用表述为实例级选择问题。具体而言，我们提出了一种基于GRPO的强化学习框架，其奖励用于概率风险最小化和分歧感知协同学习，从而促进对错误工具共识的实例级纠正。此外，采用熵引导采样策略来加重高分歧实例的权重，这些实例为学习实例特定的工具协同提供了更强的信号。这两个组件相辅相成，以缓解实例级异质性并改善工具协同。在两个任务和七个医疗基准上的实验表明，我们的方法在广泛的基线上持续实现了稳健且稳定的改进，突显了协同感知工具使用对于可靠的医疗代理系统的重要性。

Original abstract: Medical AI agents increasingly use external tools for diagnosis, treatment recommendation, and evidence retrieval, yet most existing approaches assume that task-appropriate tools are reliable within their intended scope. This assumption is fragile in real clinical settings, where even relevant tools may fail on challenging instances and lead to unsafe downstream decisions. To address this issue, we study medical tool use under imperfect-tool settings to correct failure instances missed by individual tools. Instance-dependent failure patterns create a gap between the best fixed single tool and an ideal instance-wise selector, which we refer to as the Single-Oracle risk gap. The core challenge is that conventional task-level tool selection cannot realize this gap, as it is inherently bounded by the performance of the best single tool. Motivated by this observation, we therefore account for instance-level heterogeneity and formulate tool use as an instance-level selection problem. Particularly, we propose a GRPO-based reinforcement learning framework with rewards for probabilistic risk minimization and disagreement-aware synergy learning, which promotes instance-level correction of erroneous tool consensus. Furthermore, an entropy-guided sampling strategy is adopted to upweight high-disagreement instances, which provide stronger signals for learning instance-specific tool synergy. These two components complement each other in mitigating instance-level heterogeneity and improving tool synergy. Experiments on two tasks and seven medical benchmarks show that our method consistently achieves robust and stable improvements over a broad range of baselines, highlighting the importance of synergy-aware tool use for reliable medical agentic systems.

### [26] [Towards Feedback-to-Plan Decisions for Self-Evolving LLM Agents in CUDA Kernel Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26720v1)
*Yee Hin Chong,Jiaming Wu,Youhui Zhang,Peng Qu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接研究LLM agent在CUDA kernel生成中的反馈与规划，与自动代码优化高度相关。

TL;DR: CUDAnalyst通过轨迹冻结和选择性反馈注入，揭示了LLM在CUDA内核生成中规划决策与异质反馈信号的因果归因关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法无法分离迭代规划中不同反馈成分的贡献，因为端到端消融会混淆反馈效应和轨迹漂移。

Method: 提出CUDAnalyst，通过轨迹冻结（冻结规划路径）和选择性反馈注入，在生成级别对反馈进行受控归因分析。

Result: 显式规划仅在反馈对齐时有效；有效规划来自结构化多反馈交互；高级规划可部分从强模型迁移到弱模型；这些趋势在多种设置下鲁棒。

Conclusion: CUDAnalyst提供了一种受控的方法来解析反馈到规划的结构，揭示了反馈对齐和交互的重要性，并表明规划知识可迁移。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）在作为自我进化的CUDA内核生成智能体方面展现出强大的实证增益，这得益于跨代的条件反馈规划。然而，规划决策如何归因并组合异质反馈信号仍然是模糊的。标准的端到端消融研究无法解决这个问题，因为迭代规划放大了早期扰动并将反馈效应与轨迹依赖漂移混为一谈。我们引入了CUDAnalyst，一种统一的分析层，通过轨迹冻结和选择性反馈注入实现对规划决策归因于反馈组件的受控、生成级归因。CUDAnalyst能够实现稳定的生成级评估和原则性的联盟式归因，用于反馈效应及其交互。我们的结果表明，显式规划仅在反馈对齐时有益，有效的规划源于结构化的多反馈交互，且来自更强推理模型的高级规划可以部分迁移到较弱模型。这些趋势在参考骨干网络、代表性工作负载和参考归纳机制中保持一致，表明在受控轴内，识别出的反馈到规划结构是鲁棒的。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown strong empirical gains as self-evolving agents for CUDA kernel generation, driven by feedback-conditioned planning across generations. However, how planning decisions attribute and combine heterogeneous feedback signals remains opaque. Standard end-to-end ablations fail to resolve this question, as iterative planning amplifies early perturbations and conflates feedback effects with trajectory-dependent drift.
  We introduce \texttt{CUDAnalyst}, a unified analysis layer for controlled, generation-level attribution of planning decisions to feedback components via trajectory freezing and selective feedback injection. \texttt{CUDAnalyst} enables stable generation-level evaluation and principled coalitional-style attribution of feedback effects and interactions. Our results show that explicit planning is beneficial only when feedback is aligned, that effective planning emerges from structured multi-feedback interactions, and that high-level plans from stronger reasoning models can partially transfer to weaker ones. These trends hold across reference backbones, representative workloads, and reference induction regimes, indicating that the identified feedback-to-plan structure is robust within the controlled axes studied.

### [27] [It's Not the Capability: Harness Sensitivity Is Non-Monotone Across LLM Agent Tiers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26731v1)
*Yong-eun Cho*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究LLM agent的harness敏感性，提供agent可靠性与失效分析，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 通过432次受控实验，发现LLM代理部署中模型能力与最优约束复杂度之间并非单调反比关系，存在约束复杂度悖论，且约束敏感性取决于模型类型（聊天 vs. 推理），并提出了失败分类法和层级感知约束选择指南。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战和检验LLM代理部署中普遍假设：更结构化约束提高可靠性，且高能力模型需要更少约束，即模型能力与最优约束复杂度间存在单调反比关系。

Method: 在HEAT-24基准上，对6个模型（4个能力层级）进行432次受控实验，使用3种约束条件（轻度、平衡、严格），测量VTSR和延迟，并分析失败类型。

Result: 反驳了单调反比关系：聊天模型（Gemini 2.5 Flash）中增加约束降低VTSR 29-38个百分点（约束复杂度悖论）；推理模型（Qwen3.5-122B）严格约束下VTSR最高（91.7%）且延迟最低；2B模型（Gemma4:e2B）在所有约束下达到91.7% VTSR；失败类型中格式违规主导高能力模型，错误文件主导低能力模型。

Conclusion: 约束敏感性非单调且依赖模型类型（聊天 vs. 推理）；不能简单假设高能力模型需要更少约束；需要根据模型层级和类型选择约束策略，并提出了层级感知约束选择指南。

中文摘要：在LLM代理部署中，一个普遍的假设是，更结构化的约束普遍能提高可靠性，并且更高能力的模型需要比例更少的结构性指导——这共同暗示模型能力层级与最优约束复杂度之间存在单调反比关系。我们通过一项受控的432次实验来检验这一假设，实验跨越了四个能力层级的六个模型，在HEAT-24（一个包含24个基于git的工作区验证的合成基准任务）上采用了三种约束条件（轻度、平衡、严格）。我们的结果在两个方面驳斥了单调反比关系。首先，对于评估的前沿聊天模型（Gemini 2.5 Flash），增加约束的详细程度使VTSR降低了29-38个百分点——这是一个约束复杂度悖论。其次，对于评估的前沿推理模型（Qwen3.5-122B，启用扩展思考），严格约束实现了最高的VTSR（91.7%）和最低的延迟，与预测相反。在受限层级内，一个2B模型（Gemma4:e2B）在所有约束条件下以91.7%的VTSR匹配了强开放层级的稳定性。由于本研究中的每个层级仅由一个模型代表，这些结果应被视为特定模型的观察结果；约束敏感性似乎在评估的模型中是非单调的，并且关键取决于模型类型（聊天 vs. 推理）。我们引入了一个六标签失败分类法，显示格式违规主导了高能力模型的失败，而错误文件主导了低能力模型的失败，并且我们推导出了实用的层级感知约束选择指南。

Original abstract: A prevalent assumption in LLM agent deployment holds that more structured harnesses universally improve
  reliability, and that higher-capability models need proportionally less structural guidance -- together
  implying a monotone inverse relationship between model capability tier and optimal harness complexity. We
  test this hypothesis through a controlled 432-run experiment crossing six models across four capability
  tiers with three harness conditions (light, balanced, strict) on HEAT-24, a 24-task synthetic benchmark
  with git-based workspace verification. Our results refute the monotone inverse relationship on two
  fronts. First, for the frontier chat model evaluated (Gemini 2.5 Flash), increased harness verbosity
  lowers VTSR by 29-38 percentage points -- a harness-complexity paradox. Second, for the frontier
  reasoning model evaluated (Qwen3.5-122B, extended thinking enabled), strict harness achieves the highest
  VTSR (91.7%) and the lowest latency, the opposite of the prediction. Within the constrained tier, a 2B
  model (Gemma4:e2B) matches strong-open-tier stability at 91.7% across all harnesses. Because each tier is
  represented by a single model in this study, these results should be interpreted as model-specific
  observations; harness sensitivity appears non-monotone across the models evaluated, and depends
  critically on model type (chat vs. reasoning). We introduce a six-label failure taxonomy showing that
  format_violation dominates capable-model failures while wrong_file dominates low-capability failures, and
  we derive practical tier-aware harness selection guidelines.

</details>


### [28] [Evaluating Interactive Reasoning in Large Language Models: A Hierarchical Benchmark with Executable Games](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00103v1)
*Mingyuan Fan,Weiguang Han,Daixin Wang,Cen Chen,Zhiqiang Zhang,Jun Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多轮交互推理评测框架，涉及主动查询与信念更新，对agent评测有启发。

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个多轮交互推理评估框架，通过主动证据获取和信念更新来评估LLM，并构建了包含474个游戏的基准测试，揭示了模型在成功率和效率上的差异以及不同因素对性能的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理评估方法多依赖静态问答，缺乏对主动证据获取和信念更新过程的评估，以及鲁棒性和元认知适应能力的考察。

Method: 构建多轮交互框架，LLM需主动查询隐藏环境并整合信息，评估标准包括成功率、效率、上下文鲁棒性和元认知适应，并开发了474个游戏的基准测试。

Result: 基准测试具有高度区分性，揭示了模型在成功率和效率上的显著差异；上下文扰动导致中等持续下降，反事实修正和必要性判断导致更大下降。

Conclusion: 提出的框架和基准测试能有效评估LLM的主动推理能力，并揭示不同因素对性能的影响。

中文摘要：我们提出了一种用于推理评估的多轮交互框架，将推理视为主动的证据获取和信念更新。其中，LLMs仅接收任务规则，必须向隐藏环境发出有针对性的查询，随时间整合部分观察结果，并决定何时提交最终答案。除了标准成功率和交互效率外，我们还在受控上下文扰动下评估上下文鲁棒性，并通过反事实修正和必要性判断评估元认知适应。我们将该框架实例化为一个包含474个可执行游戏的基准测试，每个游戏在五个固定配置搜索空间下进行评估，对应五个难度级别，并评估了一系列前沿LLM。结果表明，该基准测试具有高度区分性，不仅揭示了成功率的巨大差异，还揭示了交互效率的巨大差异。此外，我们实证表明，上下文扰动会导致中等但持续的下降，而反事实修正和必要性判断则导致更大的下降。

Original abstract: We introduce a multi-turn interactive framework for reasoning evaluation that treats reasoning as active evidence acquisition and belief updating. Wherein, LLMs receive only the task rules, must issue targeted queries to a hidden environment, integrate partial observations over time, and decide when to submit a final answer. Beyond standard success rate and interaction efficiency, we evaluate contextual robustness under controlled contextual perturbations, and metacognitive adaptation through counterfactual revision and necessity judgment. We instantiate the framework as a benchmark of 474 executable games, each evaluated under five fixed configuration search spaces corresponding to five difficulty levels, and evaluate a broad set of frontier LLMs. Results show that the benchmark is highly discriminative, exposing large differences not only in success rate but also in interaction efficiency. Moreover, we empirically show that contextual perturbations cause moderate but consistent declines, whereas counterfactual revision and necessity judgment lead to much larger drops.

### [29] [Beyond a Single Direction: Chain-of-Thought Disrupts Simple Steering of Refusal](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26772v1)
*Kia-Jüng Yang,Dominik Meier,Jiachen Zhao,Terry Ruas,Bela Gipp*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究链式思维对LLM拒绝行为的控制影响，对agent安全与干预有启发。

TL;DR: 大型推理模型的拒绝行为由残差流激活和思维链共同编码，激活引导仅部分有效，而通过重新生成思维链可大幅提升拒绝反转效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索大型推理模型中拒绝行为的机制，尤其是思维链的作用及其对控制干预的影响。

Method: 在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-LLaMA-8B上，通过固定CoT、移除CoT以及两阶段干预（激活引导下重新生成CoT）进行实验，比较拒绝反转率。

Result: 固定CoT时激活引导反转拒绝39%，移除CoT后升至70%，两阶段干预达到94%，且生成的CoT单独保留48%效果。

Conclusion: LRMs的拒绝由残差流激活和CoT共同编码，这种联合编码增强了对激活层面干预的鲁棒性，但CoT成为新的攻击面。

中文摘要：大型推理模型（LRMs）在生成最终输出之前会产生思维链（CoT）轨迹，引入了一种可能使拒绝等控制机制复杂化的动态内部状态。与指令微调的LLMs不同，后者的拒绝由单个方向子空间介导，而大型推理模型（LRMs）的拒绝还依赖于CoT。在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-LLaMA-8B中，当CoT保持固定时，激活引导仅在39%的情况下逆转拒绝，但完全移除CoT后，这一比例增加到70%，表明CoT积极地强化了拒绝。在一个两阶段干预中，模型在激活引导下重新生成其CoT，拒绝在94%的情况下被逆转，而即使在移除引导后，生成的CoT本身仍保留了48%的效果。这表明CoT可以独立携带并重建顺从信号。这些发现表明，LRMs中的拒绝是由残差流激活和CoT共同编码的。这种联合编码使得LRMs对仅激活层干预更具鲁棒性，但使CoT面临可能的替代表面攻击。

Original abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) generate chain-of-thought (CoT) traces before producing final outputs, introducing a dynamic internal state that may complicate control mechanisms such as refusal. Unlike instruction-tuned LLMs, where refusal is mediated by a single directional subspace, refusal in large reasoning models (LRMs) additionally depends on the CoT. In DeepSeek-R1-Distill-LLaMA-8B, activation steering reverses refusal in only 39% of cases when the CoT is kept fixed, but removing the CoT entirely increases this to 70%, indicating that the CoT actively reinforces refusal. In a two-stage intervention where the model regenerates its CoT under activation steering, refusal is reversed in 94% of cases, while the resulting CoT alone retains 48% of this effect even after steering is removed. This suggests that the CoT can carry and reconstruct the compliance signal independently. These findings indicate that refusal in LRMs is jointly encoded in residual stream activations and CoT. This joint activation makes LRM more robust against activation-level interventions alone, but exposes CoT to a possible alternative surface attack.
