### [30] [The Attribution Blind Spot: Detecting When Language Models Rely on Memory Rather Than Retrieved Context](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26778v1)
*Zhe Yu,Wenpeng Xing,Yunzhao Wei,Bo Yang,Chen Ye,Gaolei Li,Meng Han*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 检测LLM依赖记忆还是检索上下文，对RAG agent的归因与可靠性有贡献。

TL;DR: 提出计算现实监控（CRM）方法，通过比较有无上下文时的内部表示来检测预训练暴露的轨迹，解决检索增强生成中无法验证检索上下文是否真正主导生成的归因盲点问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检索增强生成缺乏可靠方法验证检索上下文是否真正主导生成，尤其当文档与预训练数据重叠时，标准假设失效，导致归因盲点。

Method: 借鉴认知科学现实监控框架，通过比较有无上下文时的内部表示差异，检测预训练暴露是否留下可测量的内部轨迹信号，从而诊断输出级监控无法察觉的归因盲点。

Result: 在9个模型变体上，差异集中在特定架构的层模式，块级噪声干预提供汇聚支持，且差异在任务和数据集上泛化，但在领域混淆的基准上消失。

Conclusion: 归因盲点可测量且部分可解决：内部表示携带输出级不可见的诊断信号，为构建内部感知证据来源的系统奠定基础。

中文摘要：检索增强生成有望将语言模型输出锚定于外部证据，但该领域缺乏可靠的方法来验证检索到的上下文是否真正主导了生成——这是高风险部署的先决条件。标准假设——上下文一致的输出意味着上下文主导的输出——在检索到的文档与模型预训练数据重叠时失效：模型可以完全从参数记忆中生成看似忠实的文本，而两种路径产生的输出无法区分。我们将此失败称为归因盲点，并引入计算现实监控（CRM）来解决它。CRM 实现了改编自认知科学现实监控框架的原则：比较有无上下文时的内部表示，揭示了输出级监控系统性地遗漏的基于成员条件的表示差异。CRM 不证明单个生成使用了哪个来源；它检测预训练暴露是否留下了可测量的内部轨迹信号，为来源归因建立了必要的基底。在跨越三个家族的九个模型变体上，这种差异集中在特定架构的层模式中，得到块级噪声干预的汇聚支持，并在任务和数据集上泛化，同时在领域混淆的基准上消失。归因盲点是可测量且部分可解决的：内部表示携带了输出级不可见的诊断信号，为那些内部意识到证据来源的系统建立基础，从而控制其外部行为。

Original abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation promises to ground language model outputs in external evidence, yet the field has no reliable way to verify whether retrieved context actually governs generation -- a prerequisite for any high-stakes deployment. The standard assumption, that context-consistent output implies context-governed output, breaks when the retrieved document overlaps with the model's pretraining data: the model can produce faithful-looking text entirely from parametric memory, and both pathways yield indistinguishable output. We name this failure the attribution blind spot and introduce Computational Reality Monitoring (CRM) to address it. CRM operationalizes a principle adapted from cognitive science's reality monitoring framework: comparing internal representations with and without context reveals membership-conditioned representational divergence that output-level monitors systematically miss. CRM does not certify which source an individual generation used; it detects whether pretraining exposure leaves a measurable internal trajectory signature, establishing a necessary substrate for source attribution. Across nine model variants spanning three families, this divergence concentrates in architecture-specific layer patterns, receives converging support from block-level noise intervention, and generalizes across tasks and datasets while collapsing on domain-confounded benchmarks. The attribution blind spot is measurable and partially addressable: internal representations carry a diagnostic signal invisible at the output level, establishing a foundation for systems whose internal awareness of evidence provenance governs their external behavior.

</details>


### [31] [What Makes Chain-of-Thought Work at Probe Time? Local Co-occurrence Rather Than Global Derivation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26795v1)
*Xiang Wang,Wei Wei*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究CoT工作原理，发现局部共现效应，对agent推理解释有参考价值。

TL;DR: CoT提示的增益主要来自词汇激活和短距离标记共现，而非句子级逻辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究CoT提示中推理文本的哪些属性驱动了准确性提升，因为之前主要研究生成时行为，而测试时影响未知。

Method: 通过固定推理文本并改变其结构（打乱词序、保留短窗口等）进行实验，分析不同条件下的性能变化。

Result: 词序打乱仍有显著增益；保留2-3个标记的连续窗口可恢复大部分增益；排除复制答案等解释；模式跨模型和数据集稳定。

Conclusion: 支持局部共现激活（LCA）解释。

中文摘要：链式思维（CoT）提示能可靠地提高语言模型的准确性，但推理文本的哪些属性驱动了这种改进尚不清楚。先前的工作主要研究了生成时的行为。我们转而提出一个测试时的问题：给定上下文中一个固定的推理文本，该文本中的什么改变了答案？我们识别出两个互补的增益来源。首先，即使是全局词序打乱的推理文本也显著优于无推理基线，表明存在强烈的词汇激活效应。更重要的是，来自结构化文本的额外增益似乎较少来自句子级别的逻辑顺序，而更多来自短距离的标记邻接。仅保留连续窗口长度为n*=2-3个标记就能恢复向完整CoT性能的大部分剩余增益。支持性实验排除了复制显式答案声明或答案值，以及完整的语法实现作为主要驱动因素。进一步的泛化实验表明，这种定性模式在多个模型家族、参数规模和数据集上保持稳定。这些结果支持了测试时CoT的局部共现激活（LCA）解释，其中观察到的增益主要来自词汇激活和短距离标记共现，而非句子级别的逻辑推导。

Original abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) prompting reliably improves language-model accuracy, but which properties of a rationale text drive the improvement is poorly understood. Prior work has largely studied generation-time behavior. We instead ask a probe-time question: given a fixed rationale in context, what in that text changes the answer? We identify two complementary sources of the gain. First, even a globally word-shuffled rationale substantially outperforms the no-rationale baseline, indicating a strong lexical activation effect. More importantly, the additional gain from structured text appears to arise less from sentence-level logical ordering and more from short-range token adjacency. Preserving contiguous windows of just $n^\star{=}2$--$3$ tokens recovers most of the remaining gain toward full CoT performance. Supporting experiments rule out copying of explicit answer declarations or answer values, as well as full grammatical realization, as primary drivers. Further generalization experiments show that the qualitative pattern remains stable across multiple model families, parameter scales, and datasets. These results support a local co-occurrence activation (LCA) account of probe-time CoT, in which the observed gains appear to arise primarily from lexical activation and short-range token co-occurrence rather than sentence-level logical derivation.

</details>


### [32] [Helicase: Uncertainty-Guided Supply Chain Knowledge Graph Construction with Autonomous Multi-Agent LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26835v1)
*Yunbo Long,Haolang Zhao,Ge Zheng,Alexandra Brintrup*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent LLM系统用于知识图谱构建，包含规划、验证、不确定性追踪，通用方法。

TL;DR: 提出Helicase，一种用于供应链知识图谱构建的自主多智能体LLM系统，通过三层不确定性框架支持多跳结构推理和校准置信度评估，并引入SCQA基准进行评测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM多智能体系统无法处理供应链中的多跳结构推理问题，且缺乏不确定性感知，无法提供可追溯的置信度评估。

Method: Helicase将高级查询分解为调查计划，通过迭代验证循环协调搜索、推理和编码智能体，逐步构建带有事实不确定性注释的知识图谱，并采用三层不确定性框架（行动、轨迹、记忆层）跟踪不确定性。

Result: 提出SCQA基准，包含80个覆盖四种复杂度象限（单/多跳、高/低数据可见性）的供应链查询。

Conclusion: Helicase能够有效进行不确定性引导的供应链知识图谱构建，实现多跳推理和校准置信度评估，填补了现有系统的能力缺口。

中文摘要：基于LLM的多智能体系统已被广泛用于知识检索和报告生成，通过网页搜索和文本推理综合已知信息。然而，供应链中的许多关键信息任务并非简单的单次查询：它们是结构推理问题，需要在复杂、碎片化的网络资源上进行多跳推理。诸如“特斯拉的哪些组件使用了来自澳大利亚矿山的锂？”之类的问题在任何单个文档中都没有答案；必须通过从碎片化、异构来源中自主构建和分析动态知识图谱来以计算方式综合答案。此外，此类发现过程必须具有不确定性意识：决策不仅取决于答案，还取决于对其可靠性的校准置信度，该置信度可追溯到来源质量和推理一致性。为了解决这一能力差距，我们提出了Helicase，一个用于不确定性引导的供应链知识图谱构建的自主多智能体LLM系统。Helicase将高级供应链查询分解为可执行的调查计划，通过迭代验证循环协调专门的网络搜索、推理和编码智能体，并逐步构建带有每个事实不确定性注释的查询特定供应链知识图谱。其三层次不确定性框架在行动、轨迹和记忆层跟踪不确定性，从而支持结构推理和校准置信度评估。为了评估完整复杂性谱上的自主推理，我们引入了SCQA（供应链查询评估），一个由80个供应链查询组成的基准，分为四个象限，涵盖了在高低数据可见性下的单跳到多跳推理。

Original abstract: LLM-based multi-agent systems have been widely adopted for knowledge retrieval and report generation, synthesizing known information through web search and textual reasoning. However, many critical information tasks in supply chains are not simple one-shot queries: they are structural inference problems requiring multi-hop reasoning across complex, fragmented web resources. Questions such as \textit{``Which Tesla components use lithium from Australian mines?''} have no answer in any single document; answers must be computationally synthesized through the autonomous construction and analysis of dynamic knowledge graphs assembled from fragmented, heterogeneous sources. Moreover, such discovery processes must be uncertainty-aware: decisions depend not only on answers but on calibrated confidence in their reliability, traceable to source quality and reasoning consistency. To address this capability gap, we propose \textit{Helicase}, an autonomous multi-agent LLM system for uncertainty-guided supply chain knowledge graph construction. \textit{Helicase} decomposes high-level supply-chain queries into executable investigation plans, coordinates specialized web-search, reasoning, and coding agents through iterative verification loops, and incrementally constructs query-specific supply chain knowledge graphs with per-fact uncertainty annotations. Its three-layer uncertainty framework tracks uncertainty at the action, trajectory, and memory layers, enabling both structural inference and calibrated confidence assessment. To evaluate autonomous reasoning across the full complexity spectrum, we introduce SCQA (Supply Chain Query Assessment), a benchmark of 80 supply chain queries organized into four quadrants spanning single-hop to multi-hop inference under both high and low data visibility.

</details>


### [33] [TADDLE: A Tool-Augmented Agent for Detecting Deficient LLM-Generated Peer Reviews](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26911v1)
*Hanqi Duan,Xiang Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 工具增强agent检测LLM评论缺陷，直接coding agent方法

TL;DR: 提出TADDLE系统，用于检测LLM生成同行评审中的缺陷，包含专家标注基准和工具增强型代理方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法无法在个体缺陷类型层面检测LLM生成评审的缺陷，缺乏细粒度检测能力。

Method: TADDLE将检测分解为Verify、Correct、Complete、Transform四个专用分析工具，由代理协调，并通过两阶段半监督学习集成输出进行二元和多标签分类。

Result: 在二元检测和多标签分类任务上均表现强劲。

Conclusion: TADDLE能有效检测LLM生成评审中的缺陷，并提供了首个基准和开源代码。

中文摘要：LLM生成的同行评审在主要会议中越来越常见，但由于它们通常流畅且结构良好，其缺陷难以检测。现有工作要么分类作者身份而不评判质量，要么使用为人类编写的评审设计的特征来评分质量；没有现有系统能够在单个缺陷类型层面检测LLM生成评审中的缺陷。为了填补这一空白，我们引入了TADDLE，一种用于检测有缺陷的LLM生成同行评审的工具增强型代理，以及首个用于此任务的专家标注基准。我们的基准包括对50篇ICLR 2025论文的1800条评审，由18位领域专家根据六种缺陷类别（加上非缺陷标签）进行多标签标注。TADDLE将检测分解为四个专门的分析工具——验证、纠正、完成和转换——由一个代理协调；一个集成器通过两阶段半监督学习将它们的输出综合为二元和多标签分类。大量实验表明，TADDLE在二元检测和多标签分类任务上都表现强劲。我们将在https://github.com/AquariusAQ/TADDLE发布基准和代码。

Original abstract: LLM-generated peer reviews are increasingly common at major venues, yet their deficiencies are hard to detect because they are uniformly fluent and well-structured. Existing work either classifies authorship without judging quality, or scores quality with features designed for human-written reviews; no prior system detects deficiencies in LLM-generated reviews at the level of individual defect types. To bridge the gap, we introduce TADDLE, a Tool-Augmented Agent for Detecting Deficient LLM-Generated Peer Reviews, together with the first expert-annotated benchmark for this task. Our benchmark comprises 1,800 reviews on 50 ICLR 2025 papers, multi-label-annotated by 18 domain experts against a taxonomy of six defect categories (plus a non-deficient label). TADDLE decomposes detection into four specialized analysis tools -- Verify, Correct, Complete, and Transform -- orchestrated by an agent; an integrator synthesizes their outputs into binary and multi-label classifications via two-stage semi-supervised learning. Extensive experiments show that TADDLE performs strongly on both binary detection and the multi-label classification task. We release the benchmark and code at https://github.com/AquariusAQ/TADDLE.

</details>


### [34] [From Norms to Indicators (N2I-RAG): An Agentic Retrieval-Augmented Generation Framework for Legal Indicator Computation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26926v1)
*Youssef Al Mouatamid,Marie Bonnin,Jihad Zahir*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: Agentic RAG框架，可迁移至通用agent架构设计

TL;DR: N2I-RAG是一个基于智能体的检索增强生成框架，用于从法律文本中自动计算可追溯的法律指标，在法国海洋环境法数据集上表现优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有NLP和生成模型在计算法律指标时存在高幻觉风险、缺乏可解释性和证据基础，需要一种透明、可追溯的自动化方法。

Method: 提出N2I-RAG，集成自适应检索、LLM智能体和验证机制的模块化流水线，每个组件负责过滤、检索、评估证据并生成带法律条款引用的二元结果，强调中间和最终决策的显式解释。

Result: 在自建法国海洋环境法语料库上，与多个LLM家族对比，N2I-RAG始终优于基线，并在两个不同禁令测试中表现良好泛化性。

Conclusion: 智能体检索增强生成能弥合开放式法律语言与标准化指标计算的差距，为建立透明、可扩展的法律观测站提供基础。

中文摘要：从规范性文本中计算法律指标是法律监测和政策评估中的一项关键任务，但由于法律语言的复杂性、规模、解释性以及可用文档质量的可变性，这面临着重大挑战。现有的自然语言处理技术和生成模型可以协助法律分析，但常常存在较高的幻觉风险，并且缺乏可靠指标计算所需的可解释性和证据基础。本文提出了N2I-RAG（从规范到指标），这是一个基于智能体的检索增强生成框架，旨在以透明和可追溯的方式自动化法律指标的计算。我们在一个模块化流水线中集成了自适应检索、基于大语言模型的智能体和验证机制，其中每个组件在过滤、检索和评估证据，以及生成与可识别的法律条款相关的二元法律结果方面执行明确的角色。该框架通过要求对中间决策和最终指标分配进行明确解释来强调可追溯性。我们使用内部构建的法国海洋环境法语料库（包括扫描件和数字来源）对N2I-RAG进行了评估。与多个语言模型家族的对比实验表明，所提出的方法始终优于基线系统，并且在两个不同禁令的测试上具有良好的泛化能力。结果表明，基于智能体的检索增强生成可以弥合开放式法律语言与标准化指标计算之间的差距，为透明且可扩展的法律观测站奠定了基础。

Original abstract: Computing legal indicators from normative texts is a key task in legal monitoring and policy evaluation, but presents significant challenges due to the complexity, scale, and interpretive nature of legal language, as well as the variability in available document quality. Existing natural language processing techniques and generative models can assist in legal analysis, but often suffer from high risk of hallucinations and lack the interpretability and evidence grounding required for reliable indicator computation. This paper presents N2I-RAG (From Norms to Indicators), an agentic retrieval-augmented generation framework designed to automate the computation of legal indicators in a transparent and traceable way. We integrate adaptive retrieval, llm-based agents, and validation mechanisms in a modular pipeline, where each component performs a defined role in filtering, retrieving, and assessing evidence, and in producing binary legal outcomes linked to identifiable legal provisions. The framework emphasizes traceability by requiring explicit explanations of intermediate decisions and final indicator assignments. We evaluate N2I-RAG using an in-house constructed French marine environmental law corpus that includes both scanned and digital sources. Comparative experiments with multiple language model families demonstrate that the proposed approach consistently outperforms baseline systems, and generalizes well when tested on 2 different bans. The results indicate that agentic retrieval-augmented generation can bridge open-text legal language and standardized indicator computation, offering a foundation for transparent and scalable legal observatories.

### [35] [Neuro-Symbolic Verification of LLM Outputs for Data-Sensitive Domains (extended preprint)](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26942v2)
*Paul Sigloch,Christoph Benzmüller*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出混合验证架构（形式化+神经语义）解决LLM可靠性问题，在医疗设备报告系统中实现高检测率和效率提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在高风险领域存在幻觉、不一致性和隐私漏洞，现有基于提示的自我验证方法继承了分布偏差，无法提供可靠保证。

Method: 采用混合验证架构：输入验证使用形式逻辑推理提供可判定保证，输出验证通过嵌入语义相似度检测上下文幻觉；并行actor流水线实现分离。

Result: 在HAIMEDA系统中，结构化实体幻觉检测率>83%，语义编造检测率72%，报告创建时间减少30%。

Conclusion: 神经符号架构能够为LLM在数据敏感领域提供原则性的安全保障，平衡可靠性与效率。

中文摘要：部署在高风险领域的LLM面临根本性的可靠性挑战：幻觉、不一致性和隐私漏洞带来了不可接受的风险，在这些领域错误会带来法律、财务或安全后果。本文提出了一种混合验证架构，结合形式化符号方法和神经语义分析，为LLM生成的内容提供互补的保证。该架构采用逻辑推理进行输入验证，利用完备性属性为结构化需求提供可判定的保证。在输出验证方面，基于嵌入的语义相似度检测形式化方法缺乏表达力的上下文幻觉。这种分离通过并行的、基于角色的流水线实现，解决了基于提示的自我验证方法的局限性，后者继承了产生幻觉的分布偏差。所提出的架构和类型感知验证方法通过HAIMEDA（一个通过行动设计研究开发的真实世界医疗设备损坏评估报告系统）进行了验证。评估显示，结构化实体的幻觉检测率超过83%，语义编造的检测率为72%，报告创建时间减少了30%，这表明神经符号架构可以为LLM在高敏感数据领域的部署提供有原则的安全保障。

Original abstract: LLMs deployed in high-stakes domains face fundamental reliability challenges: hallucinations, inconsistencies, and privacy vulnerabilities introduce unacceptable risks where errors carry legal, financial, or safety consequences. This paper presents a hybrid verification architecture combining formal symbolic methods with neural semantic analysis to provide complementary guarantees for LLM-generated content. This architecture employs logical reasoning for input verification, leveraging completeness properties to provide decidable guarantees on structured requirements. For output validation, embedding-based semantic similarity detects contextual hallucinations where formal methods lack expressiveness. This separation is realized in a parallel, actor-based pipeline, addressing limitations of prompt-based self-verification approaches, which inherit the distributional biases that produce hallucinations. The proposed architecture and type-aware verification method are validated with HAIMEDA, a real-world medical device damage assessment reporting system developed through Action Design Research. Evaluation shows hallucination detection rates of over 83% for structured entities and 72% for semantic fabrications, with a 30% reduction in report creation time, demonstrating that neuro-symbolic architectures can provide principled safeguards for LLM deployment in data-sensitive domains.

</details>


### [36] [PEAR: Permutation-Equivariant Adaptive Routing Multi-Agent Debate](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20621v1)
*Yang Feng,Ziwei Xu,Xia Hu,Fengxiang He*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出置换等变自适应路由多智能体辩论方法，通用多智能体协作策略，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出PEAR，一种动态重配置通信角色和稀疏拓扑的多智能体辩论协议，通过置换等变路由提升LLM推理可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固定拓扑的多智能体辩论存在位置偏差、放大不可靠智能体、对角色分配敏感等问题。

Method: PEAR在推理时动态切换智能体-角色分配，基于演化状态调整稀疏拓扑，实现置换等变稀疏路由。

Result: 在四个推理基准和六个LLM主干上，PEAR显著提升了平均准确率，超越最强基线。

Conclusion: PEAR通过动态路由和等变性设计有效克服了固定拓扑的缺陷，提升了多智能体辩论的鲁棒性和性能。

中文摘要：多智能体辩论通过迭代的同行评审提高了大型语言模型（LLM）的可靠性。然而，固定的拓扑结构常常引入持续的位置偏差，放大不可靠的智能体，并导致对角色分配的高度敏感。我们引入了	extit{置换等变自适应路由多智能体辩论（PEAR）}，这是一种推理时协议，在连续的辩论轮次中动态重新配置通信角色和稀疏拓扑。通过基于演化的智能体状态策略性地切换智能体到角色的分配，PEAR防止任何智能体永久占据一个特权网络位置，或者更均匀地在辩论中分配影响力。我们在理论上将PEAR描述为一个等变稀疏路由器：它在智能体重新标记下保持准确性，同时降低路由复杂度并改进泛化。在四个推理基准和六个不同的LLM主干上的全面实证评估表明，PEAR在平均准确率上显著超过了最强的辩论基线。代码位于https://github.com/EVIEHub/PEAR。

Original abstract: Multi-agent debate improves the reliability of large language models (LLMs) through iterative peer critiques. However, fixed topologies often introduce persistent positional biases, amplify unreliable agents, and cause high sensitivity to role assignments. We introduce \textit{Permutation-Equivariant Adaptive Routing Multi-Agent Debate (PEAR)}, an inference-time protocol that dynamically reconfigures communication roles and sparse topologies across consecutive debate rounds. By strategically switching agent-to-role assignments based on evolving agent states, PEAR prevents any agent from permanently occupying a privileged network position or distributes influence more evenly across the debate. We theoretically characterize PEAR as an equivariant sparse router: it preserves accuracy under agent relabeling while reducing routing complexity and improving generalization. Comprehensive empirical evaluations across four reasoning benchmarks and six diverse LLM backbones demonstrate PEAR significantly improves average accuracy over the strongest debate baselines. The code is at https://github.com/EVIEHub/PEAR.

</details>


### [37] [Generating Robust Portfolios of Optimization Models using Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27013v1)
*Eleni Straitouri,Cheol Woo Kim,Milind Tambe*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 使用LLM生成优化模型组合，类似智能体工作流（生成+评估），方法可迁移至代码优化。

TL;DR: 提出一种利用LLM作为生成器和评估器生成优化模型组合的算法，保证包含高质量候选，提升可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单个LLM生成的优化模型不可靠，仅输出单一模型的方法存在风险。

Method: 利用单个LLM同时作为随机生成器和推理评估器，构建统一框架生成模型组合，并基于理论保证确保组合质量。

Result: 理论证明了组合包含高质量候选的条件，实验验证了该方法在一系列优化建模任务中的强劲性能。

Conclusion: 该方法能有效生成鲁棒的优化模型组合，支持人机协作决策，提升模型可靠性。

中文摘要：数学优化是跨领域（如资源分配和规划）结构化决策的强大工具。然而，构建忠实于现实的优化模型仍然是一个重大瓶颈，因为这通常需要既具备领域专业知识又具备优化知识，而这些往往稀缺。大型语言模型（LLM）的最新进展有望弥合这一差距，使得能够从自然语言描述生成候选优化模型。然而，无法保证任何单个LLM生成的模型是可靠的，因此仅输出一个模型的现有方法存在风险。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种新颖的算法，生成一个优化模型组合，旨在对LLM的局限性具有鲁棒性。我们的方法利用了这样一个观察：单个LLM可以扮演两个不同的角色——作为随机生成器和作为推理评估器——并提出了一个统一的框架，以互补的方式利用这两种能力。我们提供了理论保证，表明只要生成器或评估器中的任何一个与人类偏好良好对齐，该组合就保证包含高质量候选，从而实现一个原则性的人机协作过程，决策者可以在承诺之前审查多个候选。我们进一步在经验上验证了我们的方法，在一系列优化建模任务中展示了强劲性能。

Original abstract: Mathematical optimization is a powerful tool for structured decision-making across domains such as resource allocation and planning. Formulating optimization models faithful to reality, though, remains a significant bottleneck as it typically demands both domain expertise and optimization knowledge that are often scarce. Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) promise to bridge this gap, enabling the generation of candidate optimization models from natural language descriptions. However, there is no guarantee that any single LLM-generated model is reliable, and existing approaches that output only one model are therefore risky. In this work, we propose a novel algorithm that generates a portfolio of optimization models, designed to be robust to the limitations of LLMs. Our method exploits the observation that a single LLM can play two distinct roles $\unicode{x2014}$ as a stochastic generator and as a reasoning evaluator $\unicode{x2014}$ and proposes a unified framework that leverages both capabilities in a complementary manner. We provide theoretical guarantees showing that, as long as either the generator or the evaluator is well-aligned with human preferences, the portfolio is guaranteed to contain high-quality candidates, enabling a principled human-in-the-loop process in which a decision-maker can review multiple candidates before committing to one. We further validate our approach empirically, demonstrating strong performance across a range of optimization modeling tasks.

Original abstract: The goal of artificial intelligence is to create agents capable of general, adaptive behaviour in open-ended environments. Guided by the "Bitter Lesson", we argue that the most effective path toward this goal is to systematically remove human priors and allow intelligence to naturally emerge through interaction with a "Big World" that is orders of magnitude more complex than the agent itself. We propose the mobile Graphical User Interface (GUI) as a practical proxy for such a world and introduce Darwin Mobile Agent, an open-source infrastructure designed as a foundation for autonomous reinforcement learning in this domain. This framework addresses the data-collection bottleneck in real-world mobile interactions by using an asynchronous agent-environment loop across parallel cloud-phone instances. We further propose a conceptual roadmap to systematically remove human priors from three fundamental pillars of a self-evolving agent: task curricula, outcome verification, and memory management. We validate that the Darwin infrastructure provides the stability and scalability required for the first stage of this roadmap: policy optimisation in the GUI domain. This work establishes the practical and theoretical foundation necessary to move toward truly autonomous, self-evolving GUI agents.

### [39] [ORCA: An End-to-End Interactive Copilot for Optimized Root Cause Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27022v1)
*Phi Nguyen Xuan,Nicholas Tagliapietra,Lavdim Halilaj,Kristian Kersting,Juergen Luettin*

TL;DR: ORCA是一个端到端因果分析副驾驶，通过编排智能体理解用户目标并引导工作流，支持因果发现、效应估计、可解释性和RCA，自动生成报告，在真实用例中有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: ORCA通过编排多个智能体（agents）来理解用户目标，并引导用户选择从全自动到高度用户引导的因果分析工作流，集成了因果发现、因果效应估计、可解释性和根本原因分析（RCA）。

Result: ORCA能够评估和比较因果分析性能，生成关键指标和图表，并通过结构化报告提供见解，在多个真实世界用例中展示了有效性。

Conclusion: ORCA弥合了因果分析复杂性与领域专家可用性之间的鸿沟，提供了一种灵活且全面的端到端解决方案。

中文摘要：因果分析是许多领域中的关键任务，包括制造业、社会科学和医学。然而，尽管最近取得了进展，因果方法的概念和方法论复杂性使得领域专家难以理解。这一差距阻止了专家利用这些进展，并阻碍了缺乏真实世界数据用于验证的研究人员。为了弥合这一鸿沟，我们引入了ORCA，一个用于端到端因果分析的副驾驶。ORCA编排智能体以理解用户的目标，并引导他们完成最合适的因果分析工作流程，从全自动到高度用户引导的执行。它具备因果发现、因果效应估计、可解释性和根本原因分析（RCA）功能。ORCA评估并比较性能，生成关键指标和图表，并通过结构化报告生成见解。我们强调了它在几个真实世界用例中的有效性。

Original abstract: Causal analysis is a crucial task in many domains, including manufacturing, social science, and medicine. However, despite recent progress, the conceptual and methodological complexity of causal methods makes them largely inaccessible to domain experts. This gap prevents experts from leveraging these advances and hinders researchers who lack access to real-world data for validation. To bridge this divide, we introduce ORCA, a copilot for end-to-end causal analysis. ORCA orchestrates agents to understand the user's goals and guide them through the most appropriate causal analysis workflow, from fully automatic to highly user-guided execution. It features causal discovery, causal effect estimation, explainability and Root-Cause-Analysis (RCA). ORCA evaluates and compares performance, generates key metrics and diagrams, and generates insights through structured reports. We highlight its effectiveness across several real-world use-cases.

### [40] [Can Broad Biomedical Knowledge be Contextualized into Scenario-Grounded Propositions?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27082v1)
*Qingyuan Zeng,Ziyang Chen,Pengxiang Cai,Zixin Guan,Anglin Liu,Lang Qin,Xinyao Lai,Jintai Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出bi-level multi-agent框架用于知识情境化，架构可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出SCENE框架，通过双层多智能体搜索将广泛生物医学知识上下文化为情境化命题，在临床试验和L1000研究中发现可验证的假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 背景知识太泛化，数据驱动模式难解释，需要弥合广泛知识与具体数据之间的差距，产生可检查、可验证的命题。

Method: 提出双层多智能体框架SCENE：上层将广泛知识转化为搜索方向并基于数据模式具体化；下层通过多目标优化执行搜索，平衡证据强度和数据支持；两层迭代反馈优化。

Result: 在临床试验中发现具体且支持良好的患者亚组，优于基线；在L1000研究中识别出强靶标-响应匹配和高阳性率的扰动情境。

Conclusion: SCENE成功连接广泛知识和情境特异性证据，生成可追溯、可检查的假设，便于后续验证。

中文摘要：生物医学发现通常需要将广泛的生物医学知识与特定的实验或临床数据联系起来。背景知识提示了相关机制，但通常过于泛化，无法直接映射到数据集变量上，而数据驱动的模式可能具有数据集特异性且难以从机制上解释。我们将这一缺失的环节研究为知识上下文化：将广泛的生物医学知识转化为有证据支持的、情境化的命题，领域专家可以检查、重放和验证这些命题。我们提出了SCENE，一个双层多智能体框架，将知识上下文化视为迭代搜索。上层将广泛知识转化为搜索方向，并将它们基于数据集模式进行具体化。下层通过多目标优化执行这些方向，以识别在证据强度和数据支持之间取得平衡的具体命题。两层之间的反馈逐步优化搜索。我们在两种设置中评估SCENE：在临床试验场景中发现具有异质性治疗益处的患者亚组，以及在LINCS L1000研究中识别情境特异性生物学响应。在临床试验中，SCENE发现了具体且证据充分的亚组，优于现有基线方法。在L1000研究中，SCENE识别出具有强靶标-响应匹配和高阳性率的扰动情境。这些结果表明，SCENE连接了广泛知识和情境特异性证据，为后续验证产生了可追踪、可检查的假设。

Original abstract: Biomedical discovery often requires connecting broad biomedical knowledge with specific experimental or clinical data. Background knowledge suggests relevant mechanisms but is usually too general to map directly onto dataset variables, while data-driven patterns can be dataset-specific and hard to interpret mechanistically. We study this missing link as knowledge contextualization: transforming broad biomedical knowledge into evidence-supported, scenario-grounded propositions that domain experts can inspect, replay, and validate. We propose SCENE, a bi-level multi-agent framework that treats knowledge contextualization as iterative search. The upper level converts broad knowledge into search directions and grounds them in the dataset schema. The lower level executes these directions through multi-objective optimization to identify concrete propositions that balance evidential strength and data support. Feedback between the two levels progressively refines the search. We evaluate SCENE in two settings: discovering patient subgroups with heterogeneous treatment benefits in clinical trial scenarios, and identifying context-specific biological responses in LINCS L1000 studies. In clinical trials, SCENE discovers specific, well-supported subgroups and outperforms existing baselines. In L1000 studies, SCENE identifies perturbational contexts with strong target-response matching and high positive rates. These results show that SCENE bridges broad knowledge and scenario-specific evidence, producing traceable, inspectable hypotheses for follow-up validation.

### [41] [Position: AI Safety Requires Effective Controllability](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27117v1)
*Yige Li,Yunhao Feng,Jun Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出AI可控性作为安全目标，含benchmark，对agent中断与控制有启发。

TL;DR: 本文提出人工智能安全需要将可控性作为首要目标，并引入ControlBench基准评估可控性故障，实验发现现有关机制提供运行时控制不足，因此提出以控制为中心的架构框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对齐行为不能保证代理在开放环境中可被停止或约束，现有机制在冲突指令、长期执行等场景下缺乏可靠的运行时控制。

Method: 定义可控性概念，构建ControlBench基准，使用OpenClaw代理进行实验评估，并提出以控制为中心的架构框架。

Result: 当前对齐和护栏机制可降低风险，但在高风险代理场景中无法提供持久、权威的运行时控制。

Conclusion: AI安全需要以可控性为核心设计原则，包括明确的控制平面、运行时干预路径、持久控制状态和可审计接口。

中文摘要：人工智能安全在很大程度上仍被定义为对齐：训练模型遵循人类偏好、安全策略和规范约束。这种框架改善了现代语言模型的行为，但对齐行为本身并不能保证部署的代理在开放、交互式和使用工具的环境中可以被停止、覆盖或约束。一个系统可能在期望上是安全的，但在冲突指令、长期执行、对抗性输入或高风险工具使用下，仍可能无法服从明确的运行时权威。这篇立场论文认为，人工智能安全因此需要将可控性作为首要目标。我们将可控性定义为人工智能系统在运行时保持可靠的可中断、可覆盖、可重定向和可约束的能力，通过明确的控制信号实现，同时在无此类信号时保持正常的效用。为了研究这一差距，我们引入了ControlBench，一个用于评估高风险代理场景中可控性故障的基准。基于OpenClaw代理的实验表明，当前的对齐和护栏机制降低了风险，但往往无法提供持久、权威和可执行的运行时控制。因此，我们提出了一个以控制为中心的架构框架，强调明确的控制平面、运行时干预路径、持久控制状态和可审计的决策接口，作为未来可控人工智能系统的关键设计原则。

Original abstract: AI safety is still largely framed as alignment: training models to follow human preferences, safety policies, and normative constraints. That framing has improved the behavior of modern language models, but aligned behavior does not by itself guarantee that a deployed agent can be stopped, overridden, or constrained once it operates in open-ended, interactive, and tool-using environments. A system may be safe in expectation and still fail to yield to explicit runtime authority under conflicting instructions, long-horizon execution, adversarial inputs, or risky tool use. This position paper argues that AI safety therefore requires controllability as a first-class objective. We define \emph{controllability} as the ability of an AI system to remain reliably interruptible, overridable, redirectable, and constrainable by explicit control signals at runtime while preserving ordinary utility when such signals are absent. To study this gap, we introduce \controlbench{}, a benchmark for evaluating controllability failures in high-risk agentic scenarios. Experiments with OpenClaw-based agents show that current alignment and guardrail mechanisms reduce risk, but often fail to provide persistent, authoritative, and enforceable runtime control. We therefore propose a control-centric architectural framework that highlights explicit control planes, runtime intervention pathways, persistent control states, and auditable decision interfaces as key design principles for future controllable AI systems.

### [43] [StepOPSD: Step-Aware Online Preference Distillation for Agent Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27140v1)
*Yanfei Zhang,Xu Lin,Chenglin Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 步感知在线偏好蒸馏用于agent强化学习，改进信用分配。

TL;DR: 提出StepOPSD，一种以步为单位的信用重分配后训练偏好自蒸馏框架，通过在多个任务上取得最优结果验证了其有效性，并揭示了双旋钮定律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮对话强化学习中，轨迹级稀疏奖励与关键局部决策之间信用分配不匹配，现有OPD方法将轨迹视为整体字符串，忽略了因果交互单元。

Method: StepOPSD将轨迹分解为以动作中心的步片段，在事后增强的教师上下文中重新评分，将token级对数概率差距转化为带符号保留的优势塑形，并引入归一化的每步信用预算，最后使用GRPO更新。

Result: 在ALFWorld和Search-QA上，StepOPSD在多个子集取得最佳或次佳结果，如ALFWorld Heat 79.1%、PickTwo 95.0%、TriviaQA 61.6%、HotpotQA 40.4%（并列最佳）。

Conclusion: 较小的α_clip提供稳定局部信任区域，最优λ_mix任务依赖；步感知蒸馏在轨迹奖励与关键局部行动弱对齐时最有效。

中文摘要：针对多轮对话智能体的强化学习存在信用分配不匹配问题：奖励稀疏且是轨迹级别的，而成功往往取决于少数局部决策。现有的在线策略蒸馏（OPD）提供了更密集的token级监督，但通常将异质的智能体轨迹视为整体字符串而非因果交互单元。我们提出StepOPSD，一种后 rollout 的偏好自蒸馏框架，以智能体步作为信用重分配的单位。StepOPSD将轨迹分解为以动作中心的步片段，在事后增强的教师上下文下重新评分，并在GRPO更新前将token级对数概率差距转化为带符号保留的优势塑形和归一化的每步信用预算。在ALFWorld和Search-QA上使用Qwen3-1.7B和Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct，StepOPSD在对局部因果错误最敏感的子集上取得了最佳或次佳结果，包括ALFWorld Heat（79.1%）、PickTwo（95.0%）、Search-QA TriviaQA（61.6%）的第一名，以及HotpotQA（40.4%）的并列最佳结果。结果进一步揭示了一致的双旋钮定律：较小的α_clip作为广泛稳定的局部信任区域，而最优全局混合强度λ_mix则依赖于任务。这些发现表明，当轨迹级奖励与决定下游成功的局部行动弱对齐时，步感知蒸馏最为有用。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning for multi-turn agents suffers from a credit-assignment mismatch: rewards are sparse and trajectory-level, while success often hinges on a few local decisions. Existing online policy distillation (OPD) provides denser token-level supervision, but typically treats heterogeneous agent trajectories as monolithic strings rather than causal interaction units. We present StepOPSD, a post-rollout preference self-distillation framework that takes the agent step as the unit of credit redistribution. StepOPSD decomposes trajectories into action-centered step segments, rescoring them under hindsight-enriched teacher contexts and converting token-level log-probability gaps into sign-preserving advantage shaping with a normalized per-step credit budget before the GRPO update. Across ALFWorld and Search-QA with Qwen3-1.7B and Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct, StepOPSD attains best or second-best results on subsets most sensitive to local causal errors, including first-place performance on ALFWorld Heat (79.1%), PickTwo (95.0%), Search-QA TriviaQA (61.6%), and tied-best performance on HotpotQA (40.4%). The results further reveal a consistent two-knob law: smaller α_clip acts as a broadly stabilizing local trust region, whereas the optimal global mixing strength λ_mix remains task-dependent. These findings suggest that step-aware distillation is most useful when trajectory-level rewards are weakly aligned with the local action that determines downstream success.

</details>

*Yuxin Chen,Yi Zhang,Zhengzhou Cai,Yaorui Shi,Zhiyuan Yao,Chenhang Cui,Jingnan Zheng,Yaqi Huo,Xi Su,Qi Gu,Xunliang Cai,Xiang Wang,An Zhang,Tat-Seng Chua*

Result: 前沿LLM在个性化决策上表现不佳，揭示了当前能力与实际需求间的巨大差距及多种失败模式。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）已演变为交互式代理，与用户在现实世界任务中协作。在这种环境中，有效协作越来越依赖于理解用户超出明确陈述的内容，因为用户意图往往反映在碎片化的日常互动中，需要个性化建模和主动交互。然而，现有的代理基准主要评估推理和工具使用，很大程度上忽视了在现实场景中推断和利用用户偏好的挑战。为填补这一空白，我们引入了VitaBench 2.0，一个用于评估长期用户交互中个性化和主动代理行为的基准。在VitaBench 2.0中，任务被组织为按时间顺序排列的序列，针对单个用户，其中偏好嵌入在碎片化和异质的交互中。成功完成任务要求代理从这些交互中持续提取、利用和更新用户偏好。我们进一步通过要求代理识别缺失信息并在决策前主动从用户或环境中获取信息的任务来评估主动性。为支持系统分析，我们提供了一个可扩展的内存接口，使得不同内存架构之间的受控比较成为可能。我们对一系列前沿专有和开源LLM进行了基准测试。结果表明，即使对于最先进的模型，现实世界的个性化仍然非常具有挑战性，揭示了当前能力与实际需求之间的巨大差距。广泛的分析进一步揭示了当前代理在现实世界个性化决策中的失败模式和能力瓶颈，为未来模型改进提供了见解。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have evolved into interactive agents that collaborate with users in real-world tasks. Effective collaboration in such settings increasingly depends on understanding the user beyond what is explicitly stated, as user intent is often reflected in fragmented daily interactions and requires both personalized modeling and proactive interaction. However, existing agent benchmarks primarily evaluate reasoning and tool use, largely overlooking the challenges of inferring and leveraging user preferences in realistic scenarios. To address this gap, we introduce VitaBench 2.0, a benchmark for evaluating personalized and proactive agent behavior in long-term user interactions. In VitaBench 2.0, tasks are organized as temporally ordered sequences for individual users, where preferences are embedded in fragmented and heterogeneous interactions. Successful completion of tasks requires the agent to continuously extract, utilize, and update user preferences from these interactions. We further evaluate proactiveness through tasks that require agents to recognize missing information and actively acquire it from users or environments before making decisions. To support systematic analysis, we provide an extensible memory interface that enables controlled comparison across different memory architectures. We benchmark a diverse set of frontier proprietary and open-source LLMs. Results show that real-world personalization remains highly challenging even for state-of-the-art models, revealing a substantial gap between current capabilities and practical requirements. Extensive analysis further reveals the failure modes and capability bottlenecks of current agents in real-world personalized decision-making, providing insights for future model improvements.

### [45] [AlphaMemo: Structured Search-Process Memory for Self-Evolving Alpha Mining Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20625v1)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代理在因子挖掘中面临组合搜索空间、噪声反馈、冗余发现和过拟合风险，需改进记忆机制以提升效率和鲁棒性。

Method: AlphaMemo采用结构化搜索过程记忆，从AST差异提取编辑模式，应用置信门控残差记忆和不对称否决控制，结合搜索账本先验。

Result: 在CSI 500和S&P 500上，样本外性能和固定预算发现效率提升，消融实验验证了各组件的有效性。

Conclusion: AlphaMemo通过结构化记忆机制有效解决了因子挖掘中的关键挑战，展示了自演化代理在金融领域的潜力。

中文摘要：LLM代理通过结合金融先验知识、符号推理、可执行因子生成和反馈驱动的优化，在因子挖掘方面展现出潜力。然而，它们面临组合搜索空间、噪声非平稳反馈、重复发现以及因天真地重复使用过去成功而导致的过拟合风险。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了AlphaMemo，一种具有结构化搜索过程记忆的自演化因子挖掘代理。AlphaMemo不仅记忆最终因子或完整轨迹，而是记录哪些编辑模式在特定父因子上下文下成功或失败的可重用证据。它从抽象语法树（AST）差异中提取模式，在搜索账本先验之上应用置信门控残差记忆，并使用非对称否决控制来抑制高置信度的失败模式。在CSI 500和S&P 500上的实验显示，样本外性能和固定预算发现效率有所提升，消融实验验证了残差学习、置信门控、AST差异模式和否决记忆的作用。代码地址：https://github.com/jarrettyu/AlphaMemo。

Original abstract: LLM agents are promising for alpha mining via combining financial priors, symbolic reasoning, executable factor generation, and feedback-driven refinement. Yet, they face a combinatorial search space, noisy non-stationary feedback, redundant discoveries, and overfitting risks from naively reusing past successes. To address these challenges, we propose AlphaMemo, a self-evolving alpha mining agent with Structured Search-Process Memory. Rather than memorizing only final factors or full trajectories, AlphaMemo records reusable evidence about which edit motifs work or fail under specific parent-factor contexts. It extracts motifs from Abstract Syntax Tree (AST) differences, applies confidence-gated residual memory on top of a search-ledger prior, and uses asymmetric veto control to suppress high-confidence failure patterns. Experiments on CSI 500 and S\&P 500 show improved out-of-sample performance and fixed-budget discovery efficiency, with ablations validating the roles of residual learning, confidence gating, AST-diff motifs, and veto memory. Code is at https://github.com/jarrettyu/AlphaMemo.

</details>


### [46] [Learning to Act under Noise: Enhancing Agent Robustness via Noisy Environments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27209v1)
*Yuxin Chen,Xiaodong Cai,Junfeng Fang,Zhuowen Han,Yu Wang,Yaorui Shi,Yi Zhang,Qi Gu,Xunliang Cai,Xiang Wang,An Zhang,Tat-Seng Chua*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出NoisyAgent增强LLM agent鲁棒性，通用agent训练方法可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: 提出NoisyAgent框架，通过在训练中引入用户噪声和工具噪声，提升LLM智能体在现实动态环境中的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体在理想化训练设置中表现良好，但在现实随机且不完美的环境中性能显著下降，这是由于训练与部署之间的环境不匹配。

Method: NoisyAgent通过修改用户交互模式和模拟工具执行结果，在训练中注入用户噪声和工具噪声，并采用渐进式难度增加和部分轨迹应用噪声的策略来稳定训练。

Result: 大量实验表明，NoisyAgent在噪声和动态环境下持续提升智能体鲁棒性，并且在理想化基准测试上也取得性能提升。

Conclusion: 可控的环境噪声暴露促进了更通用的推理和决策行为，强调了建模交互不完美对于弥合训练与部署差距的重要性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）的最新进展促进了LLM作为能够推理、规划和工具使用的交互式智能体的广泛部署。尽管在现有基准测试上表现强劲，但当部署在本质上随机且不完美的现实世界环境中时，这类智能体常常表现出显著的性能下降。我们认为，这种差异源于理想化训练设置与现实交互动态之间的根本性不匹配，现有范式依赖于精心策划的任务指令和稳定、可控的环境。为了解决这一差距，我们提出了NoisyAgent，一个明确将环境不完美纳入智能体学习过程的智能体训练框架。我们识别出真实场景中交互噪声的两个主要来源：用户噪声（捕捉用户交互中的模糊性和可变性）和工具噪声（反映工具执行中的失败和异常）。我们通过修改用户交互模式并在训练环境中模拟工具执行结果，将这些扰动引入训练流程。为了稳定训练并鼓励智能体处理日益具有挑战性的不完美，噪声仅应用于部分轨迹，并随着模型适应当前噪声水平而逐渐增加难度。大量实验表明，我们的方法在噪声和动态环境下持续提升智能体的鲁棒性。我们的分析揭示，在噪声条件下训练也能在理想化基准测试上带来性能提升，这表明可控的环境噪声暴露促进了更通用的推理和决策行为。我们的发现强调了建模交互不完美对于弥合智能体训练与现实部署之间差距的重要性。

Original abstract: Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have facilitated the widespread deployment of LLMs as interactive agents capable of reasoning, planning, and tool use. Despite strong performance on existing benchmarks, such agents often exhibit notable degradation when deployed in real-world settings, where environments are inherently stochastic and imperfect. We argue that this discrepancy arises from a fundamental mismatch between idealized training settings and real-world interaction dynamics, where current paradigms rely on carefully curated task instructions and stable, well-controlled environments. To address this gap, we propose NoisyAgent, an agentic training framework that explicitly incorporates environmental imperfections into the agent learning process. We identify two major sources of interaction noise in real-world scenarios: user noise, which captures ambiguity and variability in user interaction, and tool noise, which reflects failures and anomalies in tool execution. We introduce such perturbations into the training pipeline by modifying user interaction patterns and simulating tool execution results within the training environment. To stabilize training while encouraging agents to handle increasingly challenging imperfections, noise is applied to only a subset of rollouts and progressively increased in difficulty as the model adapts to the current noise level. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach consistently improves agent robustness under noisy and dynamic environments. Our analysis reveals that training under noise conditions also yields performance gains on idealized benchmarks, suggesting that controlled exposure to environmental noise promotes more generalizable reasoning and decision-making behaviors. Our findings highlight the importance of modeling interaction imperfections for bridging the gap between agent training and real-world deployment.

### [47] [SIA: Self Improving AI with Harness & Weight Updates](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27276v2)
*Prannay Hebbar,Yogendra Manawat,Samuel Verboomen,Alesia Ivanova,Selvam Palanimalai,Kunal Bhatia,Vignesh Baskaran*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接构建自我改进AI agent，同时更新harness和weights，并在GPU kernel优化上验证，与自动代码优化紧密相关。

TL;DR: 提出SIA，一种同时更新任务智能体框架和权重的自我改进循环，在三个领域显著超越先前最优方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法孤立地分别优化框架或权重，未能充分利用两者的协同效应，而人类瓶颈限制了AI的自我改进能力。

Method: 设计一个语言模型反馈智能体（Feedback-Agent），在每次任务执行后同时调整任务特定智能体的框架（工具、提示、搜索策略等）和模型权重，形成闭环自我改进。

Result: 在中文法律分类、GPU内核优化和单细胞RNA去噪三个任务上，结合框架和权重更新（SIA-W+H）分别比先前最优方法提升25.1%、12.4%和20.4%。

Conclusion: 框架更新赋予模型智能体性和搜索能力，权重更新注入领域直觉，两者结合比单一更新更有效，为自改进AI提供了通用框架。

中文摘要：人类是构建和改进AI的瓶颈。模型及其包装的智能体都是由人编写、调整和纠正的。AI能够自行改进的长期目标仍未实现。两个大致独立的研究方向试图突破这一瓶颈。框架更新学派让元智能体重写任务特定智能体的脚手架（其工具、提示、重试逻辑和搜索过程），而模型权重保持不变。测试时训练学派则使用手工编写的强化学习流水线，基于任务反馈更新模型自身的权重，而框架保持不变。这两个领域各自孤立运作。我们提出SIA，一个自我改进循环，其中语言模型智能体（反馈智能体）同时更新任务特定智能体的框架和权重。我们在三个对比鲜明的领域进行评估：中文法律罪名分类、底层GPU内核优化和单细胞RNA去噪。结合两种杠杆在所有三个基准上都优于仅迭代脚手架。SIA-W+H在LawBench上比先前SOTA高25.1%，GPU内核比先前SOTA快12.4%（1017微秒对比1161微秒），去噪效果比先前SOTA高20.4%。框架更新使模型具有智能体性，塑造其搜索和行动方式，而权重更新建立了任何提示或脚手架都无法灌输的领域直觉。

Original abstract: Humans are the bottleneck in building and improving AI. Both the models and the agents that wrap them are written, tuned, and corrected by people. The long-horizon goal of an AI that can figure out how to improve itself remains open. Two largely disjoint research lines attack this bottleneck. The harness-update school has a meta-agent rewrite the scaffold of a task-specific agent (its tools, prompts, retry logic, and search procedure) while the model weights are held fixed. The test-time training school uses hand-written RL pipelines to update the model's own weights on task feedback while the harness is held fixed. These two silos operate in isolation. We propose SIA, a self-improving loop in which a language-model agent (the Feedback-Agent) updates both the harness and the weights of a task-specific agent. We evaluate across three contrasting domains: Chinese legal charge classification, low-level GPU kernel optimisation, and single-cell RNA denoising. Combining both levers outperforms scaffold iteration alone on all three benchmarks. SIA-W+H achieves 25.1% over prior SOTA on LawBench, 12.4% faster GPU kernels than prior SOTA (1,017 vs 1,161 μs), and 20.4% over prior SOTA on denoising. Harness updates make the model agentic, shaping how it searches and acts, while weight updates build the domain intuition that no prompt or scaffold can instil.

### [48] [Modeling Agentic Technical Debt and Stochastic Tax: A Standalone Framework for Measurement, Simulation, and Dashboarding](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27320v1)
*Muhammad Zia Hydari,Raja Iqbal,Narayan Ramasubbu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出Agentic技术债务和随机税的概念框架与方法论，对理解agent系统运维有启发。

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个区分代理技术债务和随机税的模型，阐述了它们的关系，并提供了估算方法和模拟验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI系统管理缺乏对代理技术债务和随机税之间差异的正式区分，导致治理和运营成本混淆。

Method: 从仪表板表达式出发，构建结构模型，定义变量参数，利用运营数据估算成本，并通过应付账款模拟验证。

Result: 成功区分代理技术债务（累积债务）和随机税（重复运营负担），表明债务可放大税，但税独立于债务存在。

Conclusion: 代理技术债务和随机税是不同概念，需要分别管理；模型可用于企业AI治理和成本优化。

中文摘要：代理人工智能系统将概率推理通过工具、上下文、记忆、编排和外部工作流集成与委托行动相结合。本文开发了一个正式且对管理有用的模型，该模型区分了代理技术债务与随机税。代理技术债务是累积的设计和治理责任存量。随机税是一种重复发生的运营负担流，当随机代理被用于业务工作流时产生。这两个概念相关但并不相同：债务可以放大税，而即使债务最小化，税仍可能为正。本文从一个简洁的仪表板表达式开始，将其扩展成一个更完整的结构模型，定义所有变量和参数，展示如何从运营数据中估算每个成本类别，并通过应付账款模拟和配套电子表格说明该框架。

Original abstract: Agentic AI systems combine probabilistic reasoning with delegated action through tools, context, memory, orchestration, and external workflow integration. This note develops a formal and managerially usable model that distinguishes Agentic Technical Debt from Stochastic Tax. Agentic Technical Debt is a stock of accumulated design and governance liability. Stochastic Tax is a recurring flow of operating burden that arises when stochastic agents are used in business workflows. The two constructs are related, but they are not the same: debt can amplify the tax, while the tax can remain positive even when debt is minimized. The note starts from a compact dashboard expression, expands it into a fuller structural model, defines all variables and parameters, shows how each cost category can be estimated from operational data, and illustrates the framework with an accounts-payable simulation and companion spreadsheet.

### [49] [Natural Language Query to Configuration for Retrieval Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27361v1)
*Melissa Z. Pan,Negar Arabzadeh,Mathew Jacob,Fiodar Kazhamiaka,Esha Choukse,Matei Zaharia*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 检索agent配置选择，提出成本-质量权衡的通用agent调优方法。

TL;DR: BRANE通过LLM提取查询特征，训练轻量预测器估计各配置的正确率，推理时动态选择成本-质量最优的检索流程配置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有检索流程针对工作负载静态调优，忽略了每查询的优化机会，导致成本与质量未达最优。

Method: 使用LLM将查询转换为工作负载特征，训练轻量级预测器估计每个配置的正确性；推理时选择最大化（预测正确性 - 成本）的配置。

Result: 在MuSiQue等数据集上，BRANE持续推动帕累托前沿，以最高89%的成本降低匹配最佳固定配置准确率，优于LLM路由、规则和微调基线。

Conclusion: 按查询动态配置检索流程是静态调优的有效替代，能更好平衡成本与质量。

中文摘要：现代检索代理暴露出许多配置选择——大语言模型、检索器、文档数量、跳数以及合成策略——每个选择都会影响回答质量和服务成本。如今，这些流程通常针对每个工作负载进行一次性手工调优，留下了大量未利用的按查询优化空间。我们形式化问题：给定一个自然语言查询以及一个准确率或预算目标，从预定义的流程目录中选择在推理时最小化成本或最大化准确率的配置。我们提出 **BRANE**，它使用大语言模型将每个查询转换为特定工作负载的特征，然后训练一个轻量级的按配置预测器，用于估计该流程是否能正确回答查询。在推理时，**BRANE** 选择最大化经成本惩罚后的预测正确性的配置，从而在不重新训练的情况下暴露可调的成本-质量权衡。在 MuSiQue、BrowseComp-Plus 和 FinanceBench 上，**BRANE** 持续推动成本-质量帕累托前沿，以最高 89% 的成本降低匹配最佳固定配置的准确率，并优于大语言模型路由、基于规则和微调后的 Qwen3-4B 基线。这些结果表明，按查询配置完整检索流程是静态工作负载调优的一种实用替代方案。

Original abstract: Modern retrieval agents expose many configuration choices -- LLM, retriever, number of documents, number of hops, and synthesis strategy -- each shaping both answer quality and serving cost. Today, these pipelines are typically hand-tuned once per workload, leaving substantial per-query optimization untapped. We formulate the problem: given a natural-language query and either an accuracy or a budget target, select from a predefined pipeline catalog the configuration that minimizes cost or maximizes accuracy at inference time. We propose **BRANE**, which uses an LLM to convert each query into workload-specific characteristics, then trains a lightweight per-configuration predictor that estimates whether the pipeline will answer the query correctly. At inference time, **BRANE** selects the configuration that maximizes predicted correctness penalized by cost, exposing a tunable cost-quality tradeoff without retraining. Across MuSiQue, BrowseComp-Plus, and FinanceBench, **BRANE** consistently pushes the cost-quality Pareto frontier, matches the best fixed configuration's accuracy at up to 89% lower cost, and outperforms LLM-routing, rule-based, and fine-tuned Qwen3-4B baselines. These results show that per-query configuration of the full retrieval pipeline is a practical alternative to static workload-level tuning.

</details>


### [50] [MUSE-Autoskill: Self-Evolving Agents via Skill Creation, Memory, Management, and Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27366v2)
*Huawei Lin,Peng Li,Jie Song,Fuxin Jiang,Tieying Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自进化agent框架，涵盖技能创建、记忆、管理等完整生命周期，通用性强。

TL;DR: MUSE-Autoskill通过统一技能生命周期（创建、记忆、管理、评估、改进）实现技能的高效创建、复用和演化，在SkillsBench和SkillLearnBench上超越Hermes、Codex和Claude Code。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能创建方法将技能视为孤立、静态的，限制了可复用性、可靠性和长期改进。

Method: 提出MUSE-Autoskill Agent框架，包含技能创建、记忆、管理、评估和细化的统一生命周期，按需创建技能，跨任务存储，通过目录检索，并积累技能经验。

Result: 在SkillsBench和SkillLearnBench上优于Hermes、Codex、Claude Code；自创技能超越人类作者（85.24% vs 81.17%）；技能迁移至Hermes准确率51.90%。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）智能体依赖可复用技能解决复杂任务，但现有技能创建方法常将技能视为孤立、静态的人工制品，限制了可复用性、可靠性和长期改进。我们提出MUSE-Autoskill Agent（记忆利用技能进化），一个以技能为中心的智能体框架，在统一生命周期下创建、复用和改进技能：创建、记忆、管理、评估和改进。MUSE按需创建技能，跨任务存储，通过技能目录检索，并积累每个技能的经验以供后续复用和适应。在SkillsBench和SkillLearnBench的主要报告设置中，MUSE-Autoskill优于Hermes、Codex和Claude Code。在SkillsBench上，其自创技能在成功覆盖的子集上超越了人类作者技能（85.24% vs. 81.17%），表明生命周期管理的技能可以将智能体经验提炼为高效的可复用资产；MUSE创建的技能比Codex或Claude创建的技能更有效地迁移到Hermes，迁移准确率达到51.90%。这些结果强调了将技能视为长期、经验感知和可测试资产的重要性。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents rely on reusable skills to solve complex tasks, but existing skill creation approaches often treat skills as isolated, static artifacts, limiting reusability, reliability, and long-term improvement. We propose MUSE-Autoskill Agent (Memory-Utilizing Skill Evolution), a skill-centric agent framework that creates, reuses, and refines skills under a unified lifecycle: creation, memory, management, evaluation, and refinement. MUSE creates skills on demand, stores them across tasks, retrieves them through a skill catalog, and accumulates per-skill experience for later reuse and adaptation. Across the main reported settings on SkillsBench and SkillLearnBench, MUSE-Autoskill outperforms Hermes, Codex, and Claude Code. On SkillsBench, its self-created skills surpass human-authored skills on the successfully covered subset (85.24% vs. 81.17%), showing that lifecycle-managed skills can distill agent experience into highly effective reusable assets; MUSE-created skills also transfer to Hermes more effectively than Codex- or Claude-created skills, reaching 51.90% accuracy under transfer. These results highlight the importance of treating skills as long-lived, experience-aware, and testable assets.

### [51] [DynaSchedBench: Calibrated Dynamic Scheduling Benchmarks and Observability Paradox in LLM-based Scheduling Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27566v1)
*Shijie Cao,Yuan Yuan,Jing Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 动态调度benchmark及LLM调度agent的observability悖论，对agent评估有启发。

TL;DR: 提出DynaSchedBench框架解决DFJSP中基准过拟合和噪声问题，通过SESC校准实例难度，发现LLM调度代理存在可观测性悖论和性能局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经组合优化方法在DFJSP上因静态基准和未校准生成器导致评估偏差，需要严格控制的诊断框架来公平比较算法。

Method: 设计DynaSchedBench框架，包含SESC校准器利用SSI分层实例难度，集成模块化组件进行实例生成、模拟、评估等。

Result: SESC计算效率高且收敛可靠；LLM代理存在“可观测性悖论”：过多信息反而劣化性能；工具增强和精炼策略无显著提升；多数LLM不如强调度基线。

Conclusion: DynaSchedBench为DFJSP提供可信评估平台，揭示了LLM代理的局限性，提示未来需关注信息表征和算法设计。

中文摘要：神经组合优化在动态灵活作业车间调度问题（DFJSP）上的进展目前受到方法论矛盾的阻碍：静态基准鼓励基准过拟合，而未校准的生成器用随机噪声掩盖了算法能力。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了	extbf{DynaSchedBench}，一个用于DFJSP的诊断框架，该框架严格控制了实例生成过程。我们的方法不依赖于参数采样，而是利用顺序事件空间校准器（SESC）计算一种新颖的调度压力指数（SSI）来按难度分层实例。我们证明，SESC在计算效率上显著优于进化基线，同时可靠地收敛到目标指标。该框架集成了实例生成、基于快照的模拟、智能体、评估和可视化等模块化组件，从而能够严格测试反应式和基于前瞻的策略。利用这个校准环境，我们识别了基于LLM的调度智能体的关键局限性。具体来说，在动态调度的逐步在线决策中，我们发现了“可观测性悖论”：为智能体提供完整结构信息的oracle访问可能会降低策略性能，反而劣于简洁信息。此外，尽管消耗大量令牌，工具增强和精炼策略未能可靠地提升性能，大多数LLM智能体无法持续超越强大的调度基线——它们的行为更像稳健的启发式近似器，而非卓越的优化器。

Original abstract: Progress in neural combinatorial optimization for Dynamic Flexible Job Shop Scheduling Problem (DFJSP) is currently hindered by a methodological tension: static benchmarks encourage benchmark overfitting, while uncalibrated generators obscure algorithmic capability with stochastic noise. To resolve this, we introduce \textbf{DynaSchedBench}, a diagnostic framework for DFJSP that rigorously controls the instance-generation process. Instead of relying on parameter sampling, our approach utilizes Sequential Event-Space Calibrator (SESC) that computes a novel Schedule Stress Index (SSI) to stratify instances by difficulty. We demonstrate that SESC is substantially more computationally efficient than evolutionary baselines while converging reliably to the target metrics. The framework integrates modular components for instance generation, snapshot-based simulation, agents, evaluation, and visualization, thereby enabling rigorous testing of reactive and lookahead-based policies. Leveraging this calibrated environment, we identify key limitations of LLM-based scheduling agents. Specifically, in step-wise online decision-making for dynamic scheduling, we identify an ``Observability Paradox'': providing agents with oracle access to full structural information can degrade policy performance, underperforming concise information. Furthermore, despite substantial token overhead, tool-augmented and refinement strategies fail to reliably improve performance, and most LLM agents fail to consistently surpass strong dispatching baselines-behaving more like robust heuristic approximators than superior optimizers.

### [52] [Why LLMs Fail at Causal Discovery and How Interventional Agents Escape](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27567v1)
*Amartya Roy,Sonali Parbhoo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM因果发现失败原因及介入式agent框架，理论分析可迁移。

TL;DR: 证明现有LLM因果发现方法因核障碍而无法区分等价图，并提出A-CBO方法通过外部贝叶斯优化绕过此限制，无需训练即可超越微调方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在因果发现任务上性能随复杂度增加而退化，但失败原因未被揭示；需要从理论上理解根本限制并设计超越方法。

Method: 提出Agentic Causal Bayesian Optimization (A-CBO)：冻结的LLM作为干预预言机回答干预效应查询，外部贝叶斯循环在对数轮内更新候选图的后验分布，决策发生在核障碍适用空间之外。

Result: 在Corr2Cause上A-CBO无需训练即匹配微调基线；在Extended Corr2Cause（24变量，18K测试样本）上显著优于微调和偏好优化，且优势随复杂度增长。

Conclusion: 因果发现中的核障碍是学习范式本身的固有限制，A-CBO通过将决策移出该空间实现了可证明收敛且性能优越的因果发现，无需改变底层模型。

中文摘要：因果发现是科学推理的基石，但大型语言模型能否可靠地执行因果发现仍然是一个开放问题。最近的基准测试表明，即使是经过微调的模型，在简单的因果图上也会出现性能停滞，并且随着复杂度的增加而退化，但其失败的原因尚未明确。我们证明这种失败是根本性的：监督微调、直接偏好优化和上下文学习都会产生无法区分生成相似观测数据的因果图的预测器，任何尝试区分都需要模型的内部表示无界增长，这违反了这些方法有效的条件。我们将此形式化为一个核障碍定理，确立了该限制是学习范式固有的，而不是任何特定模型或数据集的问题。我们提出了Agentic Causal Bayesian Optimization（A-CBO），其中冻结的语言模型充当干预预言机，回答关于干预效应的有针对性查询，而外部贝叶斯循环在对数轮内将后验集中在候选因果图上。由于决策发生在障碍适用的空间之外，A-CBO能够可证明地收敛，同时底层模型保持不变。在Corr2Cause上，A-CBO无需任何训练即可匹配微调基线。在扩展到24个变量和18K测试样本的Extended Corr2Cause上，A-CBO显著优于微调和偏好优化，并且优势持续增长。

Original abstract: Causal discovery is a cornerstone of scientific reasoning, yet whether large language models can perform it reliably remains an open question. Recent benchmarks show that even fine-tuned models plateau on simple causal graphs and degrade as complexity grows, but why they fail has not been established. We prove the failure is fundamental: supervised fine-tuning, direct preference optimization, and in-context learning all produce predictors that cannot distinguish between causal graphs generating similar observational data, and any attempt to do so requires the model's internal representations to grow unboundedly, violating the very conditions under which these methods work. We formalize this as a kernel obstruction theorem, establishing that the limitation is intrinsic to the learning paradigm, \emph{not any particular model or dataset}. We propose Agentic Causal Bayesian Optimization (A-CBO), wherein a frozen language model serves as an interventional oracle answering targeted queries about intervention effects, while an external Bayesian loop concentrates beliefs over candidate graphs in logarithmically many rounds. Because the decision operates outside the space where the obstruction applies, A-CBO provably converges while the underlying model remains unchanged. On Corr2Cause, A-CBO matches fine-tuned baselines without any training. On Extended Corr2Cause, a new benchmark scaling to 24 variables with 18K test samples, A-CBO significantly outperforms both fine-tuning and preference optimization, with the advantage growing

### [53] [LaneRoPE: Positional Encoding for Collaborative Parallel Reasoning and Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27570v1)
*Gabriele Cesa,Thomas Hehn,Aleix Torres-Camps,Àlex Batlle Casellas,Jordi Ros-Giralt,Arash Behboodi,Tribhuvanesh Orekondy*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 协作并行推理的位置编码，可用于多agent协作通信。

TL;DR: 提出LaneRoPE方法，通过序列间注意力掩码和RoPE扩展实现LLM并行生成时的序列协作，提升数学推理准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有并行测试时缩放技术中序列独立生成，不重用中间结果，导致准确率受限或效率低，LaneRoPE旨在通过序列间协作克服这一局限。

Method: LaneRoPE包含两个关键思想：(a) 序列间注意力掩码，使序列采样相互依赖；(b) RoPE扩展，注入位置信息以捕获跨序列和序列内的相对位置。

Result: 在数学推理任务上，LaneRoPE在有限生成长度下获得额外的准确性提升，且推理开销可忽略。

Conclusion: LaneRoPE以最小架构改动和低开销实现序列协作，适合快速集成到现有LLM推理管道。

中文摘要：并行LLM测试时缩放技术（例如，最佳N选一）需要从同一输入提示中抽取N>1个序列。这些方法通过利用批处理N个生成的计算效率来提高准确性。然而，传统上批次中的每个序列是独立生成的，因此不重用其他序列的中间生成、计算或观察。在本文中，我们提出LaneRoPE，以在生成时实现N>1个序列之间的协调与协作。LaneRoPE包含两个关键思想：(a) 一个序列间注意力掩码，使得序列的采样相互依赖；(b) 一个RoPE扩展，注入位置信息，捕获标记之间的相对位置，无论是在特定序列内部还是外部。我们在数学推理任务上评估了我们的方法，并发现了有希望的结果：LaneRoPE实现了序列间的协作，在有限的生成长度下产生了额外的准确性提升。重要的是，由于LaneRoPE在最小改动底层LLM架构的情况下实现了协调，并且在推理时引入了可忽略的开销，因此它对于将并行推理快速融入现有LLM推理管道具有吸引力。

Original abstract: Parallel LLM test-time scaling techniques (e.g., best-of-$N$) require drawing $N>1$ sequences conditioned on the same input prompt. These methods boost accuracy while exploiting the computational efficiency of batching $N$ generations. However, each sequence in the batch is traditionally generated independently and hence does not reuse intermediate generations, computations, or observations from other sequences. In this paper, we propose LaneRoPE to enable coordination and collaboration among $N>1$ sequences at generation time. LaneRoPE involves two key ideas: (a) an inter-sequence attention mask to make sampling of sequences dependent on one another; and (b) a RoPE extension that injects positional information that captures relative positions between tokens, both within and outside a particular sequence. We evaluate our approach on mathematical reasoning tasks and find promising results: LaneRoPE enables collaboration among sequences, yielding additional accuracy gains under limited generated sequence length. Importantly, since LaneRoPE enables coordination with minimal changes to the underlying LLM architecture and introduces a negligible overhead at inference time, it is appealing to rapidly incorporate parallel reasoning into existing LLM inference pipelines.

Original abstract: Modern analytics systems are fundamentally reactive, requiring users to define queries over increasingly complex and continuously evolving data. The system implements a continuous discovery loop in which agents generate hypotheses, compile them into executable analytics, validate generated artifacts, and produce visualizations and deployable applications. The architecture leverages Apache Kafka for event-driven coordination, Apache Flink for stream processing, and large language models to implement specialized agents. A key contribution is a contract-driven design based on typed intermediate artifacts, enabling modularity, observability, lineage, and safer execution of dynamically generated analytics. ### [56] [Voluntary Collusion with Secret Tools in Competing LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27593v1)
*Xijie Zeng,Frank Rudzicz*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究LLM agent在竞争环境下自愿合谋，涉及多agent协作与工具使用，对agent安全设计有启发。

TL;DR: 本研究首次系统调查了LLM多智能体系统中的自愿串通行为，发现即使明确标注工具不公平，大多数模型仍会采纳并合作，只有明确的伦理框架能部分抑制，但小模型仍易受影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 即使工具被明确描述为不公平和有害，安全对齐的LLM代理仍可能为战略优势而秘密串通，现有对齐方法不足以防止此行为，因此需要系统研究。

Method: 构建两个多智能体环境（Liar's Bar和Cleanup），提供不公平但有利的串通工具，测试12个模型（7B、70B和专有级别）在6种提示变体下的行为。

Result: 大多数代理接受工具并形成串通策略，同时承认其不公平性；公平性标签和基线对齐无效，仅有明确伦理框架可降低采纳率，但小模型仍易受影响。

Conclusion: 防止LLM多智能体系统中自愿串通需要明确的安全规则，而非依赖通用对齐模型。

中文摘要：即使一个工具被明确描述为不公平且对他人有害，表面上符合安全对齐的LLM代理仍然会在这样做能带来战略优势时自愿参与秘密串通。为了研究这一现象，我们引入了一个基于两个战略多智能体环境的实证框架：Liar's Bar（一个竞争性欺骗场景）和Cleanup（一个混合动机的资源管理场景），在这些场景中，代理被提供秘密串通工具，这些工具提供了显著优势，同时明显不利于其他代理。在12个模型（7B、70B和专有规模）和6种提示变体中，我们发现大多数代理一致地接受这些工具并发展出串通策略，同时在接受前明确承认工具的不公平性。我们进一步表明，无论是公平性标签还是基线对齐本身都不能可靠地阻止串通：只有明确的伦理框架能减少采纳，即使如此，较小的模型仍然容易受影响。更广泛地说，我们的工作首次系统性地研究了基于LLM的多智能体系统中自愿串通采纳行为，并表明防止这种行为需要明确的安全保障措施，而非依赖通用对齐。

Original abstract: Even when a tool is explicitly described as unfair and harmful to others, ostensibly safety-aligned LLM agents still voluntarily engage in secret collusion whenever doing so confers a strategic advantage. To investigate this phenomenon, we introduce an empirical framework built on two strategic multi-agent environments: Liar's Bar, a competitive deception scenario, and Cleanup, a mixed-motive resource-management scenario, in which agents are offered secret collusion tools that provide significant advantages while clearly disadvantaging the other agents. Across 12 models (at the 7B, 70B, and proprietary scales) and 6 prompt variants, we find that most agents consistently accept these tools and develop collusive strategies, while explicitly acknowledging the unfairness of the tools before accepting. We further show that neither the unfairness labels nor baseline alignment alone reliably deters collusion: only explicit ethical framing reduces adoption and, even then, smaller models remain susceptible. More broadly, our work presents the first systematic investigation of voluntary collusion adoption in LLM-based multi-agent systems, and suggests that preventing such behaviour requires explicit safeguards rather than reliance on general alignment.

中文摘要：我们介绍了Laguna M.1和Laguna XS.2，两个专家混合（MoE）基础模型，专为长周期、智能编码而构建：M.1总参数量2258亿（每个token激活234亿），XS.2总参数量334亿（激活30亿）。两个模型从零开始端到端训练于我们称之为“模型工厂”的内部系统中：一个紧密集成的版本化数据、训练、评估和推理组件栈，将模型开发转变为工业流程。我们描述了模型工厂的原理和设计选择，并详细介绍了我们模型的端到端训练过程，包括预训练数据和架构、后训练阶段、评估和量化。在智能软件工程和终端基准测试（SWE-bench Verified、SWE-bench Multilingual、SWE-Bench Pro和Terminal-Bench 2.0）上，M.1和XS.2在其各自权重类别中与最先进的开源模型竞争。Laguna XS.2的权重在Apache 2.0许可下发布在https://huggingface.co/collections/poolside/laguna-xs2。

Original abstract: We present Laguna M.1 and Laguna XS.2, two Mixture-of-Experts foundation models built for long-horizon, agentic coding: M.1 has $225.8$B total parameters ($23.4$B activated per token) and XS.2 has $33.4$B total ($3$B activated). Both models were trained from scratch end-to-end inside the same internal system that we refer to as our Model Factory: a tightly-integrated stack of versioned data, training, evaluation, and inference components that turn model development into an industrial process. We describe the principles and design choices of the Model Factory and also detail the end-to-end training process of our models, throughout pre-training data and architecture, post-training stages, evaluation, and quantization.
  On agentic software engineering and terminal benchmarks (SWE-bench Verified, SWE-bench Multilingual, SWE-Bench Pro, and Terminal-Bench 2.0) M.1 and XS.2 are competitive with state-of-the-art open models in their respective weight classes. Laguna XS.2 weights are released under Apache~2.0 at https://huggingface.co/collections/poolside/laguna-xs2.

### [59] [Intelligence as Managed Autonomy: Failure, Escalation, and Governance for Agentic AI Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27628v2)
*Srini Ramaswamy*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出SMARt模型管理agent自主性，包括失败检测、暂停、恢复与监管，直接涉及agent架构与安全。

TL;DR: 提出SMARt模型，通过四层架构形式化管理AI自主性，解决幻觉和不可靠行动问题，并使用Petri网证明其安全性和治理可达性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI系统在不确定性上升时存在无界自主性的架构脆弱性，导致幻觉和持续不合理行动，需通过架构设计引入管理机制。

Method: 提出管理自主性理论，实例化为SMARt四层框架（稳定、元认知、辅助、监管），利用定时有保护的Petri网进行形式化建模，并引入领域特定自适应触发器。

Result: 建立了理论上有界的性质，证明系统能正式强制升级、约束无效输出、确保治理可达性；自适应触发器允许安全可控地扩展操作范围。

Conclusion: 在自主生命周期内形式化失败管理是实现可靠且受治理人工智能的关键步骤。

中文摘要：随着自主和智能AI系统在机器人和人机环境中的规模扩大，管理幻觉和持续但不合理的行动仍然是一个开放挑战。本文并非将这些失败仅归因于模型或对齐限制，而是探索了无界自主性的架构脆弱性——即认为无论不确定性如何上升，智能体都应继续运行的假定。它引入了一种管理自主性理论，通过正式的能力来检测认知漂移、暂停推理、尝试恢复，并最终在可靠性降低时交出控制权。我们通过SMARt（自我管理多层自主推理与受监管/撤销转换）模型实例化该理论，这是一个四层框架，包括稳定、元认知、辅助和监管状态。通过开发一个定时、有保护的Petri网形式化，我们为系统建立了理论上有界的性质，展示了架构如何正式强制升级、约束无效输出，并在指定条件下确保治理可达性。我们进一步分析了如何在不同操作场景（例如，医疗保健、机器人等）中纳入特定领域的触发集，以在满足完整性和合理性标准的前提下系统性地保持安全性。由于这些触发器设计为自适应的，SMARt模型允许智能体操作范围随时间安全、可控地扩展。我们得出结论：在自主生命周期内将失败管理形式化是实现可靠且受治理的人工智能的关键一步。

Original abstract: As autonomous and agentic AI systems scale in robotic and human-machine environments, managing hallucination and persistent but unjustified action remains an open challenge. Rather than attributing these failures solely to model or alignment limitations, this paper explores the architectural vulnerability of unbounded autonomy - the presumption that an agent should continue operating regardless of rising uncertainty. It introduces a theory of managed autonomy that defines intelligent behavior through the formal capacity to detect epistemic drift, suspend reasoning, attempt recovery, and ultimately surrender control when reliability diminishes. We instantiate this theory via the SMARt (Self-Managing Multi-tier Autonomous Reasoning with Regulated/Revoked transitions) model, a four-layer framework featuring Stable, Meta-cognitive, Assisted, and Regulated states. By developing a timed, guarded Petri net formulation, we establish theoretically bounded properties for the system, demonstrating how architecture can formally mandate escalation, constrain invalid outputs, and ensure governance reachability under specified conditions. We further analyze how incorporating domain-specific trigger sets across varied operational settings (e.g., healthcare, robotics, etc.) can systematically preserve safety, assuming completeness and soundness criteria are met. Because these triggers are designed to be adaptive, the SMARt model accommodates the safe, controlled expansion of an agent's operational scope over time. We conclude that formalizing failure management within the autonomy lifecycle is a crucial step toward realizing reliable and governed artificial intelligence.

### [60] [Latent Goal Prediction from Language for Model-Based Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20627v1)
*Samuel Barbeau,Simon Roy,Giovanni Beltrame,Christian Desrosiers,Nicolas Thome*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出从语言预测潜在子目标用于模型规划，可应用于agent长程规划。

TL;DR: LAGO是一个从语言指令预测潜在子目标序列的框架，通过在潜在空间内进行规划并动态更新子目标，实现了长期、精确的规划，避免了复合预测误差问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于世界模型的规划方法存在复合预测误差，且视觉目标缺乏远期引导，语言目标则受限于跨模态噪声或依赖大型生成模型，不适合高采样的规划。

Method: LAGO在潜在空间中从语言指令预测一系列中间子目标，并在线更新这些子目标，使用软最小轨迹成本进行规划，从而动态分解指令为局部可处理的子目标。

Result: 在多个环境和规划时间跨度的评估中，LAGO避免了先前方法的严重性能下降，实现了稳健且精确的长期规划。

Conclusion: LAGO通过将语言指令分解为潜在子目标序列，实现了视觉目标的精确性与语言灵活性的结合，有效解决了长期规划中的瓶颈问题。

中文摘要：使用世界模型进行规划受到复合预测误差和定义可优化目标的难度制约。视觉目标提供精确的局部梯度但缺乏远期引导，而语言灵活但受限于跨模态对齐的噪声或依赖不适合基于模型的规划高采样特性的大型生成模型。为了解决这些挑战，我们引入了LAGO（Latent Goal Prediction from Language），这是一个从语言指令预测中间目标状态序列和动作条件展开的框架，所有操作均在相同的潜在空间内进行。LAGO不是针对单一全局目标进行优化，而是将指令动态分解为明确预测的、局部可处理的潜在子目标。通过在线更新这些子目标并在规划中使用软最小轨迹成本，LAGO使智能体能够遵循长期范围内连贯的潜在轨迹。在多个环境和规划时间跨度的评估中，LAGO避免了先前方法的严重性能下降。通过仅从语言实现稳健且精确的长期规划，LAGO弥合了视觉目标的精确性与文本引导控制的灵活性之间的差距。

Original abstract: Planning with world models is bottlenecked by compounding prediction errors and the difficulty of defining optimizable goals. Visual targets provide precise local gradients but poor distant guidance, while language is flexible yet limited by noisy cross-modal alignment or dependence on large generative models unsuited for the high-sampling nature of model-based planning. To address these challenges, we introduce Latent Goal Prediction from Language (LAGO), a framework that predicts both sequences of intermediate goal states from language instructions and action-conditioned rollouts, all within the same latent space. Rather than optimizing toward a single global objective, LAGO dynamically decomposes instructions into explicitly predicted, locally tractable latent subgoals. By updating these subgoals online and using a soft minimum trajectory cost during planning, LAGO enables an agent to follow coherent latent trajectories over long horizons. Evaluation across multiple environments planning horizons shows that LAGO avoids the sharp degradation of prior methods. By achieving robust and precise long-horizon planning purely from language, LAGO bridges the precision of visual goals with the flexibility of text-guided control.

*Joan Vendrell Gallart,Russell Bent,Michael Grosskopf*

Method: 提出分层控制与学习框架，先蒸馏紧凑模型学习输出模式，再通过预言机-控制器循环在线监督，控制器监控协议和语义性能，触发轻量级微调。

Original abstract: Large Language Models are increasingly deployed inside agentic systems, where they must follow structured protocols, adapt to evolving states, and operate under memory, latency, and cost constraints. In such regimes, prompt extension is unreliable: growing contexts can push compact models outside their effective prompt domain, while deployment-time fine-tuning remains limited by scarce data and compute. We propose a hierarchical control-and-learning framework in which a compact model is first distilled to learn the required output schema, then supervised online by an oracle-controller loop. The controller monitors protocol validity and semantic performance, projects accumulated histories into a feasible prompt domain, and triggers lightweight oracle-supervised fine-tuning under drift. This separates schema learning for communication compatibility from semantic adaptation for task-level correction. We formalize prompt-domain feasibility and attention-induced saturation, motivating control of the effective prompt state rather than reliance on nominal context length. Using Multi-Fidelity Bayesian Optimization as a controlled sequential testbed, we characterize a core deployment failure mode and show improved reliability and cost-efficiency over non-hierarchical, distillation-only, and non-distilled baselines.

Original abstract: Misalignment between claims and their cited evidence is a common failure mode in reports generated by large language models, limiting their reliability in scientific and other high-stakes settings. We present DeepSciVerify, a two-stage pipeline for scientific claim-citation verification that combines abstract-level reasoning with selective escalation to passage-level evidence. The system first verifies claims using the abstract and defers uncertain cases, retrieving and analyzing full-text passages only when necessary. This design leverages complementary behaviors across LLMs, as some models are more conservative while others are more decisive under uncertainty. On the SCitance benchmark, DeepSciVerify achieves 86.7 Micro-F1, outperforming strong abstract-only baselines by +4.5 points while resolving 67% of instances without full-text retrieval. These results suggest that selective evidence escalation improves both accuracy and efficiency in claim-citation verification.
