### [63] [Prefix-Safe Bayesian Belief Tracking for LLM Reasoning Reliability:Separating Calibration from Ranking](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27712v1)
*Zhenghan Song,Yunyi Li,Yulong Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 前缀安全的贝叶斯信念追踪用于LLM推理可靠性估计，可应用于agent推理过程的在线监控。

TL;DR: 提出顺序贝叶斯信念跟踪（SBBT）用于前缀条件下的成功估计，发现标量分数提升概率质量，结构感知证据提升AUROC排名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长推理轨迹在最终答案未知时需要可靠性估计，现有方法缺乏对多种观测类型的统一校准和在线更新机制。

Method: 提出SBBT框架，通过校准观测似然并递归更新二状态信念，统一处理标量分数、文本标记、自我验证信号等多种观测类型。

Result: 在MATH-500、GSM8K、AIME 2025和RIMO-N上，仅分数的SBBT改善Brier分数；结构感知观测在强基线基础上AUROC提升+0.110。

Conclusion: SBBT作为校准感知的在线推理框架有效，且揭示了概率质量与排名的证据分离现象：标量分数主要影响概率质量，结构感知信号仅在强基线未饱和时提升排名。

中文摘要：长推理轨迹在最终答案已知之前需要可靠性估计。我们研究前缀条件下的最终成功估计，即 $P(y=1 \mid o_{1:t})$，使用前缀安全观测。顺序贝叶斯信念跟踪（SBBT）校准观测似然并递归更新一个二状态信念，为标量分数、文本和自我验证标记、隐藏聚类、令牌池探针以及潜在轨迹特征提供了一个通用跟踪器。在生成的开放权重轨迹上（在MATH-500, GSM8K, AIME 2025, 和 RIMO-N上），概率质量和排名分离：仅分数的SBBT通常改善Brier分数，而AUROC提升需要超越强前缀安全基线的结构感知证据。在最强的困难数学设置中，结构感知观测相对于标准前缀安全基线达到了+0.110 AUROC。在相同前缀分类器审计下，MATH-500文本标记和RIMO-N自我验证信号保持正效果。总之，这些发现支持SBBT作为一个校准感知的在线推理框架，并揭示了一个证据机制：标量分数主要支持概率质量，而结构感知前缀信号仅在强前缀安全基线尚未吸收排名证据时支持排名。

Original abstract: Long reasoning traces need reliability estimates before final answers are known. We study prefix-conditioned eventual-success estimation, $P(y=1 \mid o_{1:t})$, using prefix-safe observations. Sequential Bayesian Belief Tracking (SBBT) calibrates observation likelihoods and recursively updates a two-state belief, providing a common tracker for scalar scores, text and self-verification markers, hidden clusters, token-pooling probes, and latent-trajectory features. Across generated open-weight traces on MATH-500, GSM8K, AIME 2025, and RIMO-N, probability quality and ranking separate: score-only SBBT often improves Brier, while AUROC gains require structure-aware evidence beyond strong prefix-safe baselines. In the strongest hard math setting, structure-aware observations reach +0.110 AUROC against standard prefix-safe baselines. Under a same-prefix classifier audit, MATH-500 text markers and RIMO-N self-verification signals remain positive. Together, these findings support SBBT as a calibration-aware online inference framework and expose an evidence regime: scalar scores mainly support probability quality, while structure-aware prefix signals support ranking only when strong prefix-safe baselines have not already absorbed the rank evidence.

</details>


### [64] [A Policy-Driven Runtime Layer for Agentic LLM Serving](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27744v1)
*Rui Zhang,Chaeeun Kim,Liting Hu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 为多agent LLM服务设计的策略驱动运行时层，直接涉及agent serving与缓存优化。

TL;DR: 提出在智能体框架和服务引擎之间插入代理运行时层，通过四个原语实现代理感知策略，实验表明显著提升缓存命中率、降低延迟和提高吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多智能体LLM系统的服务栈缺乏对代理感知策略的支持，许多跨切面策略（如前缀缓存、批处理整形等）难以有效实现。

Method: 在框架和引擎之间引入第三层——代理运行时层，暴露observe, score, predict, act四个原语，以代理身份为共享坐标，支持任意代理感知策略的插入。将九个策略映射到该层，并重点实现了跨会话KV缓存CacheSage，利用在线学习的代理转移矩阵进行基于存活的驱逐和步间预取。

Result: 在五个真实多智能体工作负载上，缓存命中率提升13-37个百分点，平均TTFT降低12-29%，吞吐量提高6-14%。

Conclusion: 代理运行时层的架构变更能够有效解决服务栈中的跨切面策略问题，提升性能。

中文摘要：多智能体LLM系统已成为主流生产工作负载，但服务栈并非为其构建。上层的代理框架知道代理身份、角色、模式和调度结构，但从未看到引擎级事件；下层的服务引擎看到每个事件，但对代理一无所知。大量横切策略依赖于两者：前缀缓存、批处理整形、投机执行、公平性、工具结果记忆化、安全执行等。每个策略都存在于两层之间的接缝中，目前通过一次性修补到某一邻层来解决。我们认为，这个接缝最好通过架构变更而非点修复来解决：在框架和引擎之间插入第三层——代理运行时层，暴露四个原语（观察、评分、预测、行动），任何代理感知策略都可以插入其中，以代理身份作为共享坐标。我们将九个具体策略映射到该层，并深入验证了其中具有最大即时服务成本杠杆的抽象：跨会话的KV缓存，实例化为CacheSage，它在线学习每个工作负载的代理转移矩阵，并用于基于存活的驱逐和步间预取。在五个真实多智能体工作负载上的初步结果显示，与未修改的服务栈相比，缓存命中率提升+13到+37个百分点，平均TTFT降低12%到29%，吞吐量提高6%到14%。

Original abstract: Multi-agent LLM systems have become the dominant production workload, but the serving stack was not built for them. The agent framework above knows agent identities, role, schemas, and dispatch structure but never sees an engine-level event; the serving engine below sees every event but knows nothing about agents. A surprising number of cross-cutting policies depend on both: prefix caching, batch shaping, speculative execution, fairness, tool-result memoization, safety enforcement, and more. Each lives in the seam between the two layers and is currently solved by a one-off patch into one neighbor or the other. We argue this seam is best addressed by an architectural change rather than point fixes: insert a third tier, an agent runtime layer, between the framework and the engine, exposing four primitives (observe, score, predict, act) into which any agent-aware policy plugs, with agent identity as the shared coordinate. We map nine concrete policies onto the layer and validate the abstraction in depth on the one with the largest immediate serving-cost lever: KV caching across sessions, instantiated as CacheSage, which learns the per-workload agent transition matrix online and uses it for survival-based eviction and between-step prefetch. Preliminary results on five real multi-agent workloads show +13 to +37 pp cache hit-rate lift, 12% to 29% lower mean TTFT, and 6% to 14% higher throughput over an unmodified serving stack.

</details>


### [65] [Asking Is Not Enough: Protocol Sensitivity in LLM Confidence Calibration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27752v2)
*Hankyeol Kim,Pilsung Kang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究LLM置信校准的协议敏感性，对agent评估与可靠性有参考价值。

TL;DR: 本文发现LLM的置信度校准测量结果高度依赖于评估协议的选择，两种置信度信号都应视为协议依赖的行为测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对LLM置信度校准的评估往往不明确测量选择的影响，导致比较结果不可靠。

Method: 通过固定口头表达置信度的引出方式，改变token概率分数的测量轴（答案字符串、读取方式、条件上下文），在多个QA基准上评估不同模型。

Result: 条件上下文改变ECE符号和幅度，token读出改变较小，指令模型在默认协议下未显示校准增益，错误答案置信度与正确答案相近。

Conclusion: 两种置信度信号是协议依赖的，应提供详细的报告清单。

中文摘要：LLM置信度校准通常通过比较两种信号来评估：token概率分数和口头表达置信度。这些信号有时被当作模型不确定性的直接读出，但它们的比较取决于很少明确说明的测量选择。在主分析中，我们固定口头表达置信度的引出方式：一个单一的提示模板、概率量表和输出格式。然后我们改变定义口头表达与token比较的测量轴：哪个答案字符串获得token概率分数、如何从答案token中读取该分数、以及在哪个条件上下文中测量。我们在四个QA基准测试中评估该设计，涉及三个开放的7-8B基础/指令模型系列，并使用更大的Qwen2.5变体作为同系列鲁棒性检查。结果比较对这些选择敏感：条件上下文改变了跨设置的ECE差距的符号或幅度，token读出产生较小但仍有符号变化的改变，改变ECE估计器影响很小。在默认的生成答案、裸上下文协议下，指令设置接近平衡，而不是表现出口头表达置信度的大校准增益。在单独的提供答案分析中，表面合理的错误答案获得了与提供的正确答案几乎相同的置信度，表明口头表达置信度也反映了答案的合理性和来源，而不仅仅是正确性。我们主张两种置信度信号都应被视为依赖于协议的测量行为，并提供了一个报告清单，涵盖引出来源、评分答案、token概率读取和条件上下文。

Original abstract: LLM confidence calibration is often evaluated by comparing two signals: token-probability scores and verbalized confidence. These signals are sometimes treated as direct readouts of model uncertainty, but their comparison depends on measurement choices that are rarely made explicit. In the main analysis, we hold the verbalized-confidence elicitation fixed: a single prompt template, probability scale, and output format. We then vary the measurement axes that define the verbalized-vs-token comparison: which answer string receives the token-probability score, how that score is read from the answer tokens, and under which conditioning context it is measured. We evaluate this design on four QA benchmarks across three open 7--8B base/Instruct model families, with larger Qwen2.5 variants as same-family robustness checks. The resulting comparison is sensitive to these choices: conditioning context changes the sign or magnitude of the ECE gap across settings, token readout produces smaller but still sign-moving changes, and changing the ECE estimator has little effect. Under the default generated-answer, bare-context protocol, Instruct settings are close to parity rather than showing a large calibration gain for verbalized confidence. In a separate supplied-answer analysis, surface-plausible wrong answers receive nearly the same confidence as supplied gold answers, suggesting that verbalized confidence also reflects answer plausibility and provenance rather than correctness alone. We argue that both confidence signals should be treated as protocol-dependent behavioral measurements, and provide a reporting checklist covering elicitation provenance, scored answer, token-probability readout, and conditioning context.

</details>


### [66] [SkillGrad: Optimizing Agent Skills Like Gradient Descent](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27760v1)
*Hanyu Wang,Yifan Lan,Bochuan Cao,Lu Lin,Jinghui Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出梯度下降启发的agent技能优化框架，直接相关用户研究的自动代码优化agent。

TL;DR: SkillGrad是一种受梯度下降启发的框架，通过将技能包视为结构化参数进行优化，利用任务损失和文本梯度迭代更新技能，在多个数据集上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能进化方法缺乏明确的优化公式，通常依赖启发式反思，导致技能不可靠、不完整或过时。

Method: 将技能包视为结构化参数，通过梯度下降方式优化：任务执行提供轨迹损失，自动诊断生成文本梯度，动量代理累积诊断模式，LLM修补器执行层感知编辑更新技能包。

Result: 在SpreadsheetBench Verified和WikiTableQuestions上，SkillGrad在两个骨干LLM上平均比最强训练基线高6.7个百分点。

Conclusion: SkillGrad通过梯度下降式的技能优化有效提升了技能质量，动量和对比诊断是关键组件。

中文摘要：Agent技能提供了一种轻量级的方法，通过将可重复使用的程序化知识存储在结构化文件中，使LLM代理能够适应专门领域。然而，无论是从第三方下载还是自行生成，这些技能通常不可靠、不完整或过时。现有的技能进化方法通常通过启发式反思来解决这些缺陷，而没有明确的优化公式。在本文中，我们提出了SkillGrad，一种受梯度下降启发的优化代理技能的框架。SkillGrad将技能包视为结构化参数，以梯度下降方式进行优化：任务执行提供轨迹级别的损失证据，自动诊断随后提供基于文本的梯度，指示修正方向。为了稳定跨迭代的优化，一个动量代理将重复出现的诊断模式累积到持久内存覆盖中。最后，基于LLM的修补器通过应用层感知编辑来执行技能包的参数更新。在SpreadsheetBench Verified和WikiTableQuestions上的评估表明，SkillGrad在两个骨干LLM上一致优于基于训练的技能进化基线，平均比最强的基于训练的基线提高了6.7个百分点。消融实验进一步显示，动量和对比诊断都对最终技能质量有贡献。

Original abstract: Agent skills provide a lightweight way to adapt LLM agents to specialized domains by storing reusable procedural knowledge in structured files. However, whether downloaded from third parties or self-generated, these skills are often unreliable, incomplete, or outdated. Existing skill-evolution methods often address these deficiencies through heuristic reflections without an explicit optimization formulation. In this paper, we propose SkillGrad, a gradient-descent-inspired framework for optimizing agent skills. SkillGrad treats the skill package as a structured parameter to optimize in a gradient descent fashion: task executions provide trajectory-level loss evidence, automatic diagnoses then provide text-based gradients that indicate the correction directions. To stabilize optimization across iterations, a momentum agent accumulates recurring diagnostic patterns into a persistent memory overlay. Finally, an LLM-based patcher executes the parameter update by applying layer-aware edits to the skill package. Evaluated on SpreadsheetBench Verified and WikiTableQuestions, SkillGrad consistently outperforms training-based skill evolution baselines across two backbone LLMs, improving over the strongest training-based baseline by $6.7$ percentage points on average. Ablations further show that momentum and contrastive diagnosis both contribute to the final skill quality.

</details>


### [67] [PEAM: Parametric Embodied Agent Memory through Contrastive Internalization of Experience in Minecraft](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27762v2)
*Yuchen Guo,Junli Gong,Weicheng Wang,Hongmin Cai,Yiu-ming Cheung,Weifeng Su*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出具身agent记忆框架，将经验内化为参数技能，涉及长期任务执行和持续学习，方法可迁移至coding agent的技能内化。

TL;DR: PEAM通过将经验内化为参数技能，结合慢速LLM和快速参数模块，并利用失败信号进行联合学习，实现了无需检索的参数级持续学习，在Minecraft中提升了长程任务性能并减少了遗忘。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有具身智能体记忆方法要么依赖检索导致效率低下，要么采用参数记忆但易出现灾难性遗忘。PEAM旨在通过将经验内化为参数技能，实现高效、自演化的记忆机制。

Method: PEAM由慢速LLM（开放式推理）和快速参数模块（反射式执行）组成；快速模块采用多模态MoE-LoRA架构，每类任务有独立适配器；通过联合行为克隆和对比目标内化失败-修正轨迹；引入参数化价值评分和自触发巩固机制控制内化时机。

Result: 在Minecraft实验中，PEAM在长程任务上表现更优，有效缓解了先前技能的遗忘，并在参数化与检索效率上优于基线方法。

Conclusion: PEAM通过参数内化记忆实现智能体自演化，在持续学习效率和任务性能上均取得显著提升。

中文摘要：我们提出PEAM，一个在Minecraft中的参数化具身智能体记忆框架，它将智能体记忆从推理时检索转变为通过经验内化的参数驻留技能。PEAM将一个慢速的深思熟虑的LLM用于开放式推理，与一个快速的参数化模块配对，用于反射式执行巩固的技能。快速模块是一个多模态的混合专家LoRA架构，具有按类别物理隔离的适配器，实现了无灾难性遗忘的参数级持续学习。我们将失败视为第一类训练信号：失败-修正轨迹对通过联合行为克隆和对比目标进行内化，因此智能体不仅学习成功的是什么，还学习修正后的动作与失败的动作有何不同。为了管理巩固，PEAM引入了参数化价值评分来决定哪些经验应该被内化，以及一个无尺度自触发巩固机制来决定何时内化，无需任务特定的手动调参阈值，使得智能体自演化，因为触发器跨任务分布转移而无需重新调参。在Minecraft中的实验表明，PEAM提高了长程任务性能，减轻了先前巩固技能的遗忘，并且相比于基于检索的具身智能体和参数化记忆变体，提高了参数化与检索的效率。

Original abstract: We present PEAM, a Parametric Embodied Agent Memory framework in Minecraft that transforms agent memory from inference-time retrieval into parameter-resident skills internalized through experience. PEAM pairs a slow deliberative LLM for open-ended reasoning with a fast parametric module for reflexive execution of consolidated skills. The fast module is a multimodal Mixture-of-Experts LoRA architecture with per-category physically isolated adapters, enabling parameter-level continual learning without catastrophic forgetting. We treat failure as a first-class training signal: failure--correction trajectory pairs are internalized through a joint behavioral-cloning and contrastive objective, so the agent learns not only what succeeds but also how corrected actions differ from failed ones. To govern consolidation, PEAM introduces a parameterization-worthiness score for deciding which experience should be internalized, and a scale-free self-triggered consolidation mechanism for deciding when to internalize without task-specific hand-tuned thresholds, making the agent self-evolving as the trigger transfers across task distributions without re-tuning. Experiments in Minecraft show that PEAM improves long-horizon task performance, mitigates forgetting on previously consolidated skills, and improves parametric-versus-retrieval efficiency over retrieval-based embodied agents and parametric memory variants.

</details>


### [68] [Got a Secret? LLM Agents Can't Keep It: Evaluating Privacy in Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27766v1)
*Aman Priyanshu,Supriti Vijay,Esha Pahwa*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 评估多agent社会交互中的隐私泄露，提供agent安全设计启示。

TL;DR: 多轮社交交互中的LLM代理隐私泄露风险显著高于单轮评估，且具有社会传染性，静态基准低估了真实部署风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM安全评估主要在隔离环境中进行，但实际部署中AI代理处于持续的社会环境，需要评估社会互动对隐私安全的影响。

Method: 构建Moltbook风格模拟平台，让数千个LLM代理在模拟一个月内跨社区交互，通过多轮社会评估测量隐私泄露。

Result: 多轮评估泄露率从19.95%升至45.30%；观察同伴泄露后敏感信息泄露概率增加8倍；隐私指令使泄露率降至仍高于37.8%。

Conclusion: 静态聊天基准低估代理部署风险，社会背景足以诱发单轮评估无法发现的敏感信息泄露。

中文摘要：LLM安全评估主要是在隔离环境中测试模型，然而部署的AI代理越来越多地与其他代理一起在持久的社会环境中运行。我们引入了一个Moltbook风格的模拟平台，其中数千个LLM代理在模拟的一个月内跨社区互动，并使用该平台评估隐私作为下游安全问题在不同程度社会压力下的表现。我们发现，从单轮到多轮社会评估会放大隐私泄露（OpenAI模型上从CIMemories的19.95%到我们方法的45.30%），且泄露具有社会传染性，代理在观察到同伴泄露后泄露敏感信息的可能性是8倍，而明确的隐私指令会减少但无法消除这种效应，即使在有保护措施的情况下泄露率仍高于37.8%。我们的研究结果表明，基于静态聊天的安全基准系统性地低估了代理部署中的风险，仅社会背景就足以引发单轮评估永远不会发现的敏感信息泄露。

Original abstract: LLM safety evaluations predominantly test models in isolation, yet deployed AI agents increasingly operate within persistent social environments alongside other agents. We introduce a Moltbook-style simulation platform where thousands of LLM agents interact across communities over a simulated month, and use it to evaluate privacy as a downstream safety concern under varying degrees of social pressure. We find that shifting from single turn to multi turn social evaluation amplifies privacy violations (CIMemories 19.95% to Ours 45.30% across OpenAI models), that leakage is socially contagious, with agents 8 times more likely to disclose sensitive information after observing a peer do so, and that explicit privacy instructions reduce but do not eliminate this effect, leaving leakage rates above 37.8% even with safeguards. Our findings suggest that static chat based safety benchmarks systematically underestimate risks in agentic deployment, and that social context alone is sufficient to elicit sensitive disclosures that single turn evaluations would never surface.

### [69] [Auditable Decision Models with Learned Abstention and Real-Time Steering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27768v1)
*Sankaranarayanan Palamadai Chandrasekaran*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出含TBD的决策控制模型，支持审计与推理时路由，可迁移至agent安全控制。

TL;DR: 提出EvaluatorDPT模型，通过学习推迟决策（TBD）实现可审计的AI操作决策控制，在测试集上达到82.6%准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI系统在处理不确定性时，强制分类器忽略不确定性，生成模型输出难以审计，需要一种显式、可路由、受策略约束且可审计的决策控制。

Method: 使用变压器编码器，主决策头输出YES/NO/TBD（TBD作为学习到的推迟结果），并带有价值观和情感辅助通道；通过操作阈值和辅助信号在推理时控制决策。

Result: 在44,597条测试样本上，准确率82.60%，宏F1 82.52%，各类F1分别为YES:83.14%, NO:84.86%, TBD:79.56%；验证集ECE=0.0338。

Conclusion: 贡献了一个受限执行接口，其中推迟是学习得到的，推理路由可检查，辅助信号支持审计行为控制，且评估证据可复现和外部审查。

中文摘要：生产型AI系统通常在不完整、冲突或不充分的证据下运行。强制分类器将此类情况压缩为动作标签，而生成式系统可能产生难以解释为可审计执行决策的输出。我们研究AI系统的操作决策控制，其中不确定性必须被明确地路由、受策略约束且可审计，而不是隐藏在强制预测或自由生成中。我们提出了EvaluatorDPT，一个受限决策控制模型，预测YES、NO或TBD，其中TBD被学习为推迟结果，而不仅仅是作为事后置信规则添加。该模型使用一个变压器编码器，带有一个主要受限决策头以及用于价值观和情感/情绪的结构化辅助通道。接口在形式上是领域无关的：部署领域提供证据和政策阈值，而模型输出一个受限分布，该分布可以通过记录的操作阈值和（经验证后）辅助语义信号在推理时进行控制。对于评估的模型版本，我们报告了在留出验证集和测试集上的决策性能；辅助情绪指标被省略，因为情绪头在此评估中被禁用。在留出测试集（n=44,597）上，模型达到准确率=0.8260和宏F1=0.8252，各类别F1分别为0.8314（YES）、0.8486（NO）和0.7956（TBD）。评估记录还包括校准证据（验证集上ECE=0.0338）、阈值扫描输出、多种子稳定性检查、混淆矩阵和可重复性命令。我们的主要贡献是一个受限执行接口，其中推迟是学习得到的，推理时路由保持可检查，辅助信号提供了可审计行为控制的路径，并且评估证据支持外部审查。

Original abstract: Production AI systems often operate with incomplete, conflicting, or insufficient evidence. Forced classifiers collapse such cases into action labels, while generative systems can produce outputs that are difficult to interpret as auditable execution decisions. We study operational decision control for AI systems, where uncertainty must be explicitly routable, policy-governed, and auditable rather than hidden inside forced predictions or free-form generation. We present EvaluatorDPT, a bounded decision-control model that predicts YES, NO, or TBD, where TBD is learned as a deferral outcome rather than added only as a post-hoc confidence rule. The model uses a transformer encoder with a primary bounded-decision head and structured auxiliary channels for values and emotions/sentiments. The interface is domain-agnostic in form: a deployment domain supplies evidence and policy thresholds, while the model emits a bounded distribution that can be controlled at inference time through recorded operating thresholds and, when validated, auxiliary semantic signals. For the evaluated model version, we report decision performance on held-out validation and test splits; auxiliary emotion metrics are omitted because the emotion head is disabled for this evaluation. On the held-out test split (n=44,597), the model achieves Accuracy = 0.8260 and Macro F1 = 0.8252, with per-class F1 of 0.8314 (YES), 0.8486 (NO), and 0.7956 (TBD). The evaluation record also includes calibration evidence (ECE = 0.0338 on validation), threshold-sweep outputs, multi-seed stability checks, confusion matrices, and reproducibility commands. Our main contribution is a bounded execution interface in which deferral is learned, inference-time routing remains inspectable, auxiliary signals provide a path to auditable behavior control, and evaluation evidence supports external review.

</details>


<div id='cs.AR'></div>

# cs.AR [[Back]](#toc)

### [70] [AssertLLM2: A Comprehensive LLM Benchmark for Assertion Generation from Design Specifications](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27472v1)
*Yuchao Wu,Wenji Fang,Jing Wang,Wenkai Li,Ziyan Guo,Zhiyao Xie*

Main category: cs.AR

Selection reason: LLM用于硬件断言生成，涉及代码生成与验证，直接相关code agent。

TL;DR: 提出AssertLLM2，一个包含真实设计和多种评估指标的断言生成基准，支持错误预防和错误狩猎两种场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有断言生成基准受限于不现实的任务表述、弱规范输入和过于简化的评估。

Method: AssertLLM2包含83个跨13个功能类别的真实设计，每个设计提供结构化规范、验证过的黄金RTL和系统突变的错误RTL变体，支持错误预防和错误狩猎两种设置，并采用涵盖语法有效性、形式可证明性、覆盖率和基于突变错误检测的严格评估框架。

Result: 基准包含83个真实设计，13个功能类别，以及针对断言生成的多维度评估（语法、形式验证、覆盖率和突变检测）。

Conclusion: AssertLLM2实现了对断言生成更现实和广泛的评估，为实际硬件验证中的LLMs建立了严格的基线。

中文摘要：基于断言的验证（ABV）是现代硬件设计的基石，但手动将设计意图转换为正式的SystemVerilog断言（SVA）仍然劳动密集且容易出错。尽管大语言模型（LLM）在自动化这一过程中显示出潜力，但现有的基准测试仍然受到不现实的任务表述、弱规范输入和过于简化评估的限制。为了解决这些限制，我们引入了AssertLLM2，这是一个用于硬件验证中现实断言生成的开源基准测试。AssertLLM2包含83个跨13个功能类别的真实设计。对于每个设计，该基准测试提供了结构化的设计规范、经过验证的依赖完整的黄金RTL，以及系统突变的错误RTL变体。这些支持两种实际设置：错误预防，即从规范生成断言以防止设计错误；以及错误狩猎，即生成断言以暴露预期行为与错误实现之间的差异。据我们所知，AssertLLM2是第一个明确使用错误RTL作为输入来评估错误检测能力的基准测试。AssertLLM2进一步采用了一个更严格的评估框架，涵盖语法有效性、形式可证明性、覆盖率和基于突变的错误检测。我们的基准测试实现了对断言生成的更现实和广泛的评估，并为实际硬件验证中的最先进大语言模型建立了严格的基准。

Original abstract: Assertion-based verification (ABV) is a cornerstone of modern hardware design, yet manually translating design intent into formal SystemVerilog Assertions (SVAs) remains labor-intensive and error-prone. While Large Language Models (LLMs) show promise for automating this process, existing benchmarks remain limited by unrealistic task formulations, weak specification inputs, and oversimplified evaluation. To address these limitations, we introduce AssertLLM2, an open-source benchmark for realistic assertion generation in hardware verification. AssertLLM2 contains 83 real-world designs across 13 functional categories. For each design, the benchmark provides a structured design specification, a verified dependency-complete golden RTL, and systematically mutated buggy RTL variants. These support two practical settings: bug-prevention, where assertions are generated from specifications to guard against design errors, and bug-hunting, where assertions are generated to expose discrepancies between intended behavior and faulty implementations. To the best of our knowledge, AssertLLM2 is the first benchmark to explicitly use buggy RTL as input to evaluate bug-detection capability. AssertLLM2 further adopts a more rigorous evaluation framework spanning syntactic validity, formal provability, coverage, and mutation-based bug detection. Our benchmark enables a more realistic and extensive assessment of assertion generation and establishes rigorous baselines for state-of-the-art LLMs in practical hardware verification.

</details>

### [71] [ProDebug: An Automated Debugging System for Prolog](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27124v1)
*Ricardo Brancas,Vasco Manquinho,Ruben Martins*

Main category: cs.PL

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: ProDebug结合LLM与频谱和变异技术自动调试Prolog作业，在1499个错误提交上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Prolog调试困难，大班教学中缺乏及时个性化反馈，现有自动调试工具不足。

Method: 提出ProDebug工具，结合基于频谱的错误定位、基于变异的错误定位和LLM推理进行故障检测，并使用基于变异的技术和LLM生成修复。

Result: 在1499个错误学生提交上的评估展示了自动化LLM增强反馈系统的潜力。

Conclusion: 结合LLM的自动调试工具可有效扩展对声明式编程教育的支持。

中文摘要：Prolog是一种众所周知的声明式编程语言，常用于逻辑与推理的入门课程。然而，许多学生发现Prolog具有挑战性，因为它缺乏命令式语言中常见的调试机制。在大班教学中，这种困难因难以提供及时且个性化的反馈而加剧。在本工作中，我们提出了ProDebug，这是第一个将大型语言模型（LLM）与基于频谱和基于变异的技术相结合，用于Prolog作业自动调试的工具。ProDebug自动识别学生Git提交中的错误并建议修复。错误检测使用三种方法——基于频谱、基于变异和LLM推理——而修复则使用基于变异的技术和LLM生成。我们在一个本科编程课程的1499个有错误的学生提交上的评估，展示了自动化、LLM增强的反馈系统在扩展对声明式编程教育支持方面的潜力。

Original abstract: Prolog is a well-known declarative programming language commonly used in introductory courses on logic and reasoning. However, many students find Prolog challenging because it lacks the familiar debugging mechanisms found in imperative languages. In large classes, this difficulty is exacerbated by the challenge of providing timely and personalized feedback to students.
  In this work, we introduce ProDebug, the first tool to combine Large Language Models (LLMs) with spectrum-based and mutation-based techniques for automated debugging of Prolog assignments. ProDebug automatically identifies faults and proposes bug repairs for student Git submissions. Faults are detected using three approaches--spectrum-based, mutation-based, and LLM reasoning--while repairs are generated using mutation-based techniques and LLMs. Our evaluation on 1499 buggy student submissions from a bachelor's level programming class demonstrates the potential of automated, LLM-augmented feedback systems to scale support for declarative programming education.

### [72] [Agentic Separation Logic Specification Synthesis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27531v1)
*Tarun Suresh,David Korczynski,Julien Vanegue*

Main category: cs.PL

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Spec-Agent是一个针对大型C++代码库的规范合成系统，通过静态分析、模糊测试和LLM迭代优化，以高准确率（85%）合成多种逻辑规范，且成本更低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM方法无法同时扩展到大型C++代码库、产生能捕获系统代码特性（如动态内存）的表达性规范，并系统性地验证这些规范。

Method: Spec-Agent使用静态分析和运行时堆追踪为每个函数选择合适的目标规范语言（命题逻辑、一阶逻辑、命题分离逻辑、一阶分离逻辑），将现有功能测试泛化为模糊测试工具，并通过反例引导反馈迭代优化LLM生成的候选规范。

Result: 在数百万行代码的开源C++代码库上，Spec-Agent为目标函数的85%合成了有效规范，无假阳性，性能优于Claude Code Opus 4.6且令牌成本低10倍。

Conclusion: Spec-Agent能够有效合成表达性强且经过验证的规范，为大型C++代码库的规范合成提供了一种可扩展且低成本的解决方案。

中文摘要：规范合成——从程序实现和自然语言中自动推断出形式规范的任务——对于重构、转译、优化和验证非常重要，但对于大型C++代码库来说仍然是一个开放的挑战。现有的基于LLM的方法无法同时扩展到此类代码库，无法产生足以捕获系统代码特性（如动态内存和堆分配数据结构）的表达性规范，也无法系统地验证这些规范以排除不正确的候选规范。我们提出了Spec-Agent，一个用于在大型C++代码库中合成表达性强且经过充分验证的规范的系统。Spec-Agent针对一个规范语言阶梯：命题逻辑、一阶逻辑、命题分离逻辑和一阶分离逻辑。对于每个函数，Spec-Agent使用静态分析和运行时堆追踪来选择合适的目标规范语言，将现有的功能测试泛化为模糊测试工具，并通过反例引导的反馈迭代地优化LLM生成的候选规范。我们在包含数百万行代码的开源C++代码库上评估了Spec-Agent。Spec-Agent为目标函数的85%合成了有效的规范，在模糊测试和专家验证下未观察到假阳性，其性能优于Claude Code Opus 4.6，同时令牌成本降低10倍。

Original abstract: Specification synthesis, the task of automatically inferring formal specifications from program implementations and natural language, is important for refactoring, transpilation, optimization, and verification, yet remains an open challenge for large C++ repositories. Existing LLM-based approaches fail to simultaneously scale to such repositories, produce specifications expressive enough to capture systems-code features such as dynamic memory and heap-allocated data structures, and systematically validate those specifications to rule out incorrect candidates. We present Spec-Agent, an agentic system for synthesizing expressive, well-validated specifications across large C++ codebases. Spec-Agent targets a ladder of specification languages: propositional logic, first-order logic, propositional separation logic, and first-order separation logic. For each function, Spec-Agent uses static analysis and runtime heap tracing to select the appropriate target specification language, generalizes existing functional tests into fuzz harnesses, and iteratively refines LLM-generated candidates via counterexample-guided feedback. We evaluate Spec-Agent on open source C++ codebases comprising millions of lines of code. Spec-Agent synthesizes valid specifications for 85% of target functions, with no false positives observed under fuzzing and expert validation, outperforming Claude Code Opus 4.6 at 10x lower token cost.

</details>

### [73] [ReasonOps: A Unified Operational Paradigm for Trustworthy Verified LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27014v1)
*Adnan Rashid*

Main category: cs.LO

Selection reason: 提出推理运维范式（ReasonOps），关注验证与可靠性，可迁移至coding agent的可靠执行。

TL;DR: 提出ReasonOps范式，将推理视为持续监控、可验证、可靠性的操作过程，整合多种推理步骤，提升可信度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理系统存在逻辑不一致、幻觉、可靠性不足等问题，且相关研究分散在多个社区，缺乏统一范式。

Method: ReasonOps范式，将推理视为持续监控、可验证、可靠性的操作过程，整合语义解释、自动形式化、符号推理、定理证明、运行时保障、概率可靠性估计和自适应修正到统一生命周期。

Result: 通过自动制动系统分析示例展示了ReasonOps架构和工作流程。

Conclusion: 操作推理范式如ReasonOps可能成为下一代可信AI生态系统的基础设施。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）已将人工智能从主要生成系统转变为日益强大的推理智能体。最近在定理证明、自动形式化、符号推理和工具增强语言模型方面的进展表明，机器辅助形式推理取得了实质性进展。然而，当前的推理系统仍然存在隐藏的逻辑不一致、幻想的符号转换、无支持的定理应用以及有限的可信性保证。现有方法在形式验证、运行时保障、神经符号推理和可信人工智能（AI）研究社区之间仍然分散。本文介绍了ReasonOps，一种统一的、可信的已验证推理系统的操作范式。受DevOps和MLOps等操作生态系统的启发，ReasonOps将推理视为一个持续监控、可验证、注重可靠性的操作过程，而非孤立的推理任务。提出的范式将语义解释、自动形式化、符号推理、定理证明、运行时保障、概率可靠性估计和自适应修正整合到一个统一的推理生命周期中。本文进一步提出了ReasonOps架构，使用自动制动系统分析示例展示了其工作流程，并讨论了其在未来安全关键自主AI系统中的潜在作用。我们认为，诸如ReasonOps之类的操作推理范式可能成为下一代可信AI生态系统的基础设施。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have transformed artificial intelligence from primarily generative systems into increasingly capable reasoning agents. Recent advances in theorem proving, autoformalization, symbolic reasoning, and tool-augmented language models demonstrate substantial progress toward machine-assisted formal reasoning. However, current reasoning systems still suffer from hidden logical inconsistencies, hallucinated symbolic transitions, unsupported theorem applications, and limited reliability guarantees. Existing approaches remain fragmented across formal verification, runtime assurance, neuro-symbolic reasoning and trustworthy Artificial Intelligence (AI) research communities.
  This paper introduces ReasonOps, a unified operational paradigm for trustworthy verified reasoning systems. Inspired by operational ecosystems such as DevOps and MLOps, ReasonOps treats reasoning as a continuously monitored, verifiable, reliability-aware operational process rather than an isolated inference task. The proposed paradigm integrates semantic interpretation, autoformalization, symbolic reasoning, theorem proving, runtime assurance, probabilistic reliability estimation, and adaptive correction into a unified reasoning lifecycle. The paper further presents the ReasonOps architecture, demonstrates its workflow using an autonomous braking system analysis example, and discusses its potential role in future safety-critical autonomous AI systems. We argue that operational reasoning paradigms such as ReasonOps may become foundational infrastructure for next-generation trustworthy AI ecosystems.

</details>


### [74] [Automating Formal Verification with Agent-Guided Tree Search](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27485v1)
*Leo Yao*

Main category: cs.LO

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文评估了LLM在Lean中生成验证代码的现状，并提出了基于搜索的代理方法，其中上下文树搜索在中等难度规范上优于基线代理，而基线代理在困难规范上仍具优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 形式化验证成本高、使用少，LLM有望加速，但需要更好的方法提升验证性能。

Method: 在vericoding-benchmark上复现并加入mathlib搜索的代理循环，设计状态和上下文两种树搜索编排器。

Result: GPT-5.4达95.0%正确率；上下文搜索以更低成本解决更多中等难度规范，基线代理在困难规范上更优。

Conclusion: 搜索结构具有选择性优势，需更挑战性的基准推动进步。

中文摘要：形式化验证为可证明正确的软件提供了一条路径，但编写经过验证的代码仍然成本高昂，以至于该技术很少在生产中使用。最近的大型语言模型可以加速这一工作，而最近的基准测试衡量了它们将规范转换为代码和机器可验证的正确性证明的能力。本论文评估了在Lean中此类LLM驱动的验证代码生成（“vericoding”）的现状，并开发了基于搜索的方法以提高验证性能。我们首先在当前的跨供应商模型池中复现了vericoding-benchmark Lean排行榜的一个子集，发现非推理性能在美国闭源模型上大致保持稳定，而开放权重模型略有改善。我们更新了vericoding-benchmark的迭代方法，引入了一个配备mathlib搜索的代理循环，发现模型性能大幅提升，并随代理预算扩展。GPT-5.4在423个规范上以K=50次LLM调用几乎达到基准饱和，正确率为95.0%。然后，我们设计了两种代理引导的树搜索形式：一种基于状态的编排器，在部分证明状态上分支；另一种基于上下文的编排器，在完整的子代理上下文上分支。与代理基线相比，基于上下文的设计以更低的令牌成本解决了更广泛的中间难度规范，而代理基线在最困难的规范上仍保持优势，在这些规范中，不间断的迭代最为重要。我们得出结论，搜索结构相对于强大的代理基线具有选择性优势，并且从现代代码中提取更具挑战性的基准对于衡量和推动自动形式化验证的进一步进展至关重要。代码可通过联系作者leoy@mit.edu获取。

Original abstract: Formal verification offers a path to provably correct software, but writing verified code remains expensive enough that the technique is rarely used in production. Recent large language models can accelerate this work, and recent benchmarks measure their ability to translate specifications into code and machine-checked proofs of correctness. This thesis evaluates the state of such LLM-driven verified-code generation ("vericoding") in Lean and develops search-based methods for improving verification performance. We first reproduce a subset of the vericoding-benchmark Lean leaderboard on a current cross-vendor model pool, finding that non-reasoning performance remains roughly steady on US closed-source models while open-weight models have slightly improved. We update the iterative methodology of vericoding-benchmark with an agentic loop equipped with mathlib search, finding that model performance greatly improves and scales with agent budget. GPT-5.4 nearly saturates the benchmark at 95.0% on 423 specs with $K=50$ LLM calls. We then design two agent-directed tree-search formulations: a state-based orchestrator that branches on partial-proof states, and a context-based orchestrator that branches on full subagent contexts. Compared against the agent baseline, the context-based design solves a wider range of intermediate-difficulty specs at lower token cost, while the agent baseline retains an advantage on the hardest specs, where uninterrupted iteration matters most. We conclude that search structure has selective advantages over a strong agent baseline, and that more challenging benchmarks drawn from modern code are important to measure and drive further progress in automated formal verification.
  Code available upon request by contacting the author at leoy@mit.edu.

</details>

### [75] [Efficient Safety Benchmarking via Item Response Theory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20626v1)
*Fabio Spagliardi,Mírian Silva,Ayan Datta,Aiden Zhou,Vamshi Bonagiri,Diogo Cruz*

Main category: cs.CY

Selection reason: 利用项目反应理论高效安全评测，方法可迁移至agent benchmark设计。

TL;DR: 本文提出使用项目反应理论和自适应项目选择方法，显著降低语言模型安全基准测试的评估成本，同时保持排序准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全基准测试的静态范式将所有项目视为同等信息，导致评估成本高昂且效率低下，尤其是在对抗性、高异质性的项目中。

Method: 采用项目反应理论（IRT）分析安全基准数据结构，并引入自适应项目选择策略，动态挑选信息量大的项目；同时提出提取固定信息子集的方法。

Result: 自适应选择能降低至少80%的评估成本（部分基准达99.9%），固定子集方法可节省高达99.8%的成本，且排序与完整基准高度一致（斯皮尔曼ρ>90%）。

Conclusion: 心理测量方法能够有效减少安全基准测试的评估成本，提升效率，且不牺牲评估质量。

中文摘要：语言模型的安全基准测试通常采用静态评估范式，将所有项目视为对所有模型具有相同的信息量，这一假设对于对抗性、高度异质的安全项目尤其成问题。如果完整应用于现代基准套件，当前评估程序需要约10^5个响应，其中大部分提供的排序信号很少。我们分析了一套广泛使用的安全基准，并提出了三项有助于更高效安全评估的贡献。第一，我们表明项目反应理论（IRT）能够恢复安全基准上的可解释结构，能力估计能够区分在原始安全指标上聚集于天花板水平的模型之间的差异。第二，我们表明自适应项目选择（根据模型响应动态选择信息量大的项目）能够近似完整基准的排序，同时将评估成本降低至少80%（在斯皮尔曼ρ>90%可实现的基准上），在AIR-Bench 2024上降低高达99.9%。第三，我们介绍了一种实用的方法，用于提取一个固定的、信息量大的项目子集，该子集可跨模型重用，作为自适应选择的替代方案，在AIR-Bench 2024上节省高达99.8%的成本。这些结果共同表明，心理测量方法能够在安全评估管道的各个环节实现基准感知的评估成本降低。

Original abstract: Safety benchmarks for language models are typically evaluated using static paradigms that treat all items as equally informative for all models, an assumption that is particularly problematic for adversarial, highly heterogeneous safety items. Applied in full to modern benchmark suites, the current evaluation procedures would require on the order of $10^5$ responses, most of which provide little ranking signal. We analyze a suite of widely used safety benchmarks and make three contributions toward more efficient safety evaluation. First, we show that Item Response Theory (IRT) recovers interpretable structure on safety benchmarks, with ability estimates resolving differences among models that cluster at the ceiling of raw safety metrics. Second, we show that adaptive item selection, which dynamically chooses informative items for each model based on its responses, approximates full-benchmark rankings while reducing evaluation cost by at least 80% on benchmarks where Spearman's $ρ>$90% with full-benchmark is attainable, and by up to 99.9% on AIR-Bench 2024. Third, we introduce a practical procedure for extracting a fixed, informative subset of items reusable across models, providing an alternative to adaptive selection with savings of up to 99.8% on AIR-Bench 2024. Together, these results establish that psychometric methods enable benchmark-aware reductions in evaluation costs across the safety evaluation pipeline.

</details>

# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [76] [Qiskit QuantumKatas: Adapting Microsoft's Quantum Computing exercises for LLM evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27210v1)
*Juan Cruz-Benito,Ismael Faro*

Main category: quant-ph

Selection reason: 量子编程LLM benchmark，虽领域特殊但评估方法对coding agent评测有启发

TL;DR: 将QuantumKatas改编到Qiskit并构建LLM基准，评估16个模型发现：区分模型能力有效，模型擅长已知算法但弱于问题编码，思维链提示效果双峰。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前缺乏系统评估LLM在量子计算能力上的标准化基准，现有课程适配和评估框架不足。

Method: 基于QuantumKatas教学设计，将350个任务从Q#适配到Qiskit，每个任务含自然语言提示、规范解和确定性测试，通过39,200次模型运行评估7种提示配置下16个LLM。

Result: 最佳配置通过率32.3%-83.1%，前沿与开源模型差距26.1 pp；算法实现任务通过率高（SimonsAlgorithm 82.1%），问题编码任务低（SolveSATWithGrover 34.4%）；链式思维提示对部分模型有利但整体不如少样本5（56.3% vs 57.8%）。

Conclusion: 基准可有效评估LLM量子编程能力，揭示模型优势与不足，发布资源支持后续研究。

中文摘要：我们将Microsoft的QuantumKatas（一个成熟的量子计算课程）从Q#改编到Qiskit（最广泛采用的量子计算框架），并打包成一个评估框架用于系统性的LLM评估。生成的基准测试包含26个类别的350个任务，涵盖从基本门到高级算法（Grover、Simon、Deutsch-Jozsa）、纠错、密钥分发和量子游戏。每个任务包括自然语言提示、规范解和通过经典电路模拟进行确定性测试验证。通过基于QuantumKatas经过验证的教学设计而不是从头创建任务，我们继承了原则性的难度递进和全面的概念覆盖，同时贡献了框架适配、评估基础设施和实证分析。我们评估了7种提示配置下的16个LLM——总共39,200次模型运行——以展示基准测试的实用性。三个关键发现：（1）基准测试有效区分模型能力，最佳配置通过率从32.3%到83.1%不等，前沿模型与开源模型平均差距26.1个百分点；（2）模型在实现已知算法方面表现良好（SimonsAlgorithm 82.1%，BasicGates 81.6%），但在问题编码方面困难（SolveSATWithGrover 34.4%，DistinguishUnitaries 40.0%）；（3）思维链提示表现出中等程度的双峰效应——对三个模型（其中两个根据供应商文档明确进行了推理调优）是最佳策略，但对其他模型则降低了性能，整体处于中游（平均56.3%），落后于少样本5（57.8%）。我们发布了基准测试、评估框架和基线结果，以支持量子计算中LLM能力的研究。

Original abstract: We adapt Microsoft's QuantumKatas -- a well-established quantum computing curriculum -- from Q# to Qiskit, the most widely-adopted quantum computing framework, and package it with an evaluation framework for systematic LLM assessment. The resulting benchmark comprises 350 tasks across 26 categories, spanning fundamental gates through advanced algorithms (Grover's, Simon's, Deutsch-Jozsa), error correction, key distribution, and quantum games. Each task includes a natural language prompt, canonical solution, and deterministic test verification via classical circuit simulation. By building on the QuantumKatas' proven pedagogical design rather than creating tasks from scratch, we inherit a principled difficulty progression and comprehensive concept coverage while contributing the framework adaptation, evaluation infrastructure, and empirical analysis. We evaluate 16 LLMs across 7 prompting configurations -- a total of 39,200 model runs -- to demonstrate the benchmark's utility. Three key findings emerge: (1) the benchmark effectively differentiates model capabilities, with best-configuration pass rates ranging from 32.3% to 83.1% and a 26.1 pp average gap between frontier and open-source models; (2) models perform well at implementing known algorithms (SimonsAlgorithm 82.1%, BasicGates 81.6%) but struggle with problem encoding (SolveSATWithGrover 34.4%, DistinguishUnitaries 40.0%); and (3) chain-of-thought prompting shows a modestly bimodal effect -- it is the best strategy for three models (two of them explicitly reasoning-tuned per vendor documentation) but degrades performance for the rest, leaving it mid-pack in aggregate (56.3% mean) behind few-shot-5 (57.8%). We release the benchmark, evaluation framework, and baseline results to support research on LLM capabilities in quantum computing.

</details>

### [77] [A Systematic Study of Behavioral Cloning for Scientific Data Annotation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07568v1)
*Ishaan Singh Chandok,Core Francisco Park*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: 行为克隆框架用于科学标注agent，含合成任务与多任务预训练，可迁移。

TL;DR: 本文提出一个行为克隆框架，在合成科学标注任务上研究，发现模型层次化学习技能、多任务扩展提升数据效率、多任务预训练实现高效微调，并揭示内部表示共享错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准方法丢弃了人类标注过程中的丰富监督信息，导致验证和纠正仍需要大量人力，需要利用行为克隆从专家标注行为中学习。

Method: 设计了9个合成标注任务和模拟人类策略的合成标注数据，训练模型进行行为克隆，并分析模型内部表示。

Result: 模型层次化学习技能、比训练数据错误更少；更大模型更高效；多任务预训练优于从零训练；模型内部表示任务阶段和共享错误表示。

Conclusion: 该框架建立了系统基准，识别关键瓶颈，为行为克隆扩展到真实科学数据标注奠定了基础。

中文摘要：科学数据标注，例如在视频中追踪动物或校对神经重建，仍然受到“最后一英里”问题的瓶颈：即使有强大的自动化，验证和纠正仍然需要大量的人力。标准方法训练模型直接预测标注，丢弃了专家如何导航、点击、验证和纠正的丰富监督信息。我们引入了一个研究科学标注上的行为克隆的框架：9个合成任务，配以模拟现实人类策略的合成标注，包括探索、错误纠正和战略决策。我们的实验揭示了几个发现。首先，技能层次性地出现：模型先学习GUI机制，再学习任务关键决策，并且比训练数据犯更少的错误，同时保留出错时纠正错误的能力。其次，在多任务行为克隆上扩展模型表明，在我们规模范围内，更大的模型数据效率更高。第三，多任务预训练能够高效微调到新任务，而从零开始训练则完全失败。第四，线性探针揭示模型内部表示标注过程的潜在变量，如任务阶段和数据位置；有趣的是，我们发现了跨不同标注任务泛化的共享错误表示。总体而言，我们的框架建立了系统基准并识别了关键瓶颈，为将行为克隆扩展到现实世界科学数据标注奠定了基础。

Original abstract: Scientific data annotation, such as tracking animals in video or proofreading neural reconstructions, remains bottlenecked by the "last mile" problem: even with strong automation, verification and correction consume substantial human effort. Standard approaches train models to directly predict annotations, discarding the rich supervision in how experts navigate, click, verify, and correct. We introduce a framework for studying behavioral cloning on scientific annotation: 9 synthetic tasks paired with synthetic annotations that simulate realistic human strategies including exploration, mistake correction, and strategic decision-making. Our experiments reveal several findings. First, skills emerge hierarchically: models learn GUI mechanics before task-critical decisions, and commit fewer mistakes than the training data while retaining the ability to correct errors when they occur. Second, scaling models on multi-task behavioral cloning shows that larger models are more data efficient within our scale range. Third, multi-task pretraining enables efficient fine-tuning to new tasks, while training from scratch fails entirely. Fourth, linear probes reveal that models internally represent latent variables of the annotation process such as task phase and data position; interestingly, we find a shared mistake representation that generalizes across different annotation tasks. Overall, our framework establishes systematic benchmarks and identifies key bottlenecks, providing a foundation for scaling behavioral cloning to real-world scientific data annotation.

</details>

### [78] [GENESIS: Harnessing AI Agents for Autonomous 6G RAN Synthesis, Research, and Testing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27360v1)
*Tamerlan Aghayev,Maxime Elkael,Michele Polese,Minh Dat Nguyen,Gabriele Gemmi,Andrea Lacava,Ali Saeizadeh,Reshma Prasad,Paolo Testolina,Angelo Feraudo,Soumendra Nanda,Pedram Johari,Salvatore D'Oro,Tommaso Melodia*

Main category: cs.NI

Selection reason: 针对6G的agent框架，提出可组合原语，架构可迁移。

TL;DR: GENESIS是一个智能体AI框架，通过将意图转化为经空口实验验证的解决方案并反馈到知识库，解决了蜂窝R&D中六个耗时过程及LLMs在RAN中的幻觉和仿真失效问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蜂窝R&D的六个结构过程耗时巨大，且LLMs在RAN用例中因API幻觉、误读规范和仿真失效而效果不佳。

Method: 提出GENESIS框架，包含三个可组合原语（智能体、技能、钩子）和SYNAPSE知识层，将意图转化为经空口实验验证的解决方案并持续反馈。

Result: 实现了将意图转化为经过空口实验验证的解决方案，并反馈到持久知识库，能力在多次运行中累积。

Conclusion: GENESIS通过智能体框架和知识层克服了LLMs在RAN中的缺陷，显著提升了蜂窝R&D的效率和可靠性。

中文摘要：蜂窝研究与开发（R&D）受到六个结构过程的制约，每个过程每次迭代都需要数月的人工工程工作：（i）将标准或研究论文中的新特性综合到生产代码中；（ii）一致性和互操作性测试；（iii）针对现场异常和多样化部署环境进行加固；（iv）网络功能的数据驱动优化；（v）发现并原型设计用于未来标准的新型波形、功能和能力；（vi）保护协议栈免受漏洞攻击。尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）已将通用软件工程中类似的研发工作从数天压缩到数分钟，但它们在无线接入网（RAN）用例中的已知缺陷更为严重：它们会产生应用程序编程接口（API）的幻觉并误读规范，一旦出错就会破坏RAN组件的互操作性；并且它们严重依赖仿真来设计算法，而仿真在转移到实际硬件时众所周知会失效。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出了GENESIS，一个智能体人工智能（AI）框架，它将意图（例如，规范条款、遥测异常或研究假设）转化为经过空口实验验证的解决方案，并反馈到持久的知识库中。GENESIS建立在三个可组合的原语（智能体、技能、钩子）和一个知识层（SYNAPSE）之上，该知识层既作为事实来源，也作为框架产生的每个产物的接收者，使得能力在运行中不断累积。

Original abstract: Cellular research and development (R&D) is throttled by six structural processes that each consume months of manual engineering work per iteration: (i) synthesizing new features from standards or research papers into production code; (ii) conformance and interoperability testing; (iii) hardening against field anomalies and diverse deployment environments; (iv) data-driven optimization of network functionalities; (v) discovering and prototyping novel waveforms, functionalities, and capabilities for future standards; and (vi) securing the stack against vulnerabilities. Although Large Language Models (LLMs) have compressed comparable R&D work in general software engineering from days to minutes, their known pitfalls worsen on Radio Access Network (RAN) use cases: they hallucinate Application Programming Interfaces (APIs) and mis-read specifications, which kills interoperability of RAN components at the first mistake, and they heavily rely on simulations for designing algorithms, which is notorious for breaking when transferred to real hardware. To address these challenges, we present GENESIS, an agentic Artificial Intelligence (AI) framework that converts intents (e.g., a specification clause, a telemetry anomaly, or a research hypothesis) into solutions validated with over-the-air experiments, fed back into a persistent knowledge base. GENESIS is built on three composable primitives (agents, skills, hooks) and a knowledge layer (SYNAPSE) that doubles as the source of ground truth and the recipient of every artifact the framework produces, making capabilities compound across runs.

</details>

# q-fin.RM [[Back]](#toc)

### [79] [Foundations of a Time-Consistent Counterfactual Actuarial Runtime for Autonomous AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26508v1)
*Hao-Hsuan Chen*

Main category: q-fin.RM

Selection reason: 自治AI agent保险框架，提出预动作风险计算方法，可迁移至agent安全与可靠性

TL;DR: 本文为自主AI智能体提出一个运行时精算框架，通过反事实风险收费和承保边界，实现动作级保险替代传统年度责任保险，并建立了四个关键理论结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI责任保险多为事后年度覆盖，无法应对自主智能体实时、高频的动作风险，需要一种预动作、细粒度的风险定价机制来确保安全可控运行。

Method: 构建一个包含反事实收费、承保边界和门控定理的数学精算层，定义动作级保险为基本单位，并用边界势能、不可逆权限溢价等概念形式化风险结构。

Result: 证明了四个结构性结果：反事实收费的非唯一性、边界内不可分割性与抗博弈性、不可逆权限溢价的分解与充要条件、以及运行时门控定理给出的预算保证。

Conclusion: 该工作为AI智能体的实时风险管理提供了数学基础，支撑后续实证、机制设计和动态承保研究，有望实现更安全的自主系统部署。

中文摘要：我们为自主AI智能体提出一个基础的运行时精算层，其中每个带有副作用的动作都会承担一个时间一致的反事实风险收费，该收费基于合约固定的安全默认值计算，并位于明确的承保边界内。该框架将每个动作的保险作为主要分析单元，并用动作前交易层取代事后年度责任保险。本文建立了四个结构性结果：(i) 在选定的安全默认映射和延续策略下，定义良好的反事实收费，具有明确的非唯一性；(ii) 承保边界内的不可分割性，将路径分解的动作映射为边界势能，并给出一个推论，将抗博弈性与边界设计联系起来；(iii) 不可逆权限溢价，分为严格正的动作级组成部分和集合级稳健资本增加性的充要条件；以及 (iv) 一个保守的运行时门控定理，将高概率收费包络转化为已执行动作预算保证。结果为更广泛的项目提供了数学基础层：一个实证配套研究通过精算动作接口和权限前沿实验实例化该运行时；一个机制设计配套研究研究策略性操作者激励和跨边界聚合；一个动态承保配套研究研究经验评级和审计回放校准。本文阐述了这些后续层所依赖的基本合同、收费恒等式、边界内无套利结果和预算保证。

Original abstract: We propose a foundational runtime actuarial layer for autonomous AI agents in which every side-effect-bearing action carries a time-consistent, counterfactual risk toll computed against a contractually fixed safe default, inside an explicit underwriting boundary. The framework treats per-action insurance as the primary unit of analysis and replaces post-hoc annual liability cover with a pre-action transaction layer. The paper establishes four structural results: (i) a well-defined counterfactual toll under a chosen safe-default mapping and continuation policy, with explicit non-uniqueness; (ii) a no-splitting property within an underwriting boundary that telescopes path-decomposed actions into a boundary potential, with a corollary tying gaming-resistance to boundary design; (iii) an irreversible-authority premium, split into a strictly positive action-level component and an if-and-only-if characterisation of the set-level robust capital increase; and (iv) a conservative runtime gating theorem that translates high-probability toll envelopes into an executed-action budget guarantee. The result is the mathematical base layer for a broader program: an empirical companion instantiates the runtime through an Actuarial Action Interface and authority-frontier experiments; a mechanism-design companion studies strategic operator incentives and cross-boundary aggregation; and a dynamic-underwriting companion studies experience rating and audit-replay calibration. The present paper states the primitive contract, the toll identity, the within-boundary no-arbitrage result, and the budget guarantee on which those later layers depend.

</details>


<div id='cs.CR'></div>

# cs.CR [[Back]](#toc)

### [80] [ChainCaps: Composition-Safe Tool-Using Agents via Monotonic Capability Attenuation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26542v4)
*Xiaochong Jiang,Shiqi Yang,Ziwei Li,Lifei Liu,Haoran Yu,Yichen Liu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: ChainCaps，工具使用agent安全机制，直接解决权限提升与安全组合问题

TL;DR: ChainCaps通过运行时能力预算机制防止工具组合中的权限洗白攻击，在保持高完成率的同时大幅降低攻击成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工具使用智能体在开放环境中组合多种工具时，即使每个工具都满足权限检查，仍可能产生不安全端到端效果（权限洗白），需要一种运行时安全机制。

Method: 提出ChainCaps，每个值携带接收器特定能力预算，工具组合通过交集传播预算，确保值不能通过组合获得新权限。实现为透明MCP代理。

Result: 在82个任务上，攻击成功率从25-68%降至0-4.8%，良性任务完成率96-100%。优于标量IFC和每函数隔离基线。清单质量是关键瓶颈。

Conclusion: ChainCaps有效解决了工具组合中的权限洗白问题，但依赖于可信清单和代理可见数据移动，适用于当前部署的智能体。

中文摘要：使用工具的智能体日益在开放式部署环境中运行，它们在运行时组合文件系统、网络API、代码解释器以及企业服务。这造成了工具组合中的安全缺口：智能体可以满足每个工具的权限检查，但仍会产生不安全的端到端效果，例如读取机密文档、总结并将其发送到外部端点。我们将这种失败模式称为权限洗白（permission laundering）。ChainCaps通过一个运行时规则来解决这一问题：每个值都携带一个特定于接收器的能力预算，工具组合通过交集传播预算。一个值在通过工具链移动时，可以保留或丧失权限，但不能通过组合获得新的权限。我们将ChainCaps实现为一个透明的MCP代理，无需对智能体或工具服务器进行任何更改。在来自三个提供商的五个前沿模型的82个任务上，ChainCaps将攻击成功率从25-68%降低到0-4.8%，同时保留了96-100%的正常任务完成率。在重放实验中，它也优于标量IFC和每函数隔离基线。清单质量是主要的部署瓶颈：专家级清单达到100%的攻击阻止率，而简单清单则降至27.3%。我们的声明仅限于在可信清单和代理可见数据移动下的显式流组合安全性，这是当前部署的工具使用智能体中的一个实际缺口。

Original abstract: Tool-using agents increasingly operate in open-ended deployment environments, where they compose file systems, web APIs, code interpreters, and enterprise services at runtime. This creates a safety gap in tool composition: an agent can satisfy every per-tool permission check and still produce an unsafe end-to-end effect, such as reading a confidential document, summarizing it, and sending the summary to an external endpoint. We call this failure mode permission laundering. ChainCaps addresses it with a runtime rule: every value carries a sink-specific capability budget, and tool composition propagates budgets by intersection. A value can preserve or lose authority as it moves through a tool chain, but it cannot gain new authority through composition. We implement ChainCaps as a transparent MCP proxy that requires no changes to the agent or tool servers. On 82 tasks across five frontier models from three providers, ChainCaps reduces attack success rate from 25-68% to 0-4.8% while preserving 96-100% benign completion. In replay experiments, it also outperforms scalar-IFC and per-function-isolation baselines. Manifest quality is the dominant deployment bottleneck: expert manifests reach 100% attack blocking, while naive manifests fall to 27.3%. Our claims are limited to explicit-flow composition safety under trusted manifests and proxy-visible data movement, a practical gap in deployed tool-using agents today.

</details>


### [81] [Cordyceps: Covert Control Attacks on LLMs via Data Poisoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26595v2)
*Zedian Shao,Charles Fleming,Teodora Baluta*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 数据投毒隐蔽控制攻击，对agent安全有警示意义

TL;DR: 提出了一种利用语义关联隐藏恶意指令的隐蔽控制攻击，在多个LLM和防御下表现出高成功率和强隐蔽性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有投毒攻击依赖固定触发器，易被防御机制中和，需要更隐蔽的攻击方法以揭示LLM微调中的新漏洞。

Method: 通过共享知识与攻击者选择短语的语义关联，教会LLM一种信息隐藏方案，使模型能够编码和解码任意恶意指令。

Result: 隐蔽控制攻击在平均攻击成功率上比启发式提示注入高出约40%，且能绕过多种防御，成功率最高达98%。

Conclusion: 隐蔽控制攻击揭示了LLM微调中一种新的投毒诱导漏洞，威胁现有防御机制。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）通常在未经整理的文本数据集上进行微调，而攻击者可以毒化这些数据集。现有的投毒攻击主要依赖于固定的触发短语，而异常检测、干净数据正则化或在线监控等防御措施可以中和这些触发短语。在本文中，我们提出了一种数据投毒方法，通过共享知识（如事实或概念）与攻击者选择的短语之间的语义关联，可靠且隐蔽地教会LLM一种信息隐藏方案。诱导出的隐藏方案可以编码和解码任意恶意指令，从而揭示了一种新的且微妙的投毒诱导漏洞：隐蔽控制攻击。我们精确描述了隐蔽控制攻击，并在5个LLM、3种后门防御和4种提示注入防御上进行了评估。使用少量投毒样本时，隐蔽控制攻击在平均攻击成功率上比基于启发式的提示注入攻击高出约40%（相对于干净微调模型）。它们还绕过了基于检测和微调的防御，在后门防御后保持高达93%的攻击成功率，在提示注入防御后保持高达98%的攻击成功率。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are often fine-tuned on uncurated text datasets that adversaries can poison. Existing poisoning attacks primarily rely on fixed trigger phrases that defenses such as outlier detection, clean-data regularization, or online monitoring can neutralize. In this paper, we propose a data poisoning method that teaches an LLM an information hiding scheme reliably and stealthily through semantic associations between shared knowledge such as facts or concepts and attacker-chosen phrases. The induced hiding scheme can encode and decode arbitrary malicious instructions, thus revealing a new and subtle poisoning-induced vulnerability: covert control attacks.
  We precisely characterize covert control attacks and evaluate them across $5$ LLMs, $3$ backdoor defenses, and $4$ prompt injection defenses. With a small poisoned fraction, covert control attacks outperform heuristic-based prompt injection attacks in average attack success rate by about $40\%$ relative to clean fine-tuned models. They also circumvent defenses based on detection and fine-tuning, maintaining up to $93\%$ attack success rate after backdoor defenses and up to $98\%$ after prompt injection defenses.

</details>


### [82] [Cordon-MAS: Defending RAG against Knowledge Poisoning via Information-Flow Control](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26754v1)
*Zhe Yu,Wenpeng Xing,Gaolei Li,Shuguang Xiong,Hongzhi Wang,Xuyang Teng,Meng Han*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: RAG防御中的agent信息流控制架构，对agent安全与可迁移设计有启发。

TL;DR: 提出CORDON-MAS框架，通过信息流控制而非检测来防御RAG投毒攻击，将攻击成功率降低92.4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有防御假设检测到投毒证据就能防止危害，但模型存在监控-控制差距，即能检测到矛盾但仍会依据被投毒信息行事，因此需要新的防御思路。

Method: 引入Cordon原则，通过CORDON-MAS框架架构上强制执行，将证据提取、跨源审计和答案合成分离为具有不对称内存权限的智能体。

Result: 在五个BEIR数据集上，攻击成功率降低92.4%。

Conclusion: 将RAG投毒攻击从检测问题重新定义为信息流控制问题。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）日益支撑着高风险应用，但仍易受Confundo式投毒攻击，其中对抗性优化的文档会操纵生成输出。现有防御假设检测到被投毒的证据就能防止危害。我们表明这一假设不正确：模型存在监控-控制差距——它们能检测到检索证据中的矛盾，但仍会依据被投毒的声称行事。我们引入Cordon原则——任何能够进行最终合成的智能体不得访问不可信的自然语言证据——并通过CORDON-MAS实现该原则，这是一个分区框架，通过将证据提取、跨源审计和答案合成分离到具有不对称内存权限的智能体中来在架构上强制执行该原则。在五个BEIR数据集上，CORDON-MAS相对于未防御的RAG将攻击成功率降低了92.4%。这将RAG投毒从一个检测问题重新定义为信息流控制问题。

Original abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) increasingly underpins high-stakes applications, yet remains vulnerable to Confundo-style poisoning where adversarially optimized documents manipulate generated outputs. Existing defenses assume that detecting poisoned evidence prevents harm. We show this assumption is incorrect: models exhibit a monitoring-control gap -- they can detect contradictions in retrieved evidence yet still act on poisoned claims. We introduce the Cordon Principle -- no agent capable of final synthesis may access untrusted natural-language evidence -- and realize it through CORDON-MAS, a compartmentalized framework that enforces this principle architecturally by separating evidence extraction, cross-source audit, and answer synthesis into agents with asymmetric memory privileges. Across five BEIR datasets, CORDON-MAS reduces attack success rate by 92.4\% relative to undefended RAG. This reframes RAG poisoning from a detection problem to an information-flow control problem.

</details>


### [83] [Lessons from Penetration Tests on Large-Scale Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27042v1)
*Kevin Eykholt,Dhilung Kirat,Xiaokui Shu,Jiyong Jang,Frederico Araujo,Ian Molloy*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 大型智能体系统渗透测试经验，提供安全洞见，可迁移至coding agent安全设计。

TL;DR: 本文通过2025年的两次渗透测试，评估了专有AI代理系统的安全弱点，并与开源系统对比，探讨了安全态势的改善情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究主要关注开源AI代理的漏洞，但专有代理系统在更严格的开发标准下是否也存在类似弱点尚不清楚，因此需要评估其安全性。

Method: 在2025年对两个专有AI代理产品进行了渗透测试。

Result: 两次渗透测试发现了专有AI代理中的安全漏洞，并评估了自评估以来安全态势的改善。

Conclusion: 专有AI代理系统在更严格的开发标准下仍存在安全弱点，但安全态势可能有所改善，需要持续关注和测试。

中文摘要：随着人工智能系统获得越来越高的自主性和执行能力，发现的安全漏洞数量持续增加。然而，许多这些漏洞并非根本上的新颖，而是反映了先前计算系统中长期观察到的重复出现的弱点类别。能够执行任务的AI智能体实际上是无限的、自修改的程序，它们与计算堆栈的多个层次广泛交互。这种广泛的交互表面给开发者带来了显著的安全负担，他们必须推理并保护复杂的跨层行为。先前的研究主要关注开源智能体和智能体框架中的漏洞。相比之下，目前尚不清楚专有智能体系统——在更严格的编码标准和正式审查流程下开发——是否表现出类似的安全弱点。在本文中，我们介绍了2025年对专有智能体产品进行的两次渗透测试的结果，并评估自这些评估以来AI智能体的安全态势是否有所改善。

Original abstract: As AI systems gain increasing autonomy and execution capability, the number of discovered security vulnerabilities continues to rise. However, many of these vulnerabilities are not fundamentally novel, but instead reflect recurring classes of weaknesses long observed in prior computing systems. Execution-capable AI agents are effectively unbounded, self-modifying programs that interact extensively with multiple layers of the computing stack. This broad interaction surface imposes a significant security burden on developers, who must reason about and secure complex cross-layer behaviors. Prior research has primarily focused on vulnerabilities in open-source agents and agent frameworks. In contrast, it remains unclear whether proprietary agent systems -- developed under stricter coding standards and formal review processes -- exhibit similar security weaknesses. In this paper, we present findings from two penetration tests conducted in 2025 against proprietary agent products and evaluate whether the security posture of AI agents has improved since these assessments.

</details>


### [84] [Grimlock: Guarding High-Agency Systems with eBPF and Attested Channels](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27488v2)
*Qiancheng Wu,Wenhui Zhang,Gan Fang,Sheng Mao,Biao Gao,David Levitsky,Shawna Murphy Butterworth,Rob Cameron*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: agent系统安全守卫机制，可应用于coding agent的安全部署

TL;DR: Grimlock是一个基于eBPF和TLS通道绑定的代理守卫，在不修改代理代码的情况下实现跨沙箱的安全通信、授权和最小权限委派。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主系统中身份、授权等安全机制被推入应用代码，导致难以一致执行和审计。

Method: 使用eBPF强制流量拦截，结合TLS 1.3通道绑定的握手后认证，生成短期作用域令牌，并在接收端重新验证后释放明文。

Result: 实现了透明、可审计、作用域绑定的代理间通信，使用Linux原语，无需修改用户代码。

Conclusion: Grimlock为异构多云环境中的代理通信提供了安全路径。

中文摘要：自主系统越来越多地运行用户编写的编排代码，这些代码调用工具、生成子任务，并在机器和云之间委派工作。尽管这种高自主性富有成效，但它带来了一个安全问题：身份、授权、来源和委派常常被推入应用程序代码中，导致难以一致地执行和审计。我们提出Grimlock，一个代理守卫，通过将信任执行移动到沙箱子系统中，同时保持代理代码不变，从而恢复了关注点分离。Grimlock使用eBPF强制流量拦截来确保沙箱通信通过守卫，并将其与绑定到标准TLS 1.3通道绑定上的握手后认证相结合。在通道建立后，守卫授权通信并生成短暂的、绑定通道的作用域令牌，捕获最小权限委派。在接收端，目标守卫重新验证身份、作用域和通道绑定，终止TLS，并且仅在策略检查成功后向目标沙箱释放明文。kTLS为受保护的通信提供了高效的数据平面。因此，Grimlock提供了一条路径，实现跨异构多云环境的透明、可审计且作用域绑定的代理间通信，使用通用的Linux原语，并且无需更改用户层编排代码。

Original abstract: Agentic systems increasingly run user-authored orchestration code that invokes tools, spawns subtasks, and delegates work across machines and clouds. Although this high agency is productive, it creates a security problem: identity, authorization, provenance, and delegation are often pushed into application code, where they become difficult to enforce consistently and difficult to audit.
  We present Grimlock, an Agent Guard that restores separation of concerns by moving trust enforcement into the sandbox substrate while leaving agent code unchanged. Grimlock uses eBPF-enforced traffic interception to ensure that sandbox communication passes through a guard, and combines it with post-handshake attestation bound to standard TLS~1.3 channel bindings. After a channel is established, the guard authorizes communication and mints short-lived, channel-bound scope tokens that capture least-privilege delegation. At the receiving side, the destination guard re-validates identity, scope, and channel binding, terminates TLS, and releases plaintext to the destination sandbox only after policy checks succeed. kTLS provides an efficient dataplane for protected communication.
  As a result, Grimlock offers a path toward transparent, auditable, and scope-bound agent-to-agent communication across heterogeneous multi-cloud environments, using commodity Linux primitives and without requiring changes to user-layer orchestration code.

</details>


### [85] [HARP: Measuring Harm Amplification in Multi-Agent LLM Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27489v1)
*Md Hafizur Rahman,Zafaryab Haider,Tanzim Mahfuz,Prabuddha Chakraborty*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 多agent系统危害放大测量方法，直接适用于coding agent安全评测

TL;DR: HARP是一种追踪优先的方法，用于量化多智能体LLM系统中局部扰动如何放大为全局危害，发现单一专家妥协放大最强，共享上下文破坏攻击成功率最高，时间持久性恶意影响最大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估仅关注攻击成功率，忽视了模块化架构中危害在组件间的传播放大风险，因此需要一种方法来衡量局部到全局的危害放大。

Method: 提出HARP方法，通过比较成对的干净和扰动执行，定义局部危害（偏离目标组件）、全局危害（全追踪偏离）和危害放大因子（全局/局部），并在一个七智能体金融系统中实例化，支持多种攻击模式和防御评估。

Result: 单一专家妥协导致最强放大，共享上下文破坏产生最高攻击成功率，时间持久攻击造成最大恶意影响；防御中IntegrityGuard实现最低攻击成功率和全局危害，但牺牲了效用或成本。

Conclusion: 安全的多智能体评估必须同时衡量绕过和传播，而不仅仅是绕过。

中文摘要：多智能体LLM系统将工作流分解到多个智能体、工具、共享上下文、记忆和决策门中。这种模块化提高了可解释性，但同时也带来了传播风险：对一个组件的有限扰动可能被其他智能体重用，并放大为系统级危害。我们提出了HARP（通过角色扰动进行危害放大），这是一种用于研究多智能体LLM系统中从局部到全局危害放大的追踪优先方法。HARP比较成对的干净执行和扰动执行，并记录专家输出、工具调用、内存读/写、防护事件、预言机日志、延迟、令牌成本和决策。我们将局部危害定义为偏离目标智能体或被破坏的通道，全局危害定义为在整个追踪中的偏离，危害放大定义为（H_global/H_local）。这补充了攻击成功率，衡量了编排如何将危害从攻击点传播出去。我们在一个面向金融的七智能体系统中实例化HARP，该系统具有确定性决策门和可配置的攻击工具，用于专家妥协、合谋、共享上下文破坏以及时间或内存持续性攻击。在五种防御措施中，仅提示防御保持了良性效用，但保留了高成功率和隐蔽性；工具前和步骤级防护以效用或延迟成本减少了一些失败；而IntegrityGuard，一种追踪一致性防御，实现了最低的攻击成功率和全局危害，但引入了效用/成本权衡。结果表明，单一专家妥协产生了最强的放大，共享上下文破坏产生了最高的攻击成功率，而时间持续性产生了最大的恶意影响。HARP认为，安全的多智能体评估必须不仅衡量绕过，还要衡量传播。

Original abstract: Multi-agent LLM systems decompose workflows across agents, tools, shared context, memory, and decision gates. This modularity improves interpretability, but creates a propagation risk: a bounded perturbation to one component can be reused by other agents and amplified into system-level harm. We introduce HARP (Harm Amplification through Role Perturbation), a trace-first methodology for studying local-to-global harm amplification in multi-agent LLM systems. HARP compares paired clean and perturbed executions and records specialist outputs, tool calls, memory reads/writes, guard events, oracle logs, latency, token cost, and decisions. We define local harm as deviation from targeted agents or corrupted channels, global harm as deviation over the full trace, and harm amplification as (H_global/H_local). This complements attack success rate with a measure of how strongly orchestration spreads harm beyond the attack point. We instantiate HARP in a finance-oriented seven-agent system with a deterministic decision gate and configurable attack harness for specialist compromise, collusion, shared-context corruption, and temporal or memory-persistent attacks. Across five defenses, prompt-only defenses preserve benign utility but leave high success and stealth; pre-tool and step-level guards reduce some failures with utility or latency costs; and IntegrityGuard, a trace-consistency defense, achieves the lowest attack success and global harm but introduces utility/cost trade-offs. Results show that single-specialist compromise produces the strongest amplification, shared-context corruption yields the highest attack success, and temporal persistence produces the largest malicious impact. HARP argues that secure multi-agent evaluation must measure not only bypass, but propagation.

</details>

# cs.DB [[Back]](#toc)

### [86] [Knowledge Graphs as the Missing Data Layer for LLM-Based Industrial Asset Operations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26874v3)
*Madhulatha Mandarapu,Sandeep Kunkunuru*

Main category: cs.DB

Selection reason: 知识图谱作为LLM agent的数据层优化，可迁移至coding agent信息检索。

TL;DR: 研究证明，在工业资产操作中，使用类型化知识图谱作为数据层比LLM编排范式更关键，将准确率从65%提升至99%（图可回答场景），并通过GAK处理缺失数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代理在平面文档上推理准确率低，研究数据层对提升性能的影响。

Method: 采用类型化知识图谱，路由问题至三种方式：LLM生成Cypher查询、原生图计算、生成增强知识（GAK）物化缺失事实。

Result: 结构化检索提升GPT-4至82-83%，原生图达99%，GAK将缺失场景可回答性从0%升至81.8%。

Conclusion: 在结构化操作领域，数据层是主要杠杆，类型化知识图谱可作为基础底层。

中文摘要：基于LLM的工业资产操作代理在处理平面文档存储时，其推理准确率有限。AssetOpsBench（KDD 2026）建立了GPT-4代理在139个工业维护场景中达到65%的准确率，并比较了LLM编排范式（Agent-As-Tool vs. Plan-Execute）在固定数据层上的表现。我们提出正交问题：工具背后的数据模型有多重要？我们将类型化知识图谱作为基础底层，并根据每个问题的最佳回答方式路由：（i）LLM生成的Cypher进行结构化检索，将同一GPT-4模型从65%提升到82-83%；（ii）原生图和优化原语，无需LLM，在图可回答场景中达到99%；（iii）生成增强知识（GAK）用于数据中不存在的答案——引擎的代理将缺失的事实物化为带有来源标签的图节点，然后回答。一个反复出现的主题是反向LLM使用：我们限制LLM从类型化模式进行查询生成或一次性增强，让图确定性执行。在88个真实的AssetOpsBench故障模式场景中（基准本身标记为非确定性——十种设备类型在图谱中缺失），GAK将可回答性从零提升到100%的设备类型，并回答了81.8%的场景，每个物化的事实都标记了来源：LLM衍生以进行审计追踪。我们还贡献了40个原生图场景。对于结构化操作领域，数据层——而非LLM编排——是主要杠杆，类型化知识图谱作为原始工业数据和LLM推理之间的基础底层。

Original abstract: LLM-based agents for industrial asset operations show limited accuracy when reasoning over flat document stores. AssetOpsBench (KDD 2026) establishes that GPT-4 agents achieve 65% on 139 industrial maintenance scenarios, and compares LLM orchestration paradigms (Agent-As-Tool vs. Plan-Execute) on a fixed data layer. We ask the orthogonal question: how much does the data model behind the tools matter?
  We treat a typed knowledge graph as a grounding substrate and route each question by how it is best answered: (i) LLM-generated Cypher for structured retrieval, which lifts the same GPT-4 model from 65% to 82-83%; (ii) native graph and optimization primitives, with no LLM, reaching 99% on graph-answerable scenarios; and (iii) generation-augmented knowledge (GAK) for answers absent from the data -- the engine's agent materializes the missing facts as provenance-tagged graph nodes, then answers. A recurring theme is inverted LLM usage: we constrain the LLM to query generation or one-shot enrichment from a typed schema and let the graph execute deterministically.
  On the 88 real AssetOpsBench failure-mode scenarios the benchmark itself flags non-deterministic -- ten equipment types absent from the graph -- GAK lifts answerability from zero to 100% of equipment types and answers 81.8% of scenarios, every materialized fact tagged source:LLM-derived for auditability. We also contribute 40 graph-native scenarios. For structured operational domains the data layer -- not the LLM orchestration -- is the primary lever, and a typed knowledge graph serves as a grounding substrate between raw industrial data and LLM reasoning.

</details>


<div id='cs.CV'></div>

# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [87] [Tensor Memory: Fixed-Size Recurrent State for Long-Horizon Transformers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27686v1)
*Kabir Swain,Sijie Han,Daniel Karl I. Weidele,Mauro Martino,Antonio Torralba*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 提出固定大小的循环记忆模块用于长序列Transformer，可迁移至agent长期记忆设计。

TL;DR: 提出Tensor Memory模块，通过固定大小的循环3D记忆张量为Transformer提供持久空间状态，解耦容量与序列长度，在多种基准上有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer缺乏显式的持久空间状态，导致长期视频理解和遮挡推理困难，且内存随序列长度增长。

Method: Tensor Memory模块：可微软写入将token内容存入固定大小3D体素网格，局部交互和门控循环更新记忆，连续采样读取，与Transformer块无缝集成。

Result: 在语言、图像、视频基准和诊断套件上评估，性能提升，且与标准训练流程兼容。

Conclusion: Tensor Memory解耦状态容量与输入长度，保留空间归纳偏置，可轻松集成到现有Transformer中。

中文摘要：Transformers通过将空间和时间展平为长token序列来处理图像和视频。尽管注意力和KV缓存保留了过去的特征，它们的内存随序列长度增长，并且缺乏显式的、持久化的空间状态，这使得长期视频理解和遮挡敏感推理变得困难。我们提出Tensor Memory，一个轻量级模块，通过一个固定大小的循环3D记忆张量增强Transformer块：token通过可微软写入将内容作为高斯加权体积围绕预测的连续3D位置写入体素网格，通过高效的局部交互算子和门控循环动力学更新记忆，token通过连续采样和门控残差融合读取上下文。由于记忆张量大小固定，Tensor Memory将状态容量与输入长度解耦，同时保留空间归纳偏置。我们在标准语言、图像和视频基准以及一个旨在隔离持久状态有益的受控玩具诊断套件上评估该模块；它与标准Transformer训练流程集成，可以附加到或从现有块中移除，无需其他架构更改。

Original abstract: Transformers process images and videos by flattening space and time into long token sequences. While attention and KV caching preserve past features, their memory grows with sequence length and they lack an explicit, persistent spatial state, making long-horizon video understanding and occlusion-sensitive reasoning difficult. We propose Tensor Memory, a lightweight module that augments Transformer blocks with a fixed-size recurrent 3D memory tensor: tokens write into a voxel grid via a differentiable soft write that deposits content as a Gaussian-weighted volume around a predicted continuous 3D location, the memory is updated with an efficient local interaction operator and gated recurrent dynamics, and tokens read back context via continuous sampling with gated residual fusion. Because the memory tensor has a constant size, Tensor Memory decouples state capacity from input length while preserving a spatial inductive bias. We evaluate the module on standard language, image, and video benchmarks and on a controlled toy diagnostic suite designed to isolate when persistent state is beneficial; it integrates with standard Transformer training pipelines and can be attached to or removed from existing blocks without other architectural changes.

</details>


### [88] [AndroidDaily: A Verifiable Benchmark for Mobile GUI Agents on Real-World Closed-Source Applications](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27761v1)
*Yifan Sui,Xin Huang,Hongbing Li,Fang Xu,Jiahe Lv,Haolong Yan,Yeqing Shen,Litao Liu,Zhimin Fan,Ziyang Meng,Jia Wang,Junbo Qi,Kaijun Tan,Zheng Ge,Xiangyu Zhang,Daxin Jiang,Osamu Yoshie*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 针对现实闭源移动应用评估难题，提出AndroidDaily基准和GRADE自动评估方法，基于外部准则进行过程诊断，达到87.37%的人机一致性，揭示当前模型在实际任务中的能力差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GUI代理评估多依赖模拟环境或开源应用，无法有效评估真实闭源应用，因为缺乏内部状态导致自动验证困难。

Method: 构建AndroidDaily基准（350个日常任务，94个高频率Android应用），提出GRADE评估器，基于操作义务、输出质量和负面约束三类外部准则，通过视觉轨迹进行步骤级诊断。

Result: GRADE与人类评估者一致率达87.37%，最强模型在AndroidDaily上成功率为62.0%。

Conclusion: 当前推理能力与实际移动工作流执行之间存在显著差距，GRADE为闭源环境下的自动评估提供了可行方案。

中文摘要：GUI基础模型和移动GUI代理的快速发展催生了许多评估基准，但大多数依赖于模拟环境或开源应用，使得真实的闭源应用在很大程度上未被评估。核心难点在于闭源应用不暴露内部状态，导致传统的自动验证方法不适用。为了弥补这一差距，我们引入了AndroidDaily，一个大规模的基准测试，包含跨94个高频Android应用的350个现实日常任务，涵盖交通、购物、本地服务、娱乐、内容创作、社交媒体和日常工具。为了在这些不透明环境中实现自动化和可验证的评估，我们提出了基于准则的自动诊断评估审阅者（GRADE），这是一个基于三层可观察外部准则（操作义务、输出质量和负面约束）的过程感知评估器。GRADE根据这些标准跟踪代理的视觉轨迹，并生成步骤级诊断判断，将长时域、开放式的移动交互转变为可验证的评估，而无需依赖隐藏的内部状态。实验表明，GRADE与人类评估者的一致率达到87.37%。最强模型在AndroidDaily上的成功率为62.0%，突显了当前推理能力与现实移动工作流实际执行之间的巨大差距。

Original abstract: The rapid development of GUI foundation models and mobile GUI agents has spurred numerous evaluation benchmarks, yet most rely on simulated environments or open-source applications, leaving real-world closed-source applications largely unevaluated. The core difficulty is that closed-source applications do not expose internal states, making traditional automatic verification inapplicable. To bridge this gap, we introduce AndroidDaily, a large-scale benchmark comprising 350 realistic daily-use tasks across 94 high-frequency Android applications spanning transportation, shopping, local services, entertainment, content creation, social media, and everyday utilities. To enable automatic and verifiable assessment in these opaque environments, we propose Guideline-grounded Reviewer for Automatic Diagnostic Evaluation (GRADE), a process-aware evaluator built on a three-tiered system of observable external guidelines: operational obligations, output quality, and negative constraints. GRADE tracks the agent's visual trajectory against these criteria and produces step-level diagnostic judgments, turning long-horizon, open-ended mobile interactions into verifiable evaluation without relying on hidden internal states. Experiments show that GRADE achieves 87.37\% agreement with human evaluators. The strongest model reaches a 62.0\% success rate on AndroidDaily, highlighting a substantial gap between current reasoning capabilities and practical execution in realistic mobile workflows.

### [89] [Towards Error-Free EHRs: Reasoning-Intensive Consistency Verification Between Clinical Notes and Structured Tables in Electronic Health Records](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26463v1)
*Yeonsu Kwon,Jiho Kim,Junseong Choi,Paloma Rabaey,Minseo Kim,Sujeong Im,Jeewon Yang,Jun-Min Lee,Sangji Lee,Jiwon Kim,Hangyul Yoon,Hyunwook Kwon,Edward Choi*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LLM agent框架用于EHR一致性验证，含规划与工具使用，可迁移到代码agent。

TL;DR: 提出EHR-ReasonCon基准和EHR-Inspector框架，用于电子健康记录中临床笔记与表格的推理密集型一致性验证，在MIMIC-III上取得最先进性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法仅基于表面匹配，无法捕捉临床推理、事件关系和时间变化，需要更智能的一致性验证。

Method: 构建EHR-ReasonCon基准（来自MIMIC-III，包含8048个实体，专家注释），并提出EHR-Inspector（LLM框架，包括笔记分割、锚点实体和时间参考提取、表格探索工具验证）。

Result: 在严格和宽松标准下，EHR-Inspector在多个模型上达到最先进性能，组件有效性得到验证。

Conclusion: 该工作填补了推理密集型一致性验证的空白，展示了LLM在EHR数据一致性检查中的潜力。

中文摘要：电子健康记录（EHR）中非结构化临床笔记与结构化表格之间的数据一致性对于患者安全和临床决策至关重要。然而，现有的笔记-表格一致性验证工作主要依赖于数值或简单事件的表面匹配。这些方法无法捕捉真实世界EHR文档背后的推理，包括临床解释、事件关系和时间变化。为了解决这一差距，我们引入了EHR-ReasonCon，一个用于笔记-表格一致性验证的推理密集型基准。基于MIMIC-III并通过专家指导的注释构建，它包含来自临床笔记的8,048个实体，并提供高质量的真实标签。注释协议由专门的表格探索工具支持，以确保系统化的证据检索和可靠的一致性评估。我们还提出了EHR-Inspector，一个基于LLM的框架，它分割笔记，提取锚点实体和时间参考，并使用表格探索工具验证与结构化表格的一致性。使用经过专家验证的LLM作为评判指标的严格和宽松标准进行评估，EHR-Inspector在多个模型骨干上取得了最先进的性能。分析进一步证明了其组件的有效性，并突出了与人类验证的差异。

Original abstract: Data consistency between unstructured clinical notes and structured tables in Electronic Health Records (EHRs) is essential for patient safety and clinical decision-making. However, existing work on note-table consistency verification mainly relies on surface-level matching of numeric values or simple events. Such approaches fail to capture the reasoning underlying real-world EHR documentation, including clinical interpretation, event relations, and temporal changes. To address this gap, we introduce EHR-ReasonCon, a reasoning-intensive benchmark for note-table consistency verification. Built on MIMIC-III with expert-guided annotations, it comprises 8,048 entities derived from clinical notes and provides high-quality ground-truth labels. The annotation protocol is supported by specialized table-exploration tools to ensure systematic evidence retrieval and reliable consistency assessment. We also propose EHR-Inspector, an LLM-based framework that segments notes, extracts anchor entities and temporal references, and uses table-exploration tools to verify consistency against structured tables. Evaluated using expert-validated LLM-as-a-judge metrics under harsh and lenient criteria, EHR-Inspector achieves state-of-the-art performance across multiple model backbones. Analyses further demonstrate the effectiveness of its components and highlight differences from human verification.

### [90] [Evidence Absence Is Not Evidence Insufficiency: Diagnosing NEI Construction Artifacts in Fact Verification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26663v1)
*Jingxi Qiu,Zeyu Han,Cheng Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出NEI-CAP协议评估事实核查中的证据不足情况，发现不同构建方式会导致模型能力无法迁移，且聚合分数掩盖真实问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有事实核查基准中，“信息不足”（NEI）标签的操作化方式不同，导致模型实际学习内容与分数含义存在歧义，需要更细致的诊断方法。

Method: 设计NEI-CAP协议，每个NEI示例标注构建家族，审计捷径线索、通过人工裁决验证困难案例，并测试跨构建迁移能力；在SciFact、FEVER和HoVer数据集上实验。

Result: NEI能力无法可靠跨构建迁移；捷径倾向构建训练的模型难以识别语义相关的不充分证据；混合构建训练缩小差距但未消除；证据条件影响对支持/反驳标签的信心及NEI召回率。

Conclusion: 聚合NEI分数可能掩盖模型实际解决的问题，构建感知的诊断对评估证据不足至关重要。

中文摘要：证据缺失并非证据不足，但事实核查基准可以使它们在观测上相似。“信息不足”（NEI）标签通常通过不同的证据条件来操作化，而这种选择默默地决定了验证器学习的内容以及其分数可能隐藏的信息。我们引入了NEI-CAP，一种针对证据不足评估的构建感知诊断协议。每个NEI示例都带有产生它的构建族；NEI-CAP审计捷径线索，通过人工裁决验证困难案例，并测试能力是否跨构建迁移。我们在SciFact风格的科学验证中实例化该协议，并以FEVER和HoVer作为有界外部控制。在这些设置中，NEI能力无法可靠迁移：在易受捷径影响的构建上训练的模型无法识别语义相关的不充分证据，而混合构建训练缩小了差距但并未消除。固定主张的诊断进一步表明，证据条件会改变对参考支持/反驳标签的信心，而不仅仅是NEI召回率，因此聚合的NEI分数可能隐藏模型实际解决了哪个问题。

Original abstract: Evidence absence is not evidence insufficiency, but fact verification benchmarks can make them observationally similar. The Not Enough Information (NEI) label is often operationalized through different evidence conditions, and that choice silently determines what a verifier learns and what its score can hide. We introduce NEI-CAP, a construction-aware diagnostic protocol for insufficient-evidence evaluation. Each NEI example carries the construction family that produced it; NEI-CAP audits shortcut cues, validates hard cases through human adjudication, and tests whether competence transfers across constructions. We instantiate the protocol in SciFact-style scientific verification, with FEVER and HoVer as bounded external controls. Across these settings, NEI competence does not transfer reliably: models trained on shortcut-prone constructions fail to recognize semantically related insufficient evidence, and mixed-construction training narrows but does not close the gap. Fixed-claim diagnostics further show that the evidence condition shifts confidence in the reference Support/Refute label, not only NEI recall, so an aggregate NEI score can hide which problem a model has actually solved.

</details>


### [91] [SeDT: Sentence-Transformer Decision-Transformer Conditioning for Multi-Turn Conversation Reliability](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26788v1)
*Ramakrishna Vamsi Setti,Jagadeesh Rachapudi,Sachin Chaudhary,Praful Hambarde,Amit Shukla*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出SeDT方法改进多轮对话可靠性，使用离线RL的return-to-go conditioning，对agent对话推理有启发。

TL;DR: 大型语言模型在多轮对话中性能显著下降（“迷失在对话”），主要源于可靠性失败。提出SeDT方法，通过引入返回目标条件对对话历史进行相关性标注，无需训练即可恢复性能，在多个模型和任务上平均提升高达37.7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在多轮对话中性能显著下降（高达39%），而单轮推理性能良好，这种下降主要是可靠性问题而非能力问题。现有方法未能有效解决结构性的历史平等权重问题。

Method: 提出SeDT（Sentence-transformer Decision-Transformer），一种无需训练、推理时的方法，借鉴离线强化学习中的返回目标条件，用语义、词汇、位置三个互补信号计算累积相关性分数，标注每个对话片段，并在最后一轮呈现完整的标注历史。

Result: 在三个LLM和三个生成任务的Lost-in-Conversation基准上，SeDT在所有九种组合中均优于分片基线，平均性能提升高达37.7%，同时在九种组合中的七种中降低了不可靠性。

Conclusion: 通过告诉模型哪些过去的轮次重要（即相关性标注），可以大幅恢复多轮对话中丢失的性能，而无需修改模型权重或训练数据。

中文摘要：大型语言模型在单轮中完全指定任务时表现令人印象深刻，但相同的模型在相同的任务通过多轮逐步揭示时，性能会下降高达39%，这一现象被大规模记录为“迷失在对话中”。至关重要的是，这种崩溃几乎完全是可靠性失败；最佳情况下，能力仅下降16%，而不可靠性则增加一倍以上（+112%）。我们认为根本原因是结构性的：平坦的对话历史给每个先前的轮次分配了相等的隐式权重，使模型无法区分关键约束与无关对话。我们提出了SeDT（Sentence-transformer Decision-Transformer），一种无需训练、推理时的方法，通过从离线强化学习中引入“返回目标”条件来解决这一问题。SeDT用三个互补的信号（语义、词汇和位置）导出的累积相关性分数标注每个对话片段，并在最后一轮将完整的标注历史呈现给模型，无需改变权重、无需训练数据、无需丢弃上下文。在三个LLM和三个生成任务的Lost-in-Conversation基准测试中，SeDT在所有九种模型-任务组合中均优于分片基线，平均性能P提升高达37.7%，同时在九种组合中的七种中同时降低了不可靠性。简而言之，告诉模型哪些过去的轮次重要足以大幅恢复对话中丢失的性能。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) achieve impressive performance when a task is fully specified in a single turn, yet the same models lose up to 39% of that performance when the identical task is revealed incrementally across multiple turns, a phenomenon documented at scale as Lost in Conversation. Crucially, this collapse is almost entirely a reliability failure; the best case, the aptitude only falls 16%, while the unreliability more than doubles (+112%). We argue that the root cause is structural, a flat conversation history assigns equal implicit weight to every prior turn, giving the model no signal to distinguish a critical constraint from incidental dialog. We present SeDT Sentence-transformer Decision-Transformer, a training-free inference-time method that resolves this by importing return-to-go conditioning from offline reinforcement learning. SeDT annotates each conversation shard with a cumulative relevance score derived from three complementary semantic, lexical, and positional signals and presents the full annotated history to the model at the final turn, without weight changes, without training data, and without discarding context. Evaluated on the Lost-in-Conversation benchmark in three LLMs and three generation tasks, SeDT outperforms the sharded baseline in all nine model-task combinations, with gains up to +37.7% in mean performance P and simultaneous reductions in unreliability in seven of the nine combinations. In short, telling the model which past turns matter is sufficient to substantially recover the performance lost in conversation.

</details>


### [92] [ContextGuard: Structured Self-Auditing for Context Learning in Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26827v1)
*Hongbo Jin,Chi Wang,Haoran Tang,Zhongjing Du,Xu Jiang,Jingqi Tian,Qiaoman Zhang,Jiayu Ding*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出结构化自我审计方法改进上下文学习，可启发agent自我反思。

TL;DR: 大型语言模型在复杂上下文任务中会遵循核心推理但忽略外围或格式要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解LLMs在复杂上下文知识应用中的失败模式。

Method: 通过基准测试分析LLMs在上下文丰富任务中的表现。

Result: 发现模型能完成主要推理路径，但常忽略外围、持久或格式敏感的要求。

Conclusion: LLMs需改进对上下文知识完整性的应用。

中文摘要：最近的基准测试显示，尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）具有强大的推理能力，但它们仍然难以忠实地应用复杂的上下文知识。这些失败通常不是全面的推理崩溃：在上下文丰富的任务中，模型可能会遵循主要推理路径，而忽略了外围的、持久的或格式敏感的要求。

Original abstract: Recent benchmarks reveal that despite strong reasoning capabilities, large language models (LLMs) still struggle to faithfully apply complex contextual knowledge. ### [93] [GeoFaith: A Spatio-Temporal Dual View of Faithful Chain-of-Thought](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26893v1)

Experiments show the proposed method achieves superior performance on both faithfulness detection and downstream reasoning, producing shorter, more interpretable chains without sacrificing accuracy. Our code will be made available publicly.
