### [94] [Reasoning Depth and Environment Complexity: A Controlled Study of RLVR Data Allocation across Logical Reasoning Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26934v1)
*Yihua Zhu,Qianying Liu,Fei Cheng,Jiaxin Wang,Akiko Aizawa,Sadao Kurohashi,Hidetoshi Shimodaira*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: RLVR数据分配研究，对agent训练策略有启发

TL;DR: 提出二维推理空间（深度+复杂性）和四种推理形式，通过合成知识图谱环境发现联合覆盖、不均匀任务响应和均匀混合优于阶段性课程，并揭示现成模型的演绎-溯因不对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR研究对推理空间的理解过于狭隘，仅关注推理深度和演绎状态跟踪，忽略了环境复杂性和多种推理形式（溯因、归纳、类比），导致模型在现实推理任务中泛化不足。

Method: 构建一个受控的合成知识图谱环境，沿推理深度和环境复杂性两个维度变化，并设计四种推理任务（演绎、溯因、归纳、类比）进行实验，比较不同训练策略（单轴覆盖、联合覆盖、均匀混合、阶段性课程）的效果。

Result: 联合深度-复杂性覆盖优于单轴方案；推理家族反应不均匀，溯因在RL覆盖区域外退化，任务相关性聚类为演绎-溯因和归纳-类比对；均匀混合优于阶段性课程；现成模型也存在演绎-溯因不对称。

Conclusion: RLVR训练应考虑多维推理空间和多种推理形式，均匀混合策略更有效，且当前模型存在演绎偏斜，需进一步改进溯因等非演绎推理能力。

中文摘要：具有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为后训练推理模型的核心，但现有研究的一个关键局限性在于其对推理空间的狭隘视角：难度仅被视为推理深度，而奖励则集中在前向演绎状态跟踪上。我们则从两个维度刻画推理空间。难度：除了推理深度，我们还研究了环境复杂性，即模型必须在干扰项和交互结构中识别正确路径。奖励的推理形式：我们考虑了现实世界推理所必需的四种核心能力：演绎状态跟踪、隐藏事件或事实的溯因恢复、归纳规则归纳以及类比迁移。为了分离这些因素，我们构建了一个合成知识图谱环境，其中预训练和后训练分布受到控制，每个实例在深度、复杂性和任务族上有所变化。三个发现浮现出来：联合深度-复杂性覆盖优于单轴方案；推理家族反应不均匀，溯因推理在RL覆盖区域外退化，任务相关性聚集成演绎-溯因和归纳-类比对；在固定预算下，均匀混合优于阶段性课程。我们还发现，最近的现成模型表现出同样的演绎-溯因不对称性，表明这种差距并非我们受控设置的人为产物。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has become central to post-training reasoning models, yet a key limitation of existing studies is their narrow view of the reasoning space: difficulty is treated as reasoning depth alone, and reward is concentrated on forward deductive state tracking. We instead characterize the reasoning space along two dimensions. Difficulty. Beyond reasoning depth, we study environment complexity, where models must identify the correct path amid distractors and interacting structures. Rewarded reasoning form. We consider four abilities core to real-world reasoning: deductive state tracking, abductive recovery of hidden events or facts, inductive rule induction, and analogical transfer. To disentangle these factors, we construct a synthetic knowledge-graph environment with controlled pre- and post-training distributions, where each instance varies along depth, complexity, and task family. Three findings emerge: joint depth-complexity coverage outperforms single-axis recipes; reasoning families respond non-uniformly, with abductive reasoning degrading outside the RL-covered region and task correlations clustering into deductive-abductive and inductive-analogy pairs; and uniform mixing outperforms staged curricula under a fixed budget. We also find that recent off-the-shelf models exhibit the same deductive-over-abductive asymmetry, suggesting that this gap is not merely an artifact of our controlled setup.

Method: 引入开放式知识评估范式，构建BeQu基准（10,000实体及参考语料），通过开放式提示评估模型自然表达的知识。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）中的参数化知识是其成功的基石，但仍然知之甚少。现有的知识基准通常依赖于预定义的问题（例如，“M.L. King的出生日期是什么？”），仅评估基准设计者明确选择查询的知识，这是一种有问题的可得性偏差。在本文中，我们引入了开放式知识评估，这是一种新的LLM知识基准测试范式。它不是提出狭隘的问题，而是评估模型在回应开放式引导提示（例如，“告诉我所有关于M.L. King的知识”）时选择呈现的知识。这将焦点从预定义答案检索转向表征模型自然表达的知识。我们通过BeQu（Beyond Questions）实例化这一范式，这是一个包含10,000个实体的基准，每个实体配有用于陈述验证的参考语料库。使用BeQu，我们评估了广泛的语言模型，并分析了推理努力、模型规模、提示格式和知识领域的影响。数据和排行榜可在本工作的GitHub仓库和基准网站上获取。

Original abstract: Parametric knowledge in large language models (LLMs) is a cornerstone of their success, yet remains poorly understood. Existing knowledge benchmarks typically rely on predefined questions (e.g., "What is the birth date of M.L. King?"), evaluating only knowledge that benchmark designers explicitly choose to query, a problematic availability bias.
  In this paper, we introduce open knowledge evaluation, a new paradigm for LLM knowledge benchmarking. Instead of asking narrow questions, it evaluates models on the knowledge they choose to surface in response to open-ended elicitation prompts (e.g., "Tell me everything you know about M.L. King"). This shifts the focus from predefined answer retrieval toward characterizing the knowledge models naturally express.
  We instantiate this paradigm with BeQu (Beyond Questions), a benchmark of 10,000 entities paired with reference corpora for statement verification. Using BeQu, we evaluate a broad range of language models and analyze the effects of reasoning effort, model scale, prompt format, and knowledge domain. Data and leaderboard are available on this work's GitHub repository and at the benchmark's website.

### [96] [JuICE: A Benchmark for Evaluating LLM-Judge in Identifying Cultural Errors](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26955v1)
*Jiho Jin,Junho Myung,Juhyun Oh,Junyeong Park,Rifki Afina Putri,Sunipa Dev,Vinodkumar Prabhakaran,Alice Oh*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LLM作为评判者benchmark，对agent评估有参考价值

TL;DR: JuICE数据集显示LLM评判者检测文化错误能力有限（F1=0.52），尤其漏掉深层文化错误，需更深入的文化评估框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文化基准将文化视为扁平事实，且LLM-as-a-Judge未验证能否捕捉深层文化错误，因此需要新基准来评估。

Method: 构建JuICE数据集，包含4个国家1050个问答对、7470个文化/语言错误跨度标注，覆盖英语及当地语言，用于评估LLM评判者的错误检测能力。

Result: 最强LLM评判者F1仅0.52，且 consistently 漏掉当地居民识别的深层文化错误。

Conclusion: 文化评估需超越表面检测，采用考虑文化深度和情境性的框架。

中文摘要：随着大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被部署给世界各地的用户，它们被整合到不同文化背景下的日常任务中，从起草个人通信到头脑风暴创意想法。这些任务本质上是文化的：它们需要语境适当性、符号共鸣以及母语者本能依赖的隐性文化期望，这意味着一个回答可能在事实上合理，但对本地读者来说却明显错误。现有的文化基准通过事实验证或规范蕴涵方法将文化视为一组扁平的事实，并采用LLM作为评判者，而没有检查它们是否能捕捉这种深层的文化错误。为了填补这一空白，我们提出了JuICE（LLM评判者识别文化错误的基准），这是一个包含7470个跨度和级别的文化和语言错误标注的多语言数据集，涵盖来自四个国家（美国、韩国、印度尼西亚和孟加拉国）的1050个查询-响应对，包括英语和这些国家的主要语言。使用JuICE，我们发现即使是最强的LLM评判者在错误跨度检测任务中也仅达到0.52的F1分数。此外，LLM评判者 consistently 漏掉了当地居民容易识别的深层文化错误。我们的研究结果表明，稳健的文化评估必须超越表面检测，转向考虑文化意义的深度和情境性的框架。

Original abstract: As large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed to users around the world, they are integrated into everyday tasks across diverse cultural contexts, from drafting personal communications to brainstorming creative ideas. These tasks are inherently cultural: they require contextual appropriateness, symbolic resonance, and tacit cultural expectations that native speakers draw on instinctively, meaning that a response can be factually plausible yet unmistakably wrong to a local reader. Existing cultural benchmarks have treated culture as a flat set of facts via fact verification or norm entailment methods, and have adopted LLM-as-a-Judge without examining whether they can capture such thick cultural errors. To address this gap, we present JuICE (Benchmark for LLM-Judge in Identifying Cultural Errors), a multilingual dataset of 7,470 span-level annotations of cultural and linguistic errors in long-form LLM responses. It covers 1,050 query-response pairs from four countries (the United States, South Korea, Indonesia, and Bangladesh), in both English and their countries' main languages. Using JuICE, we find that even the strongest LLM-judge achieves only an F1 of 0.52 in the erroneous span detection task. Furthermore, LLM-judges consistently miss thick cultural errors that local residents readily identify. Our findings suggest that robust cultural evaluation must move beyond surface-level detection toward frameworks that account for the depth and situatedness of cultural meaning.

### [97] [Tournament-GRPO: Group-Wise Tournament Rewards for Reinforcement Learning in Open-Ended Long-Form Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26958v1)
*Zixuan Yang,Yiqun Chen,Wei Yang,Erhan Zhang,Zihan Shen,Xiaochi Wei,Yan Gao,Yi Wu,Yao Hu,Jiaxin Mao*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 锦标赛奖励强化学习，适用于agent训练中的奖励设计

TL;DR: 提出Tournament-GRPO，通过分组锦标赛比较将LLM评判转化为相对奖励，在开放式长文本生成中显著优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于评分标准的方法使用绝对分数，难以校准、区分度弱且易饱和，需要更有效的奖励信号。

Method: Tournament-GRPO：对同一查询的多个生成结果进行多轮分组锦标赛，累积比较结果并归一化为分组相对奖励，用于GRPO训练。

Result: 在Deep Research Bench上，Tournament-GRPO比最强基线提升4.52分，且锦标赛奖励在有效性和效率间取得良好平衡。

Conclusion: 基于评分标准的锦标赛比较为开放式长文本生成的强化学习提供了有效奖励信号。

中文摘要：在开放式长文本生成中，强化学习具有挑战性，因为可靠的参考答案和自动评估指标往往不可用。现有的基于评分标准的方法通常依赖于点式LLM作为评判者进行评分，但绝对分数难以在复杂回答间校准，可能对同一查询的生成结果提供弱区分性，并在优化过程中变得饱和。我们提出Tournament-GRPO，一种分组奖励框架，通过在同一查询的生成结果间进行多轮锦标赛比较，将基于评分标准的LLM判断转化为相对奖励。Tournament-GRPO在组内比较候选者，累积锦标赛结果，并将其归一化为用于GRPO训练的分组奖励。在Deep Research Bench上的实验表明，Tournament-GRPO一致优于现有的奖励设计基线，在最强基线上实现了4.52分的总体分数提升。进一步分析表明，锦标赛奖励提供了有利的有效性-效率权衡，且锦标赛设计影响训练动态。这些结果表明，基于评分标准的锦标赛比较为开放式长文本生成中的强化学习提供了有效的奖励信号。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning in open-ended long-form generation is challenging because reliable reference answers and automatic metrics are often unavailable. Existing rubric-based methods typically rely on pointwise LLM-as-a-judge scoring, but absolute scores are difficult to calibrate across complex responses, may provide weak discrimination among same-query rollouts, and can become saturated during optimization. We propose Tournament-GRPO, a group-wise reward framework that converts rubric-guided LLM judgments into relative rewards through repeated multi-round tournaments among same-query rollouts. Tournament-GRPO compares candidates within groups, accumulates tournament outcomes, and normalizes them into group-wise rewards for GRPO training. Experiments on Deep Research Bench show that Tournament-GRPO consistently outperforms existing reward-design baselines, achieving a 4.52-point overall-score improvement over the strongest baseline. Further analyses show that tournament rewards provide a favorable effectiveness--efficiency trade-off and that tournament design affects training dynamics. These results suggest that rubric-guided tournament comparison provides an effective reward signal for reinforcement learning in open-ended long-form generation.

</details>


### [98] [Recon: Reconstruction-Guided Reasoning Synthesis for User Modeling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26969v1)
*Alan Zhu,Mihran Miroyan,Carolyn Wang,Andrew Zhou,Lisa Dunlap,Narges Norouzi,Joseph E. Gonzalez*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 推理合成方法，可迁移至agent推理生成

TL;DR: 提出Recon方法，通过动作重构评分推理轨迹，避免事后合理化，在用户建模中显著优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法使用事后合理化生成的推理轨迹不能编码真实的因果决策路径，导致推理质量低下。

Method: Recon使用动作重构模型对候选推理评分：给定上下文和推理，重构模型预测动作，以重构保真度作为推理质量的指标。

Result: 在四个领域中，Recon相比Backward Synthesis胜率54.7%；用于训练推理合成模型后，下游用户建模胜率达70.0%。

Conclusion: 事后合理化不足以为推理合成提供足够质量，有效推理应能自然地从上下文引出动作，Recon通过动作重构实现了这一点。

中文摘要：用户建模旨在使用语言模型（LM）从过去上下文-动作对（例如对话轮次）的语料库中模仿个体的行为，从而在行为科学、人机协作和市场研究等环境中模拟用户。最近的方法通过合成推理轨迹来增强这些语料库，通常是通过在上下文和动作上进行条件生成。然而，这种条件构成了事后合理化而非推理：轨迹保证能证明动作的合理性，但可能不编码底层的潜在因果决策路径。我们提出Recon，它使用动作重构来根据预测能力对推理轨迹进行评分：给定上下文和候选推理，重构模型预测动作，重构保真度决定推理质量。在四个领域中，Recon相比标准的后验合理化基线Backward Synthesis实现了54.7%的胜率。此外，我们发现使用从Recon中导出的奖励训练推理合成模型可以提高下游用户建模性能，相比基线胜率高达70.0%。我们还展示了Recon合成的推理可以在模型间转移，并改善超越重构模型的用户建模。我们的工作表明，后验合理化对于推理合成是不够的，有用且可解释的推理应自然地从上下文引出动作。

Original abstract: User modeling aims to use language models (LMs) to mimic an individual's behavior from a corpus of past context-action pairs (e.g., conversation turns), enabling the simulation of users in settings like behavioral science, human-AI collaboration, and market research. Recent approaches augment these corpora with synthesized reasoning traces, typically generated by conditioning on both context and action. However, such conditioning constitutes post-hoc rationalization rather than reasoning: the trace is guaranteed to justify the action, but may not encode the underlying latent causal decision paths. We propose Recon, which uses action reconstruction to score reasoning traces by their predictive power: given a context and candidate reasoning, a reconstruction model predicts the action, and reconstruction fidelity determines reasoning quality. Across four domains, Recon achieves a 54.7% win rate over Backward Synthesis, a standard post-hoc rationalization baseline. Further, we find that training a reasoning synthesis model with rewards derived from Recon improves downstream user modeling performance, achieving a win rate of up to 70.0% over baselines. We further show that Recon-synthesized reasoning transfers across models, and improves user modeling beyond the reconstruction model. Our work demonstrates that post-hoc rationalization is insufficient for reasoning synthesis, and that useful and interpretable reasoning should naturally elicit the action from the context.

</details>


### [99] [Debate Helps Weak Judges Reward Stronger Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27483v1)
*Ethan Elasky,Frank Nakasako,Naman Goyal*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 探讨弱法官从强辩手辩论中受益，涉及多智能体协作与认证，可迁移至coding agent的验证与协作。

TL;DR: 在强辩论者/弱裁判的辩论中，只有当批评者能力超过裁判且裁判将批评视为待验证主张时，辩论才有效；单次独立批评可达到类似效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理论上辩论作为可扩展监督协议有潜力，但实证结果好坏参半，尤其是在裁判没有隐藏信息时效果不显著。本文旨在探究在可验证领域（代码和逻辑任务）中，辩论在更强辩论者/更弱裁判设置下的有效性条件。

Method: 在程序可验证的代码和逻辑任务上，使用更强辩论者/更弱裁判的提议者-批评者辩论设置，与咨询基线对比，并测试不同模型配对及去除反驳轮次的消融。

Result: 在五个配对中的三个（最有能力的配对）中，辩论显著优于咨询；在另外两个配对中无效，且裁判验证率下降。去除反驳轮次对性能无影响，单次独立批评恢复了大部分好处。

Conclusion: 提出一个更便宜的免训练可扩展监督原语（答案、批评、裁判），以及一个部署前审计（检查批评者是否击败裁判、裁判是否验证它），用于预测辩论何时有效。

中文摘要：尽管理论上承诺，辩论作为一种可扩展的监督协议已产生混合的实证结果：在某些设置中有所增益，在其他设置中则无效，尤其是当裁判没有隐藏信息时。我们研究在程序可验证的代码和逻辑任务上，在更强辩论者/更弱裁判的设置中的提议者-批评者辩论。当批评者提供可用的优势时，辩论帮助裁判超越咨询基线：批评者的分类能力必须超过裁判的，并且裁判必须将批评者的言论视为待验证的主张而非待总结的证词。在五个配对中的三个，条件成立时，提议者-批评者辩论的增益在统计上显著优于咨询，并且这些配对是最有能力的模型配对。在我们的集合中的两个非响应配对中，辩论产生无效效果，并且一旦批评者进入对话，裁判验证率下降几十个百分点。在这些情况下，批评者的二分类能力和裁判的彼此在噪声范围内，并且批评者的分歧被解析为证词而非待检查的主张。去除辩论中的反驳轮次对裁判性能没有可测量的变化：单个独立批评以较低的推理成本恢复了辩论的大部分好处。这些发现表明一种更便宜的用于可验证领域免训练可扩展监督的原语（答案，批评，裁判）和一个部署前审计（批评者是否击败裁判，裁判是否会验证它？），该审计预测辩论何时会有帮助。

Original abstract: Despite theoretical promise, debate as a scalable oversight protocol has produced mixed empirical results: gains in some settings, and null effects in others, especially when the judge does not have information hidden from it. We study proposer-critic debate in a stronger-debater/weaker-judge setting on programmatically verifiable code and logic tasks. Debate helps the judge over a consultancy baseline when the critic provides a usable advantage: the critic's classification ability must exceed the judge's, and the judge must treat critic speeches as claims to verify rather than testimony to summarize.
  On the three of five pairings where the condition holds, proposer-critic debate's gains are statistically significant over consultancy, and these pairings are the most capable model pairings. On the two non-responder pairings in our set, debate produces null effects, and judge verification rates drop by tens of percentage points once a critic enters the transcript. In these cases the critic's binary-classification ability and the judge's are within noise of each other, and the critic's disagreement is parsed as testimony rather than a claim to check.
  Ablating rebuttal rounds from debate produces no measurable change in judge performance: a single independent critique recovers the bulk of debate's benefit at lower inference cost. These findings suggest a cheaper primitive for training-free scalable oversight in verifiable domains (answer, critique, judge) and a pre-deployment audit (does the critic beat the judge, and will the judge verify it?) that predicts when debate will help.

</details>


### [100] [Cast a Wider Net: Coordinated Pass@K Policy Optimization for Code Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27000v3)
*Yilong Li,Suman Banerjee,Tong Che*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出协调式Pass@K策略优化用于代码推理，直接提升代码生成agent的效率，与自动代码优化高度相关。

TL;DR: 提出CPPO，通过联合规划策略优化代码生成的pass@K，在多个基准上取得显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准独立采样导致重复推理路径浪费预算，而竞争编程需要多样化策略，一次正确即可。

Method: 规划器输出K=4个备选方法元组，共享求解器为每个方法生成一个解，使用乘法规划奖励训练联合策略。

Result: 在APPS、CodeContests、LiveCodeBench-v6上，pass@4优于多种基线，最大提升+0.16（Qwen3.5-9B LiveCodeBench-v6）。

Conclusion: CPPO有效协调多策略探索，显著提升代码生成的pass@K性能。

中文摘要：使用验证器进行重复采样是为代码生成分配测试时计算的标准方式，并以pass@$K$作为规范指标。然而，标准策略类从单个答案分布中抽取$K$个独立样本，因此尝试常常坍缩到近乎重复的推理路径上，从而浪费预算于冗余多次运行。这种失败在竞争编程中代价高昂，因为许多问题允许多种不同的算法策略，而pass@$K$只需一次正确尝试。我们提出协调式pass@$K$策略优化（CPPO），它将对pass@$K$的生成转化为对策略的联合探索：一个规划器输出$K{=}4$个备选高层方法的元组，一个共享求解器为每个方法尝试一个解决方案。CPPO使用乘法规划奖励$R_{\mathrm{plan}} = J_\psi \cdot R_{\mathrm{out}}$训练该联合策略，仅将奖励分配给导致验证器确认的pass@$K$成功的有效策略元组。在APPS、CodeContests和LiveCodeBench-v6上，在相同的$K{=}4$求解器尝试预算下，CPPO相比直接采样、规划基线、仅规划器SFT和面向pass@$K$的强化学习改进了pass@$4$，在九个模型-基准单元格中的六个上取得了统计显著的增益。最大的单项增益是在Qwen3.5-9B LiveCodeBench-v6上相对于最强基线PKPO取得的$+0.16$（$0.588 \rightarrow 0.748$；配对bootstrap检验，$p < 0.05$）。

Original abstract: Repeated sampling with a verifier is the standard way to allocate test-time compute for code generation, with pass@$K$ as the canonical metric. Yet the standard policy class draws $K$ independent samples from a single answer distribution, so attempts often collapse onto near-duplicate reasoning paths and waste the budget on redundant rollouts. This failure is costly in competitive programming, where many problems admit multiple distinct algorithmic strategies and pass@$K$ requires only one correct attempt. We propose Coordinated Pass@$K$ Policy Optimization (CPPO), which turns pass@$K$ generation into joint exploration over strategies: a planner emits a tuple of $K{=}4$ alternative high-level methods, and a shared solver attempts one solution per method. CPPO trains this joint policy with a multiplicative planner reward, $R_{\mathrm{plan}} = J_ψ\cdot R_{\mathrm{out}}$, assigning credit only to valid strategy tuples that lead to verifier-confirmed pass@$K$ success. Across APPS, CodeContests, and LiveCodeBench-v6, CPPO improves pass@$4$ over direct sampling, planning baselines, planner-only SFT, and pass@$K$-oriented RL under the same $K{=}4$ solver-attempt budget, with statistically significant gains on six of nine model--benchmark cells. The largest single gain is $+0.16$ on Qwen3.5-9B LiveCodeBench-v6 over the strongest baseline, PKPO ($0.588 \rightarrow 0.748$; paired bootstrap, $p < 0.05$).

</details>


### [101] [Evaluating the Relevance of Uncertainty Estimators for LLM Hallucination](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27016v1)
*Yedidia Agnimo,Anna Korba,Annabelle Blangero,Nicolas Chesneau,Karteek Alahari*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 系统评估不确定性估计与幻觉的关系，为智能体可靠性提供参考。

TL;DR: 系统性实证研究表明，LLM中不确定性估计与幻觉之间的关联通常是弱的，且依赖于幻觉类型和模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不确定性估计常被用作模型失败的代理，但不确定性与幻觉间的关系未经充分验证，需要直接评估。

Method: 采用多种不确定性估计器（信息论、采样、反射性）在四个基准（RAGTruth, HalluLens等）上，对内在和外在幻觉进行实验。

Result: 关联高度可变且通常较弱，取决于幻觉类型和LLM。

Conclusion: 挑战了不确定性作为幻觉直接信号的观点，并明确了何时可提供可操作信息。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）容易出现幻觉，即与输入或训练数据不符的陈述，这阻碍了其可靠部署。与此同时，许多不确定性估计（UE）方法被提出来量化模型置信度，并且通常被隐式地视为模型失败的代理。然而，不确定性与幻觉之间的关系尚未得到充分描述。我们针对LLM中不确定性估计与幻觉之间的关联进行了系统的实证研究。我们不是假设这种关联，而是直接评估它在何时以及何种程度上成立。我们考虑了一组多样化的不确定性估计器，包括信息论、基于采样和反射性估计器，并检查了它们在各种幻觉设置中的行为。我们的实验涵盖了内在幻觉（对输入忠实性的违反）和外在幻觉（相对于训练数据的未经支持的声明），使用了四个互补基准，包括RAGTruth和HalluLens。我们发现这种关联高度可变且通常较弱，取决于幻觉类型和所评估的LLM。这些结果挑战了将不确定性作为幻觉直接信号的做法，并阐明了何时它提供可操作信息。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are prone to hallucinations, i.e., statements unsupported by the input or training data, hindering reliable deployment. In parallel, numerous uncertainty estimation (UE) methods have been proposed to quantify model confidence and are often implicitly treated as proxies for model failure. However, the relationship between uncertainty and hallucinations remains insufficiently characterized. We present a systematic empirical study of the association between uncertainty estimators and hallucinations in LLMs. Rather than assuming this association, we evaluate directly when and to what extent it holds. We consider a diverse set of uncertainty estimators, including information-theoretic, sampling-based, and reflexive estimators, and examine their behavior across hallucination settings. Our experiments cover both intrinsic hallucinations (violations of input faithfulness) and extrinsic hallucinations (unsupported claims relative to training data), using four complementary benchmarks, including RAGTruth and HalluLens. We find that the association is highly variable and often weak, depending on the hallucination type and the LLM under evaluation. These results challenge the use of uncertainty as a direct signal of hallucination and clarify when it provides actionable information.

### [102] [QUACK: Questioning, Understanding, and Auditing Communicated Knowledge in Multimodal Social Deduction Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27068v1)
*Ye Yuan,Rui Song,Weien Li,Zeyu Li,Haochen Liu,Xiangyu Kong,Changjiang Han,Yonghan Yang,Zichen Zhao,Zixuan Dong,Fuyuan Lyu,Bowei He,Haolun Wu,Jikun Kang,Xue Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多模态社交推理智能体评估框架，可迁移至coding agent的接地性评测。

TL;DR: QUACK是一个用于审计多模态社交推理中智能体语言接地性的开源框架，通过三级评估和语句验证管线，发现最强VLM仍有15.1%空间幻觉和过半无根据指控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有社交推理环境仅以游戏结果评分且多为文本交互，无法判断语言是否基于实际感知和行动，也难以识别失败模式。

Method: 提出QUACK框架，在游戏结果、行为轨迹和话语一致性三个层面评估智能体，核心语句验证管线通过重建真实轨迹并核对讨论声明来检测接地性问题。

Result: 评估三个前沿VLM，最强模型有15.1%空间声明出现幻觉，超过一半指控无实际证据。

Conclusion: QUACK框架有效揭示了当前VLM在多模态社交推理中的语言接地性缺陷，并提供了开源工具以支持进一步研究。

中文摘要：社交推理游戏已成为测试大型语言模型（LLM）智能体在推理、欺骗、协调和信念建模方面的热门平台。然而，大多数环境仅通过游戏结果（如胜率）进行评分，且主要局限于纯文本交互，这使得难以判断智能体的语言是否真正基于其感知和行动，也难以识别其行为背后的失败模式。为解决这一差距，我们引入了QUACK，一个用于审计多模态社交推理中智能体语言接地性的开源环境和评估框架。QUACK在三个层面评估智能体：游戏结果、行为轨迹和话语级别一致性。其核心的语句验证管线从引擎日志中重建每个智能体的真实轨迹，并检查每个讨论声明与之是否一致，自动标记空间幻觉、无根据指控、欺骗崩溃和语言-行动不一致。我们在同构和跨模型对抗设置中评估了三个前沿视觉语言模型（VLM），发现即使最强的智能体也有15.1%的可验证空间声明出现幻觉，并且超过一半的指控缺乏实际证据。我们在https://github.com/AAAAA-Academia-Attractions/QUACK 发布了完整的引擎、评估框架、工具包和日志。

Original abstract: Social deduction games have become a popular testbed for probing reasoning, deception, coordination, and belief modeling in Large Language Model (LLM) agents. However, most environments are scored only by game outcomes such as win rates and largely remain to text-only interaction, making it difficult to tell whether an agent's language is actually grounded in what it perceived and did, or to identify the failure modes underlying its behavior. To address this gap, we introduce QUACK, an open-source environment and evaluation framework for auditing the grounding of agent language in multimodal social reasoning. QUACK evaluates agents at three levels: game outcomes, behavioral trajectories, and utterance-level consistency. Its core Statement Verification Pipeline reconstructs each agent's ground-truth trajectory from engine logs and checks every discussion claim against it, automatically flagging spatial hallucination, unsupported accusation, deception collapse, and language-action inconsistency. Evaluating three frontier VLMs in both homogeneous and cross-model adversarial settings, we find that even the strongest agent hallucinates 15.1% of its verifiable spatial claims and makes over half of its accusations without grounded evidence. We release the full engine, evaluation framework, toolkit, and logs at https://github.com/AAAAA-Academia-Attractions/QUACK.

### [103] [GrowLoop: Self-Evolving Conversation Evaluation Seeded by Human](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28882v2)
*Yihang Lin,Yunze Gao,Zeyang Lin,Dongbo Li,Kun Peng,Yue Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出自我进化对话评估系统，包含Agent迭代和Rubric自演化，可迁移到agent评估与改进。

TL;DR: 提出了GrowLoop系统，通过自我演化的标准-案例共进化机制，持续适应模型进步和场景变化，在开放域对话的人类相似性评估中优于现有方法，并实现基准的自动演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法（专家基准、奖励模型、自进化基准）无法同时解决人类相似性评估中标准难以表述、判断存在分歧、定义动态变化的三大挑战。

Method: 构建GrowLoop系统：从少量人类种子注释出发，LLM代理通过启发式学习迭代提取评估标准；采用人类-AI一致性或合理性要求，并设计标准-案例共进化机制，使系统随评估目标变化而扩展覆盖范围。

Result: AI评估器在人类判断一致性上大幅优于现有方法，能发现注释者忽略的问题；生成的基准有效区分模型能力层级，并推广到新场景。

Conclusion: 将基准测试范式从手动更新或难度扩展转变为全面的、持续的自我进化，适应模型进展和场景变化。

中文摘要：随着大型语言模型的快速发展，评估开放域对话中的人类相似性变得越来越重要。然而，人类相似性是一种隐性知识，人类能够直觉地感知，但其背后的标准难以明确表述。人类判断差异很大，在某些情况下高度一致，而在其他情况下存在合理分歧。同时，人类判断背后的标准仍然是隐性的，没有明确的基础来构建案例。此外，人类相似性的定义并非一成不变，而是随着模型能力和人类期望的演变而变化。尽管在评估方法上取得了进展，如专家编写的基准、奖励模型和自我演变的基准，但没有一种方法能同时解决这三个挑战。因此，我们提出了GrowLoop，一个自我演变的对话评估系统，随着模型的进步和场景的变化不断适应。从最少的人类种子注释开始，LLM代理通过启发式学习迭代地提取和完善评估标准。在注释者意见一致的地方要求人类与AI达成一致，而在意见分歧的地方仅要求合理性。此外，标准-案例共同进化机制实现了持续进化。当评估目标发生变化时，新的人类种子会相应扩展系统的覆盖范围。当应用于开放域对话中的人类相似性评估时，由这些标准指导的AI评估器不仅在人类判断一致性上大幅优于现有方法，而且还揭示了注释者忽略的问题。生成的基准有效地区分了不同能力级别的模型，并揭示了它们的不足之处，同时还能推广到新场景并随着模型的进步而适应。我们的工作将基准测试范式从手动更新或难度扩展转变为全面的、持续的自我进化。

Original abstract: With the rapid advancement of large language models, evaluating human-likeness in open-ended conversation has become increasingly important. However, human-likeness is a form of tacit knowledge that humans perceive intuitively, yet the underlying criteria resist explicit formulation. Human judgments vary widely, with strong agreement on some cases and legitimate disagreement on others. Meanwhile, the criteria behind human judgments remain implicit, leaving no clear basis for constructing cases. Further, what counts as human-likeness is not static, but evolving with model capability and human expectations. Despite progress in evaluation methods such as expert-authored benchmarks, Reward Models, and self-evolving benchmarks, none addresses all three challenges simultaneously. Therefore, we propose GrowLoop, a self-evolving conversation evaluation system that continuously adapts as models advance and scenarios shift. Starting from minimal human seed annotations, LLM agents iteratively extract and refine evaluation rubrics through Heuristic Learning. Human-AI agreement is required where annotators converge, while only plausibility is expected where they diverge. Moreover, the Rubric-Case co-evolution mechanism enables continuous evolution. When the evaluation target shifts, new human seeds expand the system's coverage accordingly. When applied to human-likeness evaluation in open-ended conversation, the AI judge guided by these rubrics not only substantially outperforms existing methods in alignment with human judgments, but also uncovers issues that annotators overlook. The resulting benchmark effectively discriminates models across capability tiers and reveals where they fall short, while generalizing to new scenarios and adapting as models advance. Our work shifts the benchmarking paradigm from manual updates or difficulty scaling to comprehensive, continuous self-evolution.

</details>


### [104] [UserHarness: Harnessing User Minds for Stronger Agent Theory-of-Mind](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27721v1)
*Cheng Qian,Jiayu Liu,Heng Ji*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 重构用户心智状态的框架，提升agent的心智理论能力，对agent交互设计有启发。

TL;DR: 提出UserHarness框架，通过显式重建用户心理状态实现ToM推理，在五个基准上取得显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ToM方法采用复杂管道间接建模行为，未能显式重建用户心理状态，忽略了用户信念、意图与行动的核心关系。

Method: UserHarness框架将ToM推理重构为显式用户心理重建，分解用户心理状态（观察、信念、意图、行动）及其与外部环境的关系，使智能体能够跟踪用户所想所为。

Result: 在五个基准测试中达到95.94%宏平均准确率，相对现有推理方法提升超过15%，相对最强纯提示harness提升约20%。

Conclusion: 鲁棒的用户理解需要从用户思想根源推理，用户驾驭是构建更自适应未来助手的可行基础。

中文摘要：理解用户的信念和意图对于构建有效的智能助手至关重要。这种能力通常通过心理理论（Theory-of-Mind, ToM）任务来评估，在这些任务中，成功需要从用户的角度进行推理。然而，许多现有方法采用复杂的 pipeline 来间接建模行为，而没有显式重建用户的心理状态。这忽略了问题的核心结构：用户根据其信念行动，信念通过观察环境得到更新；信念和意图共同决定行动，行动反过来改变环境；社会推理往往需要关于他人相信或意图的嵌套信念。我们提出了 UserHarness，一个简单的框架，将 ToM 推理重新定义为显式的用户心理重建。UserHarness 分解了用户的心理状态、其与外部环境的关系以及随之而来的行动，使智能体能够追踪用户观察、相信、意图和做的事情。在五个基准测试中，UserHarness 达到了高达 95.94% 的宏平均准确率，相对现有推理方法提高了超过 15%，相对最强的纯提示 harness 提高了约 20%。这些结果表明，鲁棒的用户理解需要从用户思想的根源进行推理，将用户驾驭视为未来更自适应助手的可行基础。

Original abstract: Understanding what a user believes and intends is central to building effective agent assistants. This ability is often evaluated through Theory-of-Mind (ToM) tasks, where success requires reasoning from the user's perspective. However, many existing approaches address ToM with complex pipelines that model behavior indirectly, without explicitly reconstructing the user's mental state. This misses the core structure of the problem: users act based on their beliefs, which are updated through observations of the environment; beliefs and intentions jointly determine actions, which in turn change the environment; and social reasoning often requires nested beliefs about what others believe or intend. We propose UserHarness, a simple framework that reframes ToM reasoning as explicit user-mind reconstruction. UserHarness decomposes the user's mental state, its relation to the external environment, and the actions that follow from it, enabling agents to track what the user observes, believes, intends, and does. Across five benchmarks, UserHarness reaches up to 95.94% macro accuracy, improving over existing inference methods by more than 15% relative and over the strongest prompt-only harness by about 20% relative. These results suggest that robust user understanding requires reasoning from the roots of the user's mind, positioning user harnessing as a promising foundation for more adaptive future assistants.

</details>


### [105] [Do Models Know Why They Changed Their Mind? Interpretability and Faithfulness of Chain-of-Thought Under Knowledge Conflict](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27773v1)
*Pruthvinath Jeripity Venkata*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究CoT推理忠实性，分析知识冲突下模型决策，为agent推理可信性提供启示。

TL;DR: 研究语言模型思维链推理的忠实度，发现决策信息主要由置信度承载而非论证内容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作表明模型面对矛盾文档时选择取决于事实熟知度，但未知思维链是否忠实反映这一机制。

Method: 引入内省忠实度，在200题、8模型、4提示条件下测试，分析思维链相似性、置信度预测能力等。

Result: 思维链在相反决策下高度相似（96%），置信度携微弱信号，GPT-4o耦合可靠，Claude Sonnet 4.6置信度反转，内部思考令牌更敏感。

Conclusion: 思维链分解为决策不变的展示知识和置信度层，监控应关注置信度而非论证。

中文摘要：当语言模型看到与其训练知识相矛盾的文档时，它必须做出选择：遵循文档还是相信自身。先前的工作证明这一选择取决于事实的熟知程度。我们提出疑问：模型的思维链推理是否忠实地反映了这一机制？我们引入了内省忠实度，并在200个问题、8个模型和4种提示条件下进行了测试。我们发现思维链推理在相反决策下高度稳定：翻转对保留了96%的相同答案相似度（d=0.34；通过ROUGE-L确认，d=0.45）。然而自我评定的置信度携带微弱的真实信号：对于实体知名度无信息性的模糊事实，置信度仍然能预测决策（p<0.001）并追踪项目层面的知识（r=0.134）。GPT-4o是唯一具有统计上可靠的推理-决策耦合的模型。Claude Sonnet 4.6显示出最宽的置信度范围（SD=1.39）但近乎为零的汇总相关性，因为置信度-决策关系在不同条件下反转；温度消融实验确认了这是模型特定的。内部思考令牌显示出比面向用户的思维链更高的决策敏感性（p=0.033）。思维链可分解为决策不变的展示知识（约96%）和一层薄弱的置信度信号（弱但真实）。监控建议：阅读置信度，而非论证。

Original abstract: When a language model sees a document contradicting its training knowledge, it must choose: follow the document or trust itself. Prior work proved this choice depends on how well-known the fact is. We ask: does the model's chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning faithfully report this mechanism? We introduce introspective faithfulness and test it across 200 questions, 8 models, and 4 prompt conditions. We find CoT reasoning is highly stable across opposite decisions: flip pairs retain 96% of same-answer similarity (d=0.34; confirmed by ROUGE-L, d=0.45). Yet self-rated confidence carries a faint genuine signal: for obscure facts where entity fame is uninformative, confidence still predicts decisions (p<0.001) and tracks item-level knowledge (r=0.134). GPT-4o is the only model with statistically reliable reasoning-decision coupling. Claude Sonnet 4.6 shows the widest confidence range (SD=1.39) but near-zero pooled correlation because the confidence-decision relationship reverses between conditions; a temperature ablation confirms this is model-specific. Internal thinking tokens show greater decision-sensitivity than user-facing CoT (p=0.033). CoT decomposes into a decision-invariant knowledge display (~96%) and a thin confidence layer with weak but real signal. For monitoring: read confidence, not the argument.

</details>

### [106] [AgensFlow: A Coordination-Policy Substrate for Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27466v1)
*Nicole Koenigstein*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多agent协调策略框架，将协调视为在线策略学习，通用方法可迁移

TL;DR: AgensFlow将多智能体协调视为在线策略学习问题，通过学习路由改善协调密集型工作流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以预先固定多智能体协调选择，静态管道和一次性比较提供有限视角。

Method: 提出AgensFlow框架，将多智能体协调视为部分可观测性下的在线策略学习问题，使协调决策可观测且可学习。

Result: 在分布式系统事件和安全咨询任务上，学习路由比固定管道基线更高质量，skip:X识别拓扑压缩为有意义部分，热启动策略图减少探索成本。

Conclusion: 学习到的、可审计的路由可以改善协调密集型多智能体工作流，优于静态布线。

中文摘要：基于大型语言模型（LLM）构建的多智能体系统需要许多难以预先固定的协调选择：调用哪个技能协议，哪个智能体角色应执行子任务，将哪个模型绑定到每个角色，角色之间如何交互，何时使用检索或验证，以及何时完全省略某个步骤。这些选择与任务机制和操作约束相互作用，因此静态管道和一次性模型比较仅提供了设计空间的一个有限视角。本文介绍了AgensFlow，这是一个开源框架，它将多智能体协调视为部分可观测性下的在线策略学习问题。该框架使协调决策变得可观测且可从重复轨迹中学习，而不是将技能、角色、模型、拓扑和评估选择视为固定的管道设计。
  AgensFlow在两个语料库上进行了评估：分布式系统事件任务和安全咨询任务。评估显示了三个主要结果：在协调密集型类别上，学习到的路由比固定管道基线达到了更高质量的操作点；skip:X将拓扑压缩识别为基底的一个有意义的组成部分；而热启动策略图可以减少探索成本，同时保持平台质量。总体而言，结果支持：学习到的、可审计的路由可以改善协调密集型多智能体工作流，优于静态布线。

Original abstract: Multi-agent systems built on large language models (LLMs) require many coordination choices that are difficult to fix a priori: which skill protocol to invoke, which agent role should perform a subtask, which model to bind to each role, how roles should interact, when to use retrieval or verification, and when to omit a step entirely. These choices interact with task regime and operational constraints, so static pipelines and one-off model comparisons provide only a limited view of the design space. This paper introduces AgensFlow, an open-source framework that treats multi-agent coordination as an online policy-learning problem under partial observability. The framework makes coordination decisions observable and learnable from repeated trajectories, rather than treating skill, role, model, topology, and evaluation choices as fixed pipeline design.
  AgensFlow is evaluated on two corpora: distributed-systems incident tasks and security-advisory tasks. The evaluation shows three main results: learned routing reaches a higher-quality operating point than a fixed pipeline baseline on coordination-heavy classes; skip:X isolates topology compression as a meaningful part of the substrate; and warm-started policy graphs can reduce exploration cost while preserving plateau quality. Overall, the results support that learned, auditable routing can improve coordination-heavy multi-agent workflows over static wiring.

</details>


### [107] [Persistent AI Agents in Academic Research: A Single-Investigator Implementation Case Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26870v1)
*Anas H. Alzahrani*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 持久化agent在学术研究中的实践，涉及内存、工具、调度等架构经验。

TL;DR: 通过案例研究发现，持久代理环境以缓存读取为主，经济单位从每令牌成本转向每完成制品成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在持久代理环境中的行为缺乏研究，传统评估方法（模型、基准、短对话）不足以覆盖长期交互场景。

Method: 采用结构化自我观察案例研究，于2026年1月31日至5月25日进行，分析持久人-代理环境，并使用PARE-M框架组织结果，涵盖架构、利用率、制品生产、资源使用、可重复性和治理。

Result: 遥测数据包括96天共75,671条记录，其中用户消息8,059条，助手消息23,710条；工作空间含502个记忆文件、17个代理目录、57个技能文件；系统活跃时间579.7小时；记忆记录482个输出代理事件和889个失败/验证/纠正/协议事件；5月子集含627个模型完成事件，共计7395万令牌，82.9%为缓存读取。

Conclusion: 工作流以缓存主导，持久代理环境可能促使经济单位从每令牌成本转向每完成制品成本；未来评估应使用制品级分母、可重复解析规则、纠正分类和独立治理事件编码。

中文摘要：背景：大型语言模型通常被作为模型、基准或简短对话片段进行评估。对于当代理持久嵌入真实学术研究环境中，具有持久记忆、本地文件、外部工具、计划任务、委派角色和明确安全协议时会发生什么，我们知之甚少。方法：从2026年1月31日至5月25日进行了一项结构化的自我观察实施案例研究。分析单位是持久的人-代理环境：研究人员、代理运行时、记忆层、工具、存储库、计划任务、专门代理角色和治理规则。结果使用PARE-M（持久代理研究环境测量）组织，这是一个涵盖架构、利用率、制品生产、资源使用、可重复性和治理的测量框架。结果：可恢复的主代理遥测包含96个活跃日中的75,671条去重记录，其中8,059条用户角色消息和23,710条助手角色消息。工作空间包括502个与记忆相关的文件、17个配置的代理目录和57个技能文件。活跃系统时间为579.7小时（30分钟上限缺口估计）。记忆衍生记录识别出482个输出代理事件和889个失败、验证、纠正或协议代理事件。一个严格的2026年5月轨迹子集捕获了627个模型完成事件和7395万个记录令牌，其中82.9%是缓存读取。结论：工作流程以缓存为主，表明持久代理环境可能将经济单位从每令牌成本转移到每完成制品成本。未来的评估应使用制品级分母、可重复的解析规则、纠正分类法和独立编码的治理事件。

Original abstract: Background: Large language models are typically evaluated as models, benchmarks, or short conversational episodes. Less is known about what happens when an agent is embedded persistently in a real academic research environment with durable memory, local files, external tools, scheduled routines, delegated roles, and explicit safety protocols. Methods: A structured self-observed implementation case study was conducted from January 31 to May 25, 2026. The unit of analysis was the persistent human-agent environment: researcher, agent runtime, memory layer, tools, repositories, scheduled jobs, specialized agent roles, and governance rules. Outcomes were organized using PARE-M (Persistent Agentic Research Environment Measurement), a measurement framework covering architecture, utilization, artifact production, resource use, reproducibility, and governance. Results: Recoverable main-agent telemetry contained 75,671 de-duplicated records across 96 active days, with 8,059 user-role and 23,710 assistant-role messages. The workspace included 502 memory-related files, 17 configured agent directories, and 57 skill files. Active system time was 579.7 hours (30-minute capped-gap estimate). Memory-derived records identified 482 output-proxy events and 889 failure, verification, correction, or protocol-proxy events. A strict May 2026 trajectory subset captured 627 model-completed events and 73.95 million recorded tokens, of which 82.9% were cache reads. Conclusions: The workflow was cache-dominant, suggesting that persistent agentic environments may shift the economic unit from cost per token to cost per completed artifact. Future evaluations should use artifact-level denominators, reproducible parsing rules, correction taxonomies, and independent coding of governance events.

</details>


### [108] [Detection Without Correction: A Two-Parameter Decomposition of Multi-Stage LLM Pipelines](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27559v1)
*Prashanti Nilayam,Kiran Ramanna,Prashil Tumbade*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多阶段LLM pipeline的检测-纠正分解，揭示多agent行为机制。

TL;DR: 多阶段LLM流水线中，准确率反转等异常行为源于检测与修正的耦合决策，其中高误修正率是核心故障，该框架统一了多种现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多阶段LLM流水线（如多智能体辩论、自我修正）表现出准确率平台期、反转等异常聚合行为，且当代模型上辩论增益不复现、自我修正退化、跨供应商动态差异大，这些现象缺乏统一解释。

Method: 将下游响应分解为检测（是否采纳上游内容）和条件生成（否则生成什么）两个耦合决策，得到四个响应机制。在四个模型系列、四个基准、两种方法上进行九格实证分析，计算检测率和条件误修正率。

Result: 条件误修正率在各队列中占主导（53-94%），检测率变化超过一个数量级。四种异常现象可归因于共同机制，检测阈值是稳定的模型/协议层规律。

Conclusion: 多阶段LLM流水线的异常行为源于高误修正率这一主要故障模式，检测阈值是稳定的规律，该框架统一了多种现象并解释了观察到的行为。

中文摘要：多阶段LLM流水线，如多智能体辩论、内在自我修正或检索增强验证，展现出令人费解的聚合行为：准确率随轮次出现平台期和反转、辩论增益在当代前沿模型上无法复现、内在自我修正退化，以及辩论动态中跨供应商的定性差异。下游智能体响应可操作化为两个耦合的决策：检测（是否将上游内容视为权威）和条件生成（如果不视为权威则生成什么）。这种分解产生了四个可观察的响应机制，其中无修正的检测是主要故障模式。在跨越四个模型系列、四个基准测试（GSM8K、MATH-500、GPQA-Diamond、AIME）和两种方法（多智能体辩论、内在自我修正）的九格实证网格中，我们发现条件误修正率持续占主导（各队列为53-94%），而检测率随上下文变化超过一个数量级。该框架将上述四种现象统一为共同机制的特征，并将检测阈值描述为稳定的模型/协议层规律，在匹配基准难度的方法间持续存在。

Original abstract: Multi-stage LLM pipelines that perform multi-agent debate, intrinsic self-correction, or retrieval-augmented verification exhibit puzzling aggregate behaviors: accuracy plateaus and reversals across rounds, non-replication of debate gains on contemporary frontier models, intrinsic self-correction degradation, and qualitative cross-provider divergence in debate dynamics. Downstream agent response can be operationalized as two coupled decisions: detection (whether to treat upstream content as authoritative) and conditional generation (what to produce if not). This decomposition yields four observable response regimes, of which detection-without-correction is the load-bearing failure mode. Across a nine-cell empirical grid spanning four model families, four benchmarks (GSM8K, MATH-500, GPQA-Diamond, AIME), and two methods (multi-agent debate, intrinsic self-correction), we find that the conditional miscorrection rate is consistently dominant (53-94% across cohorts) while detection rate varies contextually by more than an order of magnitude. The framework unifies the four phenomena above as signatures of a common mechanism and characterizes detection threshold as a stable model/protocol-level regularity that persists across methods at matched benchmark difficulty.

</details>

# cs.RO [[Back]](#toc)

### [109] [PEACE: A Planner-Executor Agent with Constraint Enforcement for UAVs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00104v1)
*Erdem Uysal,Timo Kehrer,Sebastiano Panichella*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 规划执行agent架构，包含LLM规划、工具调用、约束执行，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出一种用于PX4无人机的规划-执行代理，解耦高层规划与低层控制，使用LLM进行单次任务规划，结合2D检测器和深度投影构建世界模型，通过约束执行层保证安全，在仿真中验证了可解释性提升和LLM调用减少。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法要么紧密耦合导致延迟和幻觉风险，要么生成不透明的端到端策略难以解释和约束。

Method: 提出规划-执行代理架构：LLM单次规划生成任务，通过ROS 2工具调用接口桥接MAVLink执行；世界模型融合2D检测器（如YOLO）和针孔深度投影实现3D定位；包含约束执行层（高度限制、地理围栏）和有界重规划机制。

Result: 在PX4软件在环仿真中展示可行性，相比紧耦合LLM控制，改进了可解释性、约束强制执行并减少了LLM调用次数。

Conclusion: 该方法在可解释性、约束执行和效率上具有优势，代码已开源。

中文摘要：基础模型越来越多地被用于驱动自主系统，然而现有方法要么将模型紧密集成在控制回路中，增加了延迟和幻觉风险，要么将自然语言编译成不透明的端到端策略，这些策略难以解释、约束，并且需要特定领域的数据集和微调。我们提出了一种针对基于PX4的无人机的规划-执行代理，它将高层任务规划与低层控制解耦。大型语言模型执行单次任务规划，而执行则通过桥接到MAVLink的结构化ROS 2工具调用接口处理。系统通过将模块化2D检测器（例如YOLO或视觉语言模型）与用于3D物体定位的针孔深度投影模块相结合来构建世界模型。一个约束执行层强制执行高度限制和水平地理围栏，有界重规划使得从执行时的动作失败中恢复成为可能。我们将我们的方法定位于基于基础模型的机器人系统的三种常见设计模式中，并在Gazebo中的PX4软件在环仿真中展示了其可行性。结果凸显了与紧密耦合的LLM控制相比，可解释性、约束强制执行以及减少LLM调用次数的改进。代码、数据集、视频和其他资料可在以下链接找到：https://github.com/erdemuysalx/PEACE

Original abstract: Foundation models are increasingly used to drive autonomous systems, yet existing approaches either keep the model in a tight control loop, raising latency and hallucination risk, or compile natural language into opaque end-to-end policies that are hard to explain, constraint and require domain-specific datasets and fine-tuning. We propose a planner-executor agent for PX4-based drones that decouples high-level mission planning from low-level control. A large language model performs single-pass task planning, while execution is handled through a structured ROS 2 tool-calling interface bridged to MAVLink. The system constructs a world model by combining modular 2D detectors (e.g., YOLO or vision-language models) with a pinhole depth projection module for 3D object localization. A constraint enforcement layer enforces altitude limits and horizontal geofencing, and bounded replanning enables recovery from execution-time action failures. We position our approach within three common design patterns for foundation-model-based robotics systems and demonstrate its feasibility in PX4 software-in-the-loop simulations in Gazebo. Results highlight improved explainability, constraint enforcement, and reduced LLM calls compared to tightly coupled LLM control. The code, dataset, videos, and other material can be found at the following link: https://github.com/erdemuysalx/PEACE

</details>

# math.OC [[Back]](#toc)

### [110] [OptiLoop: Coordination-in-the-Loop Verification and Repair for LLM-Generated Optimization Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27630v1)
*Yujia Xu,Zhiheng Wang,Thi Dinh*

Main category: math.OC

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出协调在环验证与修复方法OptiLoop，通过短时协调运行检测并修复LLM生成优化代理的语义错误，显著提升目标与社会匹配率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成的优化代理在去中心化协调中可能语义错误，这些错误在孤立执行中无法发现，需在协调过程中验证。

Method: 采用ADMM风格共识协议，通过短时协调运行验证代理，收集行为和静态证据进行修复，支持从局部代码修复升级到公式修复，并复用历史经验。

Result: 在40个测试场景中，目标匹配率从66.0%提升至93.0%，社会匹配率从68.5%提升至89.0%，目标差距从15.3%降至3.5%，社会差距从7.6%降至2.0%。

Conclusion: 对于去中心化决策循环中的生成优化代理，正确性应在协调循环内验证，而非仅依赖孤立执行。

中文摘要：许多去中心化决策问题需要多方在保持目标、约束和数据私有的同时协调共享决策。大型语言模型（LLM）提供了一种有前景的方式，通过从自然语言规范生成本地优化代理来降低参与门槛。然而，在协调场景中，可执行性还不够：生成的代理可能编译、求解并通过本地检查，但在语义上仍然错误，例如错误表示成本、错误界定约束或对激励做出不正确响应。此类错误通常仅在协调过程中显现，表现为系统性行为失败而非不可行性。我们提出了协调在环的验证与修复方法，用于LLM生成的优化代理。我们通过交替方向乘子法（ADMM）风格的共识协议实例化这一思想，并引入OptiLoop，这是一个从文本生成本地优化代理、通过针对固定参考对手的短时边界协调运行进行验证、提取结构化行为和静态证据、并应用证据驱动的修复的流水线。当失败是结构性的而非实现性的时，OptiLoop从局部代码修复升级为修正公式的修复，并且还可以从先前实例中重复使用情景经验。在40个保留测试场景中，相对于强局部验证基线，OptiLoop-Full将目标匹配率从66.0%提高到93.0%，社会匹配率从68.5%提高到89.0%，同时将平均目标差距从15.3%降低到3.5%，平均社会差距从7.6%降低到2.0%。这些结果表明，对于部署在去中心化决策循环内的生成优化代理，正确性应在循环本身内验证，而不是仅通过孤立执行来验证。

Original abstract: Many decentralized decision problems require multiple parties to coordinate on shared decisions while keeping objectives, constraints, and data private. Large language models (LLMs) offer a promising way to lower the barrier to participation by generating local optimization agents from natural-language specifications. In coordination settings, however, executability is not enough: a generated agent may compile, solve, and pass local checks while still being semantically wrong, for example by misrepresenting costs, mis-scoping constraints, or responding incorrectly to incentives. Such errors often surface only during coordination, as systematic behavioral failures rather than infeasibility. We propose coordination-in-the-loop verification and repair for LLM-generated optimization agents. We instantiate this idea with an Alternating Direction Method of Multipliers (ADMM)-style consensus protocol and introduce OptiLoop, a pipeline that generates local optimization agents from text, verifies them through short, bounded coordination runs against a fixed reference counterparty, extracts structured behavioral and static evidence, and applies evidence-driven repair. When failures are structural rather than implementational, OptiLoop escalates from localized code fixes to corrected-formulation repair, and it can additionally reuse episodic lessons from prior instances. On 40 held-out test scenarios, OptiLoop-Full improves objective match from 66.0% to 93.0% and social match from 68.5% to 89.0% relative to a strong local-validation baseline, while reducing mean objective gap from 15.3% to 3.5% and mean social gap from 7.6% to 2.0%. These results show that, for generated optimization agents deployed inside decentralized decision loops, correctness should be validated in the loop itself rather than through isolated execution alone.

</details>

### [111] [ICICLE: Expanding Retrieval with In-Context Documents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26902v2)
*Yu-Chen Den,Yung-Yu Shih,Zhi Rui Tam,Kuan-Yu Chen,Pu-Jen Cheng,Yun-Nung Chen,Eugene Yang*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 增量检索框架，对agent检索增强有启发

TL;DR: ICICLE通过上下文内索引和源感知docid生成解决增量式生成检索的语料扩展问题，无需重新训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式检索中语料扩展成本高，重复训练和灾难性遗忘现有文档。

Method: 提出ICICLE框架，结合基于[COPY]的路由机制、偏好校准和大上下文适应，实现源感知的docid生成。

Result: 在MS MARCO和NQ320K上，ICICLE提升了新文档检索，保持了已见文档的保留，且无需重新训练。

Conclusion: 高样本退化主要由路由失败引起，源选择校准是扩展上下文内生成式检索的关键瓶颈。

中文摘要：生成式检索（GR）直接使用参数知识将查询映射到文档标识符（docid）。然而，这种设计使得语料库扩展成本高昂：添加新文档需要更新模型参数以编码新的文档-docid关联，这会导致重复训练以及对先前索引文档的灾难性遗忘。在这项工作中，我们将增量式GR重新视为一个上下文内检索问题，其中新添加的文档作为推理时的文档-docid证据提供。我们提出了ICICLE，一个上下文内索引框架，它在参数记忆和上下文提供的文档-docid对上执行源感知的docid生成。ICICLE结合了基于`[COPY]`的路由机制、偏好校准和大上下文适应，以区分基于上下文的检索和参数检索。在MS MARCO和NQ320K上的实验表明，ICICLE提高了新引入文档的检索性能，同时保持了对已见文档的保留，无需特定于语料库的重新训练。我们的进一步分析表明，高样本退化主要是由路由失败引起的，突出了源选择校准作为扩展上下文内生成式检索的关键瓶颈。

Original abstract: Generative retrieval (GR) maps queries directly to document identifiers (docids) using parametric knowledge, However, this design makes corpus expansion costly: adding new documents requires updating model parameters to encode new document-docid associations incurs repeated training and catastrophic forgetting of previously indexed documents. In this work, we revisit incremental GR as an in-context retrieval problem, where newly added documents are supplied as inference-time document-docid evidence. We propose ICICLE, an in-context indexing framework that performs source-aware docid generation over both parametric memory and context-provided document-docid pairs. ICICLE combines a `[COPY]`-based routing mechanism, preference-based calibration, and large context adaptation to distinguish context-grounded retrieval from parametric retrieval. Experiments on MS MARCO and NQ320K show that ICICLE improves retrieval of newly introduced documents while preserving seen-document retention without corpus-specific retraining. Our analysis further shows that high-shot degradation is mainly caused by routing failure, highlighting source-selection calibration as a key bottleneck for scaling in-context generative retrieval.

</details>


### [112] [Libra: Training the Environment for Agentic Information Retrieval](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00016v1)
*Xuan Zhao,Andy Chiu,Gengyu Wang*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 通过优化环境目录提升agent信息检索性能，在SWE-bench上验证，直接支持coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出Libra框架，通过引入可变的目录和LLM驱动的优化循环，持续改进仓库中的代码定位准确性，并实现跨LLM和问题集的零样本迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法优化LLM本身，但忽略了优化智能体工作环境（仓库）的可能性。

Method: 引入可变的目录（层次化Markdown文件），通过LLM驱动的循环（Prompter生成查询，Solver导航目录，Healer根据失败重写目录）来自我进化。

Result: 在12个SWE-bench Lite仓库上，代码定位准确性持续对数级提升，改进可零样本迁移到其他LLM和问题集，且配备Libra优化目录的极简编码智能体优于基线。

Conclusion: 环境优化可以作为数据驱动方式提升LLM系统性能，且具有通用性和迁移性。

中文摘要：大型仓库内的信息定位是智能LLM系统的基石。虽然合成数据驱动优化在训练LLM方面已被证明是成功的，但很少关注以数据驱动方式优化智能体的工作环境（即仓库本身）。为弥补这一差距，我们提出了Libra，这是一个自我进化的框架，它将可变的“目录”（作为可导航索引的层次化Markdown文件）引入仓库。Libra运行一个LLM驱动的优化循环，其中Prompter生成合成查询，冻结的Solver通过导航目录尝试解决这些查询，而Healer则根据Solver的定位失败重写目录。在12个SWE-bench Lite仓库上的评估表明，这种环境修复带来了代码定位准确性的持续对数级改进。此外，这些环境改进可以零样本迁移到不同的LLM和问题集。尽管本文的重点是研究此类系统的通用行为，但我们也证明了一个配备Libra优化目录的极简编码智能体优于最先进的基线。代码可在https://github.com/salesforce-misc/Libra获取，数据可在https://huggingface.co/datasets/Salesforce/Libra获取。

Original abstract: Information localization within massive repositories is a cornerstone of agentic LLM systems. While synthetic data-driven optimization has proven successful in training LLMs, little attention has been paid to optimizing the agent's working environment (the repository itself) in a data-driven manner. To bridge this gap, we present Libra, a self-evolving framework that introduces mutable "catalogs" (hierarchical Markdown files serving as navigable indices) into the repository. Libra runs an LLM-driven optimization loop where a Prompter generates synthetic queries, a frozen Solver attempts to resolve them by navigating the catalogs, and a Healer rewrites the catalogs in response to the Solver's localization failures. Evaluations across 12 SWE-bench Lite repositories demonstrate that this environmental healing yields continual, logarithmic improvements in code localization accuracy. Furthermore, these environmental improvements transfer zero-shot across different LLMs and problem sets. Although the focus of this paper is to study the general behavior of such a system, we also demonstrate that a minimalist coding agent equipped with Libra-optimized catalogs outperforms state-of-the-art baselines. Code is available at https://github.com/salesforce-misc/Libra and data at https://huggingface.co/datasets/Salesforce/Libra.

</details>

### [113] [CiteCheck: Retrieval-Grounded Detection of LLM Citation Hallucinations in Scientific Text](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27700v1)
*Khashayar Khajavi,Shaghayegh Sadeghi,Rise Adhikari,Alexander Tessier*

Main category: cs.DL

Selection reason: 检索增强的引用幻觉检测框架，验证机制可迁移至coding agent的检索与验证。

TL;DR: 提出CiteCheck框架，结合学术检索和结构化LLM验证，有效检测引用幻觉，在物理基准上超越现有模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成的科学报告中常出现虚假或元数据错误的引用，需要可靠的自动验证方法。

Method: 混合框架：从外部来源检索候选出版物，使用结构化LLM验证器比较引用与候选，将分数映射为Exact、Minor、Major三个标签。

Result: 在982引用的物理基准上，宏F1达88.7，准确率88.9%，优于GPT、Claude、Gemini等基线。

Conclusion: 可靠的引用验证需要结合学术检索、结构化LLM比较和校准的决策规则。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被用于生成科学报告，但它们可能产生看似合理但包含损坏元数据或指向不存在的论文的参考文献。我们引入CiteCheck，一个用于检测引用幻觉的混合框架，它验证引用是否对应于真实的学术工作以及其元数据是否与该工作一致。CiteCheck从外部学术来源检索候选出版物，使用结构化的LLM验证器将引用与检索到的候选进行比较，并将验证器分数映射为三个标签：精确、次要和主要。我们还构建了一个包含982个引用的物理学基准，带有受控损坏，涵盖微妙的元数据漂移和完全捏造的参考文献。在保留测试集上，CiteCheck达到了88.7的宏F1和88.9%的准确率，优于包括网络搜索和少量样本变体在内的GPT、Claude和Gemini基线。这些结果表明，可靠的引用验证得益于结合学术检索、基于LLM的结构化比较和校准的决策规则。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to generate scientific reports, but they can produce references that appear plausible while containing corrupted metadata or pointing to papers that do not exist. We introduce CiteCheck, a hybrid framework for citation hallucination detection that verifies whether a citation corresponds to a real scholarly work and whether its metadata is faithful to that work. CiteCheck retrieves candidate publications from external scholarly sources, compares the citation against the retrieved candidate using a structured LLM verifier, and maps verifier scores into three labels: Exact, Minor, and Major. We also construct a 982-citation physics benchmark with controlled corruptions that capture both subtle metadata drift and fully fabricated references. On the held-out test set, CiteCheck achieves 88.7 macro-F1 and 88.9% accuracy, outperforming GPT, Claude, and Gemini baselines, including web-search and few-shot variants. These results show that reliable citation verification benefits from combining scholarly retrieval, structured LLM-based comparison, and calibrated decision rules.

### [114] [When Does Deep RL Beat Calibrated Baselines? A Benchmark Study on Adaptive Resource Control](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26418v3)
*Guilin Zhang,Chuanyi Sun,Kai Zhao,Xu Chu,Shahryar Sarkani,John Fossaceca*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: DRL在资源控制中的基准研究，提出RL agent评估协议，可迁移。

TL;DR: 校准的规则基自动缩放器在所有工作负载上成本优于六种主流DRL算法，DRL仅在突发和闪流流量上略有优势；离散动作算法优于连续动作算法；瓶颈在于基线校准、奖励工程和评估协议而非算法选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究深度强化学习在自适应资源控制中相较于精心校准的规则基方法的实际价值，以及何时DRL能提供帮助。

Method: 构建RLScale-Bench基准测试，在Kubernetes水平Pod自动缩放场景下，对比六种DRL算法（PPO, DQN, A2C, SAC, TD3, DDPG）与校准的规则基基线，跨六种工作负载和五种随机种子进行240次实验。

Result: 校准规则基控制器在所有六种工作负载上成本最低，但DRL在突发和闪流流量上稍优；离散动作算法约束违反比连续动作算法低一到两个数量级；没有单一算法在所有场景下表现最佳。

Conclusion: 基于RL的资源控制瓶颈在于基线校准、奖励工程和现实评估协议，而非算法选择。

中文摘要：一个经过恰当校准的基于规则的自动缩放器在我们测试的每一个工作负载上，成本都可以击败六种主流深度强化学习（DRL）算法——那么，如果存在的话，DRL究竟何时有用？我们在RLScale-Bench中研究了这个问题，这是一个用于自适应资源控制的DRL可重复基准测试和评估协议，其中代理在成本和服务水平约束下为动态工作负载分配计算资源。我们在匹配的架构、训练预算和奖励函数下，针对六种工作负载模式和五种随机种子（共240次运行），评估了PPO、DQN、A2C、SAC、TD3和DDPG，并与一个经过校准的基于规则的基线进行了比较，在Kubernetes的水平Pod自动缩放上实例化该基准测试，并探测了分布偏移下的泛化能力。三个发现挑战了常见假设：（i）校准控制器在所有六个工作负载上实现了最低成本，但在突发流量和闪流流量上落后于最佳RL代理；（ii）由于动作空间不匹配，离散动作算法在约束违反上比连续动作算法表现好一到两个数量级；（iii）没有单一算法在所有工作负载上占优，排名可能变动多达四个位置。基于RL的资源控制的瓶颈不在于算法选择，而在于基线校准、奖励工程和现实的评估协议。

Original abstract: A properly calibrated rule-based autoscaler can beat every one of six mainstream deep reinforcement learning (DRL) algorithms on cost across every workload we test - so when, if ever, does DRL actually help? We study this in RLScale-Bench, a reproducible benchmark and evaluation protocol for DRL on adaptive resource control, where an agent allocates compute to a dynamic workload under cost and service-level constraints. We evaluate PPO, DQN, A2C, SAC, TD3, and DDPG under matched architectures, training budgets, and reward functions against a calibrated rule-based baseline across six workload patterns and five seeds (240 runs), instantiate the benchmark on Kubernetes Horizontal Pod Autoscaling, and probe distribution-shift generalization. Three findings challenge common assumptions: (i) the calibrated controller achieves the lowest cost on all six workloads, though it trails the best RL agents on bursty and flash traffic; (ii) discrete-action algorithms outperform continuous-action ones by one to two orders of magnitude in constraint violations due to action-space mismatch; and (iii) no single algorithm dominates across workloads, with rankings shifting by up to four positions. The bottleneck in RL-based resource control is not algorithm selection but baseline calibration, reward engineering, and realistic evaluation protocols.

</details>


### [115] [Beyond Trajectory-Level Attribution: Graph-Based Credit Assignment for Agentic Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26684v2)
*Xin Cheng,Shuo He,Lang Feng,HaiYang Xu,Ming Yan,Lei Feng,Bo An*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 图基信用分配用于agentic RL，提出GraphGPO，对agent训练有贡献

TL;DR: 提出GraphGPO，通过构建状态转移图实现步骤级信用分配，提升RL训练效率和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于群体的RL方法中，信用分配仅依赖轨迹级结果，无法有效利用失败轨迹中的有价值步骤。

Method: 将rollout轨迹聚合为状态转移图，利用全局信息估计状态到目标的距离，并基于距离减少量计算边级别的优势函数进行信用分配。

Result: 在多个挑战性基准上达到最先进性能，显著提升训练效率。

Conclusion: GraphGPO通过细粒度信用分配有效提升了LLM在多步任务中的RL训练效率和性能。

中文摘要：基于群体的强化学习（RL）方法在提升大型语言模型（LLM）性能方面取得了显著成功，并已迅速扩展到智能体任务。然而，其信用分配严重依赖于根据最终结果进行的粗粒度轨迹级归因，难以捕捉单个步骤的贡献，例如在失败轨迹中被掩盖的有价值步骤。为了揭示潜在信息并实现更忠实的步骤级信用分配，我们提出了基于图的群体策略优化（GraphGPO），该方法首先将所有 rollout 轨迹聚合为一个统一的状态转移图，然后利用图中编码的全局信息估计每个状态到任务目标的距离。最后，GraphGPO 通过估计基于图的优势函数来为每条边分配信用，该优势基于转移减少到任务目标距离的程度。通过这种方式，GraphGPO 显著提高了训练效率，并在多个具有挑战性的基准测试中实现了最先进的性能。

Original abstract: Group-based reinforcement learning (RL) methods have achieved remarkable success in improving the performance of large language models (LLMs) and have been rapidly extended to agentic tasks. However, their credit assignment relies heavily on coarse-grained trajectory-level attribution according to final outcomes, making it difficult to capture the contribution of individual steps, such as valuable steps obscured within failed trajectories. To uncover latent information and enable more faithful step-level credit assignment, we propose Graph-based Group Policy Optimization (GraphGPO), which first aggregates all rollout trajectories into a unified state-transition graph and then estimates the distance from each state to the task goal using the global information encoded in the graph. Finally, GraphGPO assigns credit to each edge by estimating a graph-based advantage, based on how much the transition reduces the distance to the task goal. In this way, GraphGPO significantly improves training efficiency and achieves state-of-the-art performance across a range of challenging benchmarks.

</details>


### [116] [Self-Improvement Imitation with Biologically Guided Search for Protein Design Under Oracle Budgets](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26690v1)
*Ashima Khanna,Dominik Grimm*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 蛋白质设计轨迹自改进模仿学习，方法可迁移至coding agent的搜索与优化

TL;DR: 本文提出SILO框架，通过分层编辑策略和主动学习在有限的oracle预算下优化蛋白质序列，在多个景观上达到最佳表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在代理噪声下退化，且位置无关的突变提议可能破坏关键残基，需要更高效利用oracle预算的方法。

Method: 采用分层编辑策略（先选位置再选残基），通过增量随机波束搜索（SBS）采样轨迹，结合UCB代理集成和丙氨酸扫描适应度分数（AFS）选择候选，并用oracle标记轨迹进行下一个动作交叉熵模仿学习。

Result: 在8个蛋白质适应度景观上，SILO在最大和top-100平均适应度上均优于五个基线，且在低数据和噪声测试中保持竞争力。

Conclusion: SILO通过轨迹级自我改进模仿和分层编辑，有效利用oracle预算，在蛋白质设计中表现优异，其中SBS和AFS贡献显著。

中文摘要：在严格的oracle预算下进行蛋白质序列优化需要探索巨大的组合空间并使每次评估都具有信息性的方法。现有的强化学习和离策略生成方法常常在代理噪声下退化，而与位置无关的突变提议可能破坏功能关键的残基。我们提出了SILO，一种用于oracle预算蛋白质设计的轨迹级自我改进模仿框架。SILO使用分层编辑策略，将每次突变分解为位置选择后跟残基选择。在每个主动学习轮次中，策略通过增量随机波束搜索而不替换（SBS）采样候选轨迹，并且一个基于UCB的代理集成结合丙氨酸扫描适应度分数（AFS）选择具有功能性相关编辑的候选进行in silico oracle评估。然后通过该轮最佳oracle标记轨迹上的下一个动作交叉熵模仿来更新策略，避免价值函数估计。在八个复现的蛋白质适应度景观和五个先前工作的强基线上，SILO在评估的8/8个景观中实现了最高最大和top-100平均适应度，通常表现出更快的早期改进。在两个景观的低数据和噪声代理压力测试中，当几个基线退化时，SILO保持竞争力或最佳。消融实验表明，SBS与AFS占据了大部分增益，而迭代模仿提供了额外的改进。代码可在https://github.com/grimmlab/SILO.git获取。

Original abstract: Protein sequence optimization under tight oracle budgets requires methods that explore vast combinatorial spaces while making each evaluation informative. Existing reinforcement learning and off-policy generative approaches often degrade under surrogate noise, and position-agnostic mutation proposals risk disrupting functionally critical residues. We introduce SILO, a trajectory-level self-improvement imitation framework for oracle-budgeted protein design. SILO uses a hierarchical edit policy that decomposes each mutation into a position choice followed by a residue choice. In each active-learning round, the policy samples candidate trajectories via incremental stochastic beam search without replacement (SBS), and a UCB-based proxy ensemble, combined with an alanine-scan fitness score (AFS), selects candidates with functionally relevant edits for in silico oracle evaluation. The policy is then updated by next-action cross-entropy imitation on the round's best oracle-labeled trajectories, avoiding value-function estimation. Across eight reproduced protein fitness landscapes and five strong baselines from prior work, SILO achieves the highest maximum and top-100 mean fitness on 8 of 8 landscapes within our evaluations, often exhibiting faster early-stage improvement. In low-data and noisy-proxy stress tests on two landscapes per setting, SILO remains competitive or best when several baselines degrade. Ablations show that SBS with AFS account for much of the gains, with iterative imitation providing additional improvement. Code is available at: https://github.com/grimmlab/SILO.git

</details>


### [117] [Detect by Yourself: Self-Designing Agentic Workflows for Few-Shot Graph Anomaly Detection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27470v1)
*Tairan Huang,Qiang Chen,Yili Wang,Yueyue Ma,Changlong He,Xiu Su,Yi Chen*

Selection reason: 自设计agentic workflow用于图异常检测，通用agent工作流设计可迁移。

TL;DR: SignGAD通过将图异常检测任务转化为设计任务条件检测工作流的新范式，并引入保护性最终拟合策略，在少样本场景下显著提升了检测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图异常检测方法面临两大挑战：固定流程限制了跨任务适应性，以及缺乏将上下文与结构异常信号显式融入检测过程的证据。

Method: 提出SignGAD框架，包括两个核心：1）任务条件检测工作流设计范式，根据任务选择合适图编码和检测器；2）保护性最终拟合策略，通过校准拟合接受度优化工作流。

Result: 在多个真实数据集上，SignGAD优于现有最先进方法，展示了强性能。

中文摘要：图异常检测旨在识别属性图中的异常节点，并在实际应用中发挥重要作用。然而，现有的图异常检测方法仍面临两个关键挑战：1）固定流程，限制了其在有限监督下跨不同图任务的适应性；2）证据薄弱，使其无法将上下文和结构异常信号明确纳入检测过程。在本文中，我们提出了一种新颖的框架，即用于少样本图异常检测的自设计智能体工作流（SignGAD）。具体来说，我们提出了一种新的范式，将图异常检测任务从训练固定异常检测器转变为设计任务条件的检测工作流。通过构建检测工作流，SignGAD选择合适的图编码和检测器设计以利用任务特定的异常证据。同时，我们引入了一种保护性的最终拟合策略，通过校准拟合接受度来优化所选工作流，增强有限监督下的可靠性。在多个真实世界数据集上进行的广泛实验表明，SignGAD相比现有最先进方法取得了强劲的性能，突显了其在图异常检测任务上的有效性。

Original abstract: Graph anomaly detection aims to identify anomaly nodes in attributed graphs and plays an important role in real-world applications. However, existing graph anomaly detection methods still face two key challenges: 1) fixed pipelines, which restrict their adaptability across different graph tasks under limited supervision; 2) weak evidence, which prevents them from explicitly incorporating contextual and structural anomaly signals into the detection process. In this paper, we propose a novel framework, self-designing agentic workflows for few-shot graph anomaly detection (SignGAD). Specifically, we propose a novel paradigm that reformulates graph anomaly detection task from training a fixed anomaly detector to designing task-conditioned detection workflows. By constructing detection workflows, SignGAD selects suitable graph encodings and detector designs to exploit task-specific anomaly evidence. Meanwhile, we introduce a guarded final refit strategy to refine the selected workflow by calibrating refit acceptance, enhancing reliability under limited supervision. Extensive experiments conducted on several real-world datasets demonstrate that SignGAD achieves strong performance against state-of-the-art methods, highlighting its effectiveness on graph anomaly detection tasks.

### [118] [The Kalman Evolve: Closing the Gap in Kalman Filtering via Interpretable Algorithm Discovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26830v1)
*Vasileios Saketos,Ming Xiao*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 利用LLM发现算法改进Kalman滤波，思路可迁移至代码优化。

TL;DR: 提出Kalman Evolve框架，通过联合优化噪声参数和更新结构（利用LLM生成非仿射修改），改进了卡尔曼滤波器在非线性传感模型下的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准卡尔曼滤波器在非线性传感场景中性能下降，仅调参无法消除性能差距。

Method: Kalman Evolve框架，联合优化噪声参数和更新结构，利用大型语言模型作为结构化先验生成可解释的非仿射修改，同时保留递归形式。

Result: 在多个合成和真实世界跟踪基准测试中，RMSE降低高达12%，优于优化卡尔曼滤波器等强基线。

Conclusion: 优化卡尔曼滤波器的结构（而非仅参数）是一种实用且可解释的改进状态估计方法。

中文摘要：状态估计是控制和信号处理中的一个基本问题，卡尔曼滤波器在线性动态、高斯噪声和已知噪声协方差的假设下提供了最优解。然而，这些假设在诸如多普勒雷达和LiDAR等现实传感场景中常常不成立。在这些情况下，最优估计器本质上是非线性的，导致系统性性能下降。这产生了一个仅通过调整噪声协方差参数（即卡尔曼滤波器中的过程和测量噪声）无法消除的性能差距。为了解决这一局限，我们提出了Kalman Evolve，一种通过联合优化噪声参数和更新结构来发现改进滤波算法的框架。我们的方法利用大型语言模型（LLMs）作为程序空间上的结构化先验，能够生成对经典卡尔曼滤波器的可解释的非仿射修改，同时保留其递归形式。我们提供了分析结果，证明了在常见非线性传感模型下仿射估计器的次优性，从而激励了对结构感知更新的需求。在一系列合成和真实世界的跟踪基准测试中，包括多普勒雷达、基于LiDAR的定位和行人跟踪，所发现的算法持续优于强基线（如优化卡尔曼滤波器），RMSE降低高达12%。这些结果表明，优化卡尔曼滤波器的结构（而不仅仅是其参数）提供了一种实用且可解释的方式来改进状态估计。

Original abstract: State estimation is a fundamental problem in control and signal processing, for which the Kalman Filter provides an optimal solution under linear dynamics, Gaussian noise, and known noise covariances. However, these assumptions often fail in realistic sensing settings such as Doppler radar and LiDAR. In these cases, the optimal estimator is inherently nonlinear, which leads to systematic performance degradation. This creates a performance gap that cannot be eliminated by tuning the noise covariance parameters (i.e., the process and measurement noise in the Kalman Filter) alone. To address this limitation, we propose Kalman Evolve, a framework for discovering improved filtering algorithms by jointly optimizing both noise parameters and the update structure. Our approach leverages large language models (LLMs) as a structured prior over program space, enabling the generation of interpretable, non-affine modifications to the classical Kalman filter while preserving its recursive form. We provide analytical results establishing the suboptimality of affine estimators under common nonlinear sensing models, motivating the need for structure-aware updates. Across a range of synthetic and real-world tracking benchmarks, including Doppler radar, LiDAR-based localization, and pedestrian tracking, the discovered algorithms consistently improve over strong baselines such as the Optimized Kalman Filter, achieving up to 12\% reduction in RMSE. These results suggest that optimizing the structure of the Kalman filter, rather than only its parameters, provides a practical and interpretable way to improve state estimation.

### [119] [DEI: Diversity in Evolutionary Inference for Quality-Diversity Search](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27130v1)
*John Donaghy,Shikhar Rastogi*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 利用LLM作为变异算子的分布式质量多样性搜索，多agent协作方法。

TL;DR: 提出DEI框架，利用异构LLM作为分布式QD搜索的变异算子，实验证明模型多样性比并行性更关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有同质并行搜索复制单一模型偏差，缺乏多样性，需要利用不同LLM的创造性互补以提升搜索性能。

Method: 提出DEI框架，将异构LLM分配给不同节点作为变异算子，通过非阻塞通信共享局部最优解，形成跨模型对抗压力。

Result: 在Core War领域，四节点异构集成相比单节点基线QD分数提高124%，覆盖率提高28%，并优于同质集成。

Conclusion: 模型多样性是分布式LLM-based QD搜索收益的关键驱动因素，而非仅仅是并行性。

中文摘要：我们提出了DEI：进化推理中的多样性（Diversity in Evolutionary Inference），一个分布式质量-多样性（QD）搜索框架，它将异构的大型语言模型（LLM）分配为变异算子，通过非阻塞集合操作在peer节点之间通信。与同质并行搜索（在所有工作节点上复制单一模型的归纳偏差）不同，DEI将每个LLM独特的创造性先验视为行为新颖性的互补来源。通过DEI扩展数字红皇后框架，节点在每轮结束时共享局部最优解，以播种下一轮的种群。这创造了跨模型对抗压力，推动了超越模型内自我对弈的鲁棒性。在Core War领域（一个竞争性编程基准，Redcode战士程序在模拟机器内对战）上评估，一个四节点异构集成（GPT-5.4-mini、Claude Sonnet 4.6、GPT-5.2和Claude Haiku 4.5）在相等的总LLM调用预算下，与单节点基线相比，实现了合并存档QD分数提高124%（45.90对比20.46），覆盖率提高28%（80.6%对比63.0%的单元）。异构集成还在QD分数、覆盖率和所有四个模型家族的留出解通用性方面优于同等预算的同质集成。这些结果提供了第一个经验证据，表明模型多样性（而非仅仅是并行性）是分布式基于LLM的QD搜索中收益的关键驱动因素。

Original abstract: We present DEI: Diversity in Evolutionary Inference, a distributed Quality-Diversity (QD) search framework that assigns heterogeneous large language models (LLMs) as mutation operators across peer nodes communicating with non-blocking collective operations. Unlike homogeneous parallel search, which replicates a single model's inductive biases across all workers, DEI treats each LLM's distinct creative prior as a complementary source of behavioral novelty. Extending the Digital Red Queen framework with DEI, nodes share local optimal solutions at the end of each round to seed the next round's population. This creates cross-model adversarial pressure that drives robustness beyond intra-model self-play. Evaluated on the Core War domain, a competitive programming benchmark in which Redcode warrior programs battle inside a simulated machine, a four-node heterogeneous ensemble (GPT-5.4-mini, Claude Sonnet 4.6, GPT-5.2, and Claude Haiku 4.5) achieves 124 percent higher merged-archive QD-Score (45.90 vs. 20.46) and 28 percent higher coverage (80.6 percent vs. 63.0 percent of cells) than a single-node baseline at equal total LLM-call budget. The heterogeneous ensemble also outperforms an equally-budgeted homogeneous ensemble on QD-Score, coverage, and held-out solution generality across all four model families. These results provide the first empirical evidence that model diversity, not merely parallelism, is the key driver of gain in distributed LLM-based QD search.

### [120] [Transferable Reinforcement Learning via Probabilistic Latent Embeddings and Dynamic Policy Adaptation for Sim-to-Real Deployment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27659v1)
*Gengyue Han,Yiheng Feng*

Main category: cs.LG

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用元强化学习中的潜在上下文变量推断环境潜在表示，并结合分布RL框架根据潜在变量估计精度动态调整策略风险水平。

中文摘要：由于资源限制和公共安全问题，许多网络物理系统（例如自动驾驶汽车）的深度强化学习（RL）智能体首先在模拟器中进行训练。然而，当部署到现实环境中时，由于不可避免的Sim2Real差距，它们常常面临性能下降或安全违规。现有的零样本方法，如鲁棒安全RL和域随机化，缓解了这个问题，但通常以性能下降或在遇到未建模的系统动力学时残留安全风险为代价。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了一种新颖的强化学习框架，通过概率潜在嵌入和动态策略自适应实现安全高效的策略迁移。我们考虑了一系列在不同环境上下文下的约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDP）。通过利用元强化学习中的潜在上下文变量，该框架从模拟经验中推断环境的潜在表示。此外，它结合了分布RL公式，允许根据潜在上下文变量的估计精度动态调整部署策略的风险水平。这种策略在部署早期促进安全性，并通过在Sim2Real差距下的快速策略自适应提高效率。

Original abstract: Due to limited resources and public safety concerns, deep reinforcement learning (RL) agents for many cyber-physical systems (e.g., autonomous vehicles) are first trained in simulators. However, when deployed in real world environments, they often suffer from performance degradation or safety violations because of the inevitable Sim2Real gap. Existing zero-shot approaches, such as robust safe RL and domain randomization, mitigate this issue but typically at the cost of degraded performance or residual safety risks when experiencing unmodeled system dynamics. To address these limitations, we propose a novel reinforcement learning framework that enables safe and efficient policy transfer via probabilistic latent embeddings and dynamic policy adaptation. We consider a family of Constrained Markov Decision Processes (CMDPs) under different environment contexts. By leveraging latent context variable in meta-RL, the proposed framework infers the latent representation of the environment from simulated experiences. Furthermore, it incorporates a distributional RL formulation, which allows risk levels of the deployed policy to be adjusted dynamically, based on the estimation accuracy of the latent context variable. This strategy promotes safety at the early deployment stage and improves efficiency through fast policy adaptation under the Sim2Real gap.

### [121] [Restoring the Sweet Spot: Pass-Rate Weighted Self-Distillation for LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27765v1)
*Zehao Liu,Yuanpu Cao,Jinghui Chen,Vasant G. Honavar*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出自蒸馏策略优化中的难度感知加权，提升LLM推理能力，可迁移至agent推理增强。

TL;DR: 提出SC-SDPO，通过对每个问题的SDPO损失进行自适应加权引入难度意识，在多项基准上显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SDPO基于KL的优势缺乏难度意识，而GRPO通过归一化自然聚焦中等难度问题，导致SDPO性能受限。

Method: 通过分析GRPO优势归一化对可学习性的影响，发现归一化后梯度缩放因子为sqrt(p(1-p))，据此对SDPO损失加权，得到SC-SDPO；权重由批量自适应归一化在线计算，零成本。

Result: 在Qwen3-8B上mean@16提升3.2，maj@16提升4.3；在OLMo-3-7B上分别提升1.8和3.0，且训练稳定。

Conclusion: SC-SDPO通过隐式课程学习实现难度感知，有效改进SDPO，且计算开销低、训练动态稳定。

中文摘要：自蒸馏策略优化（SDPO）通过利用模型自身的反馈条件预测作为自我教师，为大型语言模型的强化学习提供了密集的token级信用分配。然而，与GRPO不同，GRPO的组相对优势自然地将学习集中在中等难度问题的甜蜜点上，而SDPO基于KL的优势缺乏隐含的难度意识。我们通过GRPO的优势归一化视角分析这一差距。将可学习性框架扩展到归一化奖励，我们表明归一化吸收了方差项p(1-p)，平衡了不同问题的前导阶可学习性，留下sqrt(p(1-p))作为每个问题梯度的唯一残差缩放因子。这一分析得出一个简单的处方：用[hat(p)(1-hat(p))]^{1/2}加权每个问题的SDPO损失，得到SC-SDPO，即SDPO的尺度一致变体。所提出的权重是通过在线策略rollout与批量自适应归一化作为零成本副产品获得的，引入了一个隐式课程，动态跟踪模型不断发展的能力。在科学推理和工具使用基准上的实验表明，SC-SDPO持续优于SDPO，在Qwen3-8B上取得了+3.2/+4.3（mean@16/maj@16）的提升，在OLMo-3-7B上取得了+1.8/+3.0的提升，同时在整个优化过程中保持稳定的训练动态。

Original abstract: Self-Distillation Policy Optimization (SDPO) provides dense token-level credit assignment for reinforcement learning with large language models by leveraging the model's own feedback-conditioned predictions as a self-teacher. Unlike GRPO, however, whose group-relative advantage naturally concentrates learning on a sweet spot of intermediate-difficulty questions, SDPO's KL-based advantage lacks an implicit notion of difficulty awareness.
  We analyze this gap through the lens of GRPO's advantage normalization. Extending the learnability framework to normalized rewards, we show that normalization absorbs the variance term $p(1-p)$, equalizing leading-order learnability across questions and leaving $\sqrt{p(1-p)}$ as the sole residual scaling factor in the per-question gradient. This analysis yields a simple prescription: weight each question's SDPO loss by $[\hat{p}(1-\hat{p})]^{1/2}$, resulting in SC-SDPO, a scale-consistent variant of SDPO.
  The proposed weights are obtained as a zero-cost byproduct of on-policy rollouts with batch-adaptive normalization, inducing an implicit curriculum that dynamically tracks the model's evolving competence. Experiments on scientific reasoning and tool-use benchmarks demonstrate that SC-SDPO consistently improves over SDPO, yielding gains of +3.2/+4.3 (mean@16/maj@16) on Qwen3-8B and +1.8/+3.0 on OLMo-3-7B, while preserving stable training dynamics throughout optimization.

</details>
